001068r 3               
001068r 3               xt_dot_s:
001068r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_depth    ; ( -- u )
00106Br 3               
00106Br 3                               ; Print stack depth in brackets
00106Br 3  A9 3C                        lda #$3c        ; ASCII for "<"
00106Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001070r 3               
001070r 3                               ; We keep a copy of the number of the things on the stack
001070r 3                               ; to use as a counter later down. This assumes that there
001070r 3                               ; are less than 255 elements on the stack
001070r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001072r 3  48                           pha
001073r 3               
001073r 3                               ; print unsigned number without the trailing space
001073r 3  CA                           dex             ; DUP
001074r 3  CA                           dex
001075r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001077r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001079r 3               
001079r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr print_u
00107Cr 3               
00107Cr 3  A9 3E                        lda #$3e        ; ASCII for ">"
00107Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001081r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP      ; ASCII for SPACE
001083r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001086r 3               
001086r 3  E8                           inx
001087r 3  E8                           inx
001088r 3               
001088r 3                               ; There will be lots of cases where the stack is empty. If that
001088r 3                               ; is so, get out of here quickly
001088r 3  E0 rr                        cpx #dsp0
00108Ar 3  F0 1E                        beq @done
00108Cr 3               
00108Cr 3               @have_stack:
00108Cr 3                               ; We have at least one element on the stack. The depth of the
00108Cr 3                               ; stack is on the stack, we can use it as a counter. We go
00108Cr 3                               ; from bottom to top
00108Cr 3  7A                           ply
00108Dr 3               
00108Dr 3  A9 rr                        lda #dsp0-1     ; go up one to avoid garbage
00108Fr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3
001091r 3  64 rr                        stz tmp3+1      ; must be zero page on the 65c02
001093r 3               @loop:
001093r 3  CA                           dex
001094r 3  CA                           dex
001095r 3               
001095r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp3)
001097r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001099r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp3
00109Br 3               
00109Br 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp3)
00109Dr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00109Fr 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp3
0010A1r 3  5A                           phy
0010A2r 3               
0010A2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dot
0010A5r 3               
0010A5r 3  7A                           ply
0010A6r 3  88                           dey
0010A7r 3  D0 EA                        bne @loop
0010A9r 3               
0010A9r 3  48                           pha             ; dummy to balance stack
0010AAr 3               @done:
0010AAr 3  68                           pla
0010ABr 3  60           z_dot_s:        rts
0010ACr 3               
0010ACr 3               
0010ACr 3               
0010ACr 3               ; ## D_DOT ( d -- ) "Print double"
0010ACr 3               ; ## "d."  tested  ANS double
0010ACr 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/double/Dd"""
0010ACr 3                       ;
0010ACr 3                       ; From the Forth code:
0010ACr 3                       ; : D. TUCK DABS <# #S ROT SIGN #> TYPE SPACE ;
0010ACr 3                       ; """
0010ACr 3               
0010ACr 3               xt_d_dot:
0010ACr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0010AFr 3               
0010AFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_tuck
0010B2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dabs
0010B5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_less_number_sign
0010B8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_s
0010BBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot
0010BEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_sign
0010C1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_greater
0010C4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
0010C7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
0010CAr 3               
0010CAr 3  60           z_d_dot:        rts
0010CBr 3               
0010CBr 3               
0010CBr 3               
0010CBr 3               ; ## D_DOT_R ( d u -- ) "Print double right-justified u wide"
0010CBr 3               ; ## "d.r"  tested  ANS double
0010CBr 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/double/DDotR"""
0010CBr 3                       ; Based on the Forth code
0010CBr 3                       ;  : D.R >R TUCK DABS <# #S ROT SIGN #> R> OVER - SPACES TYPE ;
0010CBr 3                       ; """
0010CBr 3               
0010CBr 3               xt_d_dot_r:
0010CBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
0010CEr 3                               ; From the forth code:
0010CEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r
0010D1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_tuck
0010D4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dabs
0010D7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_less_number_sign
0010DAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_s
0010DDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot
0010E0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_sign
0010E3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_greater
0010E6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from
0010E9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_over
0010ECr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
0010EFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_spaces
0010F2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
0010F5r 3               
0010F5r 3  60           z_d_dot_r:      rts

0010F6r 3               ; ## DROP ( u -- ) "Pop top entry on Data Stack"
0010F6r 3               ; ## "drop"  auto  ANS core
0010F6r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/DROP"""
0010F6r 3               xt_drop:
