001587r 3                               ; Pathological case: Drop the rest of this number off the stack
001587r 3                               ; and continue with the next word. Doesn't print a warning. We
001587r 3                               ; need to drop four cells, that is, eight bytes
001587r 3  8A                           txa
001588r 3  18                           clc
001589r 3  69 08                        adc #8
00158Br 3  AA                           tax
00158Cr 3  80 C4                        bra @loop
00158Er 3               
00158Er 3               @done:
00158Er 3                               ; Clean up return stack and calculate number of chars stored
00158Er 3  E8                           inx
00158Fr 3  E8                           inx
001590r 3  E8                           inx
001591r 3  E8                           inx                     ; 2DROP
001592r 3               
001592r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_two_r_from       ; ( addr2+n addr2 )
001595r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
001598r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus            ; ( n )
00159Br 3               
00159Br 3  60           z_hexstore:     rts
00159Cr 3               
00159Cr 3               
00159Cr 3               
00159Cr 3               ; ## HOLD ( char -- ) "Insert character at current output"
00159Cr 3               ; ## "hold"  auto  ANS core
00159Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/HOLD
00159Cr 3                       ; Insert a character at the current position of a pictured numeric
00159Cr 3                       ; output string on
00159Cr 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/numberio.fth
00159Cr 3                       ;
00159Cr 3                       ; Forth code is : HOLD  -1 HLD +!  HLD @ C! ;  We use the the internal
00159Cr 3                       ; variable tohold instead of HLD.
00159Cr 3                       ; """
00159Cr 3               xt_hold:
00159Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
00159Fr 3               
00159Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda tohold
0015A1r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
0015A3r 3  C6 rr                        dec tohold+1
0015A5r 3               @1:
0015A5r 3  C6 rr                        dec tohold
0015A7r 3               
0015A7r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0015A9r 3  92 rr                        sta (tohold)
0015ABr 3  E8                           inx
0015ACr 3  E8                           inx
0015ADr 3               
0015ADr 3  60           z_hold:         rts
0015AEr 3               
0015AEr 3               
0015AEr 3               ; ## I ( -- n )(R: n -- n)  "Copy loop counter to stack"
0015AEr 3               ; ## "i"  auto  ANS core
0015AEr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/I
0015AEr 3                       ; Note that this is not the same as R@ because we use a fudge
0015AEr 3                       ; factor for loop control; see the Control Flow section of the
0015AEr 3                       ; manual for details.
0015AEr 3                       ;
0015AEr 3                       ; We should make this native compile for speed.
0015AEr 3                       ; """
0015AEr 3               
0015AEr 3               xt_i:
0015AEr 3  CA                           dex
0015AFr 3  CA                           dex
0015B0r 3               
0015B0r 3                               ; Get the fudged index off of the top of the stack. It's
0015B0r 3                               ; easier to do math on the stack directly than to pop and
0015B0r 3                               ; push stuff around
0015B0r 3  86 rr                        stx tmpdsp
0015B2r 3  BA                           tsx
0015B3r 3               
0015B3r 3  38                           sec
0015B4r 3  BD 01 01                     lda $0101,x     ; LSB
0015B7r 3  FD 03 01                     sbc $0103,x
0015BAr 3  A8                           tay
0015BBr 3               
0015BBr 3  BD 02 01                     lda $0102,x     ; MSB
0015BEr 3  FD 04 01                     sbc $0104,x
0015C1r 3               
0015C1r 3  A6 rr                        ldx tmpdsp
0015C3r 3               
0015C3r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x         ; MSB of de-fudged index
0015C5r 3  94 00                        sty 0,x         ; LSB of de-fudged index
0015C7r 3               
0015C7r 3  60           z_i:            rts
0015C8r 3               
0015C8r 3               
0015C8r 3               
0015C8r 3               ; ## IF (C: -- orig) (flag -- ) "Conditional flow control"
0015C8r 3               ; ## "if"  auto  ANS core
0015C8r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/IF"""
0015C8r 3               
0015C8r 3               xt_if:
0015C8r 3                               ; Compile a 0BRANCH
0015C8r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>zero_branch_runtime
0015CAr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<zero_branch_runtime
0015CCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
0015CFr 3               
0015CFr 3                               ; Put the origination address on the stack for else/then
0015CFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_here
0015D2r 3               
0015D2r 3                               ; Stuff zero in for the branch address right now.
0015D2r 3                               ; THEN or ELSE will fix it later.
0015D2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
0015D5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
0015D8r 3  60           z_if:           rts
0015D9r 3               
0015D9r 3               
0015D9r 3               zero_branch_runtime:
0015D9r 3                       ; """In some Forths, this is called (0BRANCH). Tali Forth originally
0015D9r 3                       ; included 0BRANCH as a high-level word that inserted this code at
0015D9r 3                       ; runtime.
0015D9r 3                       ; """
0015D9r 3               
0015D9r 3                               ; We use the return value on the 65c02 stack to determine
0015D9r 3                               ; where we want to return to.
0015D9r 3  68                           pla
0015DAr 3  85 rr                        sta tmpbranch
0015DCr 3  68                           pla
0015DDr 3  85 rr                        sta tmpbranch+1
0015DFr 3               
0015DFr 3                               ; See if the flag is zero, which is the whole purpose of
0015DFr 3                               ; this all
0015DFr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0015E1r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
0015E3r 3  F0 0F                        beq @zero
0015E5r 3               
0015E5r 3                               ; Flag is TRUE, so we skip over the next two bytes. This is
0015E5r 3                               ; the part between IF and THEN
0015E5r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpbranch   ; LSB
0015E7r 3  18                           clc
0015E8r 3  69 02                        adc #2
0015EAr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
0015ECr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpbranch+1 ; MSB
0015EEr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; For carry
0015F0r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
0015F2r 3               
0015F2r 3  80 13                        bra @done
0015F4r 3               
0015F4r 3               @zero:
0015F4r 3                               ; Flag is FALSE (0) so we take the jump to the address given in
0015F4r 3                               ; the next two bytes. However, the address points to the last
0015F4r 3                               ; byte of the JSR instruction, not to the next byte afterwards
0015F4r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
0015F6r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmpbranch),y
0015F8r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
0015FAr 3  C8                           iny
0015FBr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmpbranch),y
0015FDr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
0015FFr 3               
0015FFr 3                               ; Now we have to subtract one byte from the address
0015FFr 3                               ; given because of the way the 6502 calculates RTS
0015FFr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001601r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
001603r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1+1
001605r 3               @1:
001605r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1
001607r 3               
001607r 3               @done:
001607r 3                               ; However we got here, tmp1 has the value we push to jump
001607r 3                               ; to
001607r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
001609r 3  48                           pha             ; MSB first
00160Ar 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
00160Cr 3  48                           pha
00160Dr 3               
00160Dr 3                               ; clean up the stack and jump
00160Dr 3  E8                           inx
00160Er 3  E8                           inx
00160Fr 3               
00160Fr 3  60                           rts
001610r 3               
001610r 3               
001610r 3               
001610r 3               ; ## IMMEDIATE ( -- ) "Mark most recent word as IMMEDIATE"
001610r 3               ; ## "immediate"  auto  ANS core
001610r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/IMMEDIATE
001610r 3                       ; Make sure the most recently defined word is immediate. Will only
001610r 3                       ; affect the last word in the dictionary. Note that if the word is
001610r 3                       ; defined in ROM, this will have no affect, but will not produce an
001610r 3                       ; error message.
001610r 3                       ; """
001610r 3               xt_immediate:
001610r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
001613r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1          ; offset for status byte
001615r 3  B1 rr                        lda (dp),y
001617r 3  09 04                        ora #IM        ; make sure bit 7 is set
001619r 3  91 rr                        sta (dp),y
00161Br 3               
00161Br 3  60           z_immediate:    rts
00161Cr 3               
00161Cr 3               
00161Cr 3               ; ## INPUT ( -- addr ) "Return address of input vector"
00161Cr 3               ; ## "input" tested Tali Forth
00161Cr 3               
00161Cr 3               xt_input:
00161Cr 3  CA                           dex
00161Dr 3  CA                           dex
00161Er 3  A9 rr                        lda #<input
001620r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001622r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>input
001624r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001626r 3               
001626r 3  60           z_input:        rts
001627r 3               
001627r 3               
001627r 3               
001627r 3               ; ## INPUT_TO_R ( -- ) ( R: -- n n n n ) "Save input state to the Return Stack"
001627r 3               ; ## "input>r"  tested  Tali Forth
001627r 3                  	; """Save the current input state as defined by insrc, cib, ciblen, and
001627r 3                       ; toin to the Return Stack. Used by EVALUTE.
001627r 3                       ;
001627r 3                       ; The naive way of doing
001627r 3                       ; this is to push each two-byte variable to the stack in the form of
001627r 3                       ;
001627r 3                       ;       lda insrc
001627r 3                       ;       pha
001627r 3                       ;       lda insrc+1
001627r 3                       ;       pha
001627r 3                       ;
001627r 3                       ; for a total of 24 byte of instruction in one direction and later
001627r 3                       ; a further 24 bytes to reverse the process. We shorten this at the
001627r 3                       ; cost of some speed by assuming the four variables are grouped
001627r 3                       ; together on the Zero Page and start with insrc (see definitions.asm
001627r 3                       ; for details). The reverse operation is r_to_input. These words must
001627r 3                       ; be flagged as Never Native. Uses tmp1
001627r 3                       ; """
001627r 3               
001627r 3               xt_input_to_r:
001627r 3                               ; We arrive here with the return address on the top of the
001627r 3                               ; 65c02's stack. We need to move it out of the way first
001627r 3  68                           pla
001628r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
00162Ar 3  68                           pla
00162Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
00162Dr 3               
00162Dr 3                               ; This assumes that insrc is the first of eight bytes and
00162Dr 3                               ; toin+1 the last in the sequence we want to save from the Zero
00162Dr 3                               ; Page.
00162Dr 3  A0 07                        ldy #7
00162Fr 3               @loop:
00162Fr 3  B9 rr rr                     lda insrc,y     ; insrc+7 is toin+1
001632r 3  48                           pha
001633r 3  88                           dey
001634r 3  10 F9                        bpl @loop
001636r 3               
001636r 3                               ; Restore address for return jump
001636r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
001638r 3  48                           pha
001639r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
00163Br 3  48                           pha
00163Cr 3               
00163Cr 3  60           z_input_to_r: 	rts
00163Dr 3               
00163Dr 3               
00163Dr 3               
00163Dr 3               ; ## INT_TO_NAME ( xt -- nt ) "Get name token from execution token"
00163Dr 3               ; ## "int>name"  auto  Tali Forth
00163Dr 3                       ; """www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Name-token.html
00163Dr 3                       ; This is called >NAME in Gforth, but we change it to
00163Dr 3                       ; INT>NAME to match NAME>INT
00163Dr 3                       ; """
00163Dr 3               
00163Dr 3               xt_int_to_name:
00163Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001640r 3               
001640r 3                               ; Unfortunately, to find the header, we have to walk through
001640r 3                               ; all of the wordlists. We are running out of tmp variables.
001640r 3                               ; (I'm assuming there is a reason this is avoiding tmp1) so
001640r 3                               ; hold the current wordlist on the data stack. This searches
001640r 3                               ; all of the wordlists in id order.
001640r 3  CA                           dex
001641r 3  CA                           dex
001642r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
001644r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001646r 3               
001646r 3               @wordlist_loop:
001646r 3                               ; A needs to have the current wordlist id in it at
001646r 3                               ; the top of this loop.
001646r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x                 ; Get the current wordlist.
001648r 3               
001648r 3                               ; Get the DP for that wordlist.
001648r 3  0A                           asl                     ; Turn offset into cells offset.
001649r 3  18                           clc
00164Ar 3  69 06                        adc #wordlists_offset
00164Cr 3  A8                           tay
00164Dr 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y              ; Save the DP for this wordlist
00164Fr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2                ; into tmp2
001651r 3  C8                           iny
001652r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
001654r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
001656r 3               
001656r 3                               ; Check for an empty wordlist (DP will be 0)
001656r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001658r 3  05 rr                        ora tmp2+1
00165Ar 3  F0 38                        beq @next_wordlist
00165Cr 3               
00165Cr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; Target xt is now behind wordlist id.
00165Er 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3        ; Save target xt in tmp3
001660r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
001662r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3+1
001664r 3               
001664r 3               @loop:
001664r 3  A0 04                        ldy #4          ; xt is four bytes down
001666r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp2),y    ; LSB of xt of current nt
001668r 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp3
00166Ar 3  D0 07                        bne @no_match
00166Cr 3               
00166Cr 3                               ; LSB is the same, now check MSB
00166Cr 3  C8                           iny
00166Dr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp2),y    ; MSB of xt of current nt
00166Fr 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp3+1
001671r 3  F0 32                        beq @match
001673r 3               
001673r 3               @no_match:
001673r 3                               ; no match, so we need to get the next word. Next nt is two
001673r 3                               ; bytes down
001673r 3  18                           clc
001674r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001676r 3  69 02                        adc #2
001678r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
00167Ar 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
00167Cr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only care about carry
00167Er 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
001680r 3               
001680r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
001682r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp2),y
001684r 3  48                           pha
001685r 3  C8                           iny
001686r 3  11 rr                        ora (tmp2),y
001688r 3  F0 09                        beq @zero
00168Ar 3               
00168Ar 3                               ; Not zero continue
00168Ar 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp2),y
00168Cr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
00168Er 3  68                           pla
00168Fr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
001691r 3  80 D1                        bra @loop
001693r 3               
001693r 3               @zero:
001693r 3                               ; if next word is zero, the xt has no nt in this wordlist
001693r 3  68                           pla             ; Leftover from above loop
001694r 3               
001694r 3               @next_wordlist:
001694r 3                               ; Move on to the next wordlist.
001694r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001696r 3  1A                           inc
001697r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001699r 3  C9 0C                        cmp #max_wordlists
00169Br 3  D0 A9                        bne @wordlist_loop
00169Dr 3               
00169Dr 3                               ; We didn't find it in any of the wordlists.
00169Dr 3                               ; Remove the wordlist id from the stack.
00169Dr 3  E8                           inx
00169Er 3  E8                           inx
00169Fr 3               
00169Fr 3                               ; We return a zero to indicate that we didn't find it.
00169Fr 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
0016A1r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
0016A3r 3  80 0A                        bra z_int_to_name
0016A5r 3               
0016A5r 3               @match:
0016A5r 3                               ; We found it. Remove wordlist id from stack.
0016A5r 3  E8                           inx
0016A6r 3  E8                           inx
0016A7r 3               
0016A7r 3                               ; It's a match! Replace TOS with nt
0016A7r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
0016A9r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0016ABr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
0016ADr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0016AFr 3               
0016AFr 3  60           z_int_to_name:  rts
0016B0r 3               
0016B0r 3               
0016B0r 3               
0016B0r 3               ; ## INVERT ( n -- n ) "Complement of TOS"
0016B0r 3               ; ## "invert"  auto  ANS core
0016B0r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/INVERT"""
0016B0r 3               xt_invert:
0016B0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0016B3r 3               
0016B3r 3  A9 FF                        lda #$FF
0016B5r 3  55 00                        eor 0,x         ; LSB
0016B7r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0016B9r 3               
0016B9r 3  A9 FF                        lda #$FF
0016BBr 3  55 01                        eor 1,x         ; MSB
0016BDr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0016BFr 3               
0016BFr 3  60           z_invert:       rts
0016C0r 3               
0016C0r 3               
0016C0r 3               ; ## IS ( xt "name" -- ) "Set named word to execute xt"
0016C0r 3               ; ## "is"  auto  ANS core ext
0016C0r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/IS"""
0016C0r 3               
0016C0r 3               xt_is:
0016C0r 3                               ; This is a state aware word with differet behavior
0016C0r 3                               ; when used while compiling vs interpreting.
0016C0r 3                               ; Check STATE
0016C0r 3  A5 rr                        lda state
0016C2r 3  05 rr                        ora state+1
0016C4r 3  F0 0C                        beq @interpreting
0016C6r 3               
0016C6r 3               @compiling:
0016C6r 3                               ; Run ['] to compile the xt of the next word as a literal.
0016C6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_bracket_tick
0016C9r 3               
0016C9r 3                               ; Postpone DEFER! by compiling a JSR to it.
0016C9r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_defer_store
0016CBr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_defer_store
0016CDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
0016D0r 3               
0016D0r 3  80 06                        bra @done
0016D2r 3               
0016D2r 3               @interpreting:
0016D2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_tick
0016D5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_defer_store
0016D8r 3               @done:
0016D8r 3  60           z_is:           rts
0016D9r 3               
0016D9r 3               
0016D9r 3               
0016D9r 3               ; ## J ( -- n ) (R: n -- n ) "Copy second loop counter to stack"
0016D9r 3               ; ## "j"  auto  ANS core
0016D9r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/J
0016D9r 3                       ; Copy second loop counter from Return Stack to stack. Note we use
0016D9r 3                       ; a fudge factor for loop control; see the Control Flow section of
0016D9r 3                       ; the manual for more details.
0016D9r 3                       ; At this point, we have the "I" counter/limit and the LEAVE address
0016D9r 3                       ; on the stack above this (three entries), whereas the ideal Forth
0016D9r 3                       ; implementation would just have two.
0016D9r 3                       ;
0016D9r 3                       ; Make this native compiled for speed
0016D9r 3                       ; """
0016D9r 3               
0016D9r 3               xt_j:
0016D9r 3  CA                           dex
0016DAr 3  CA                           dex
0016DBr 3               
0016DBr 3                               ; Get the fudged index off from the stack. It's easier to
0016DBr 3                               ; do math on the stack directly than to pop and push stuff
0016DBr 3                               ; around
0016DBr 3  86 rr                        stx tmpdsp
0016DDr 3  BA                           tsx
0016DEr 3               
0016DEr 3  38                           sec
0016DFr 3  BD 07 01                     lda $0107,x     ; LSB
0016E2r 3  FD 09 01                     sbc $0109,x
0016E5r 3  A8                           tay
0016E6r 3               
0016E6r 3  BD 08 01                     lda $0108,x     ; MSB
0016E9r 3  FD 0A 01                     sbc $010A,x
0016ECr 3               
0016ECr 3  A6 rr                        ldx tmpdsp
0016EEr 3               
0016EEr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x         ; MSB of de-fudged index
0016F0r 3  94 00                        sty 0,x         ; LSB of de-fudged index
0016F2r 3               
0016F2r 3  60           z_j:            rts
0016F3r 3               
0016F3r 3               
0016F3r 3               
0016F3r 3               ; ## KEY ( -- char ) "Get one character from the input"
0016F3r 3               ; ## "key"  tested  ANS core
0016F3r 3               xt_key:
0016F3r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/KEY
0016F3r 3                       ; Get a single character of input from the vectored
0016F3r 3                       ; input without echoing.
0016F3r 3                       ; """
0016F3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr key_a               ; returns char in A
0016F6r 3               
0016F6r 3  CA                           dex
0016F7r 3  CA                           dex
0016F8r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0016FAr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
0016FCr 3               
0016FCr 3  60           z_key:          rts
0016FDr 3               
0016FDr 3               key_a:
0016FDr 3                       ; The 65c02 doesn't have a JSR (ADDR,X) instruction like the
0016FDr 3                       ; 65816, so we have to fake the indirect jump to vector it.
0016FDr 3                       ; This is depressingly slow. We use this routine internally
0016FDr 3                       ; to avoid manipulating the Data Stack when we just want a
0016FDr 3                       ; character
0016FDr 3  6C rr rr                     jmp (input)             ; JSR/RTS
001700r 3               
001700r 3               
001700r 3               ; ## LATESTNT ( -- nt ) "Push most recent nt to the stack"
001700r 3               ; ## "latestnt"  auto  Tali Forth
001700r 3                       ; """www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Name-token.html
001700r 3                       ; The Gforth version of this word is called LATEST
001700r 3                       ; """
001700r 3               xt_latestnt:
001700r 3  CA                           dex
001701r 3  CA                           dex
001702r 3               
001702r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
001705r 3               
001705r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp
001707r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001709r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp+1
00170Br 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00170Dr 3               
00170Dr 3  60           z_latestnt:     rts
00170Er 3               
00170Er 3               
00170Er 3               ; ## LATESTXT ( -- xt ) "Push most recent xt to the stack"
00170Er 3               ; ## "latestxt"  auto  Gforth
00170Er 3                       ; """http://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Anonymous-Definitions.html"""
00170Er 3               xt_latestxt:
00170Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_latestnt         ; ( nt )
001711r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_name_to_int      ; ( xt )
001714r 3               
001714r 3  60           z_latestxt:     rts
001715r 3               
001715r 3               
001715r 3               ; ## LEAVE ( -- ) "Leave DO/LOOP construct"
001715r 3               ; ## "leave"  auto  ANS core
001715r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/LEAVE
001715r 3                       ; Note that this does not work with anything but a DO/LOOP in
001715r 3                       ; contrast to other versions such as discussed at
001715r 3                       ; http://blogs.msdn.com/b/ashleyf/archive/2011/02/06/loopty-do-i-loop.aspx
001715r 3                       ;
001715r 3                       ;       : LEAVE POSTPONE BRANCH HERE SWAP 0 , ; IMMEDIATE COMPILE-ONLY
001715r 3                       ; See the Control Flow section in the manual for details of how this works.
001715r 3                       ; This must be native compile and not IMMEDIATE
001715r 3                       ; """
001715r 3               
001715r 3               xt_leave:
001715r 3                               ; We dump the limit/start entries off the Return Stack
001715r 3                               ; (four bytes)
001715r 3  68                           pla
001716r 3  68                           pla
001717r 3  68                           pla
001718r 3  68                           pla
001719r 3               
001719r 3  60                           rts             ; this must be compiled, so keep before z_leave
00171Ar 3               z_leave:                        ; not reached, not compiled
00171Ar 3               
00171Ar 3               
00171Ar 3               
00171Ar 3               ; ## LEFT_BRACKET ( -- ) "Enter interpretation state"
00171Ar 3               ; ## "["  auto  ANS core
00171Ar 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Bracket
00171Ar 3                       ; This is an immediate and compile-only word
00171Ar 3                       ; """
00171Ar 3               xt_left_bracket:
00171Ar 3  64 rr                        stz state
00171Cr 3  64 rr                        stz state+1
00171Er 3               
00171Er 3  60           z_left_bracket: rts
00171Fr 3               
00171Fr 3               
00171Fr 3               ; ## LESS_NUMBER_SIGN ( -- ) "Start number conversion"
00171Fr 3               ; ## "<#"  auto  ANS core
00171Fr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/num-start
00171Fr 3                       ; Start the process to create pictured numeric output.
00171Fr 3                       ;
00171Fr 3                       ; The new
00171Fr 3                       ; string is constructed from back to front, saving the new character
00171Fr 3                       ; at the beginning of the output string. Since we use PAD as a
00171Fr 3                       ; starting address and work backward (!), the string is constructed
00171Fr 3                       ; in the space between the end of the Dictionary (as defined by CP)
00171Fr 3                       ; and the PAD. This allows us to satisfy the ANS Forth condition that
00171Fr 3                       ; programs don't fool around with the PAD but still use its address.
00171Fr 3                       ; Based on pForth
00171Fr 3                       ; http://pforth.googlecode.com/svn/trunk/fth/numberio.fth
00171Fr 3                       ; pForth is in the pubic domain. Forth is : <# PAD HLD ! ; we use the
00171Fr 3                       ; internal variable tohold instead of HLD.
00171Fr 3                       ; """
00171Fr 3               xt_less_number_sign:
00171Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_pad      ; ( addr )
001722r 3               
001722r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001724r 3  85 rr                        sta tohold
001726r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
001728r 3  85 rr                        sta tohold+1
00172Ar 3               
00172Ar 3  E8                           inx
00172Br 3  E8                           inx
00172Cr 3               
00172Cr 3               z_less_number_sign:
00172Cr 3  60                           rts
00172Dr 3               
00172Dr 3               ; ## LESS_THAN ( n m -- f ) "Return true if NOS < TOS"
00172Dr 3               ; ## "<"  auto  ANS core
00172Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/less"""
00172Dr 3               
00172Dr 3               xt_less_than:
00172Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001730r 3               
001730r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; default false
001732r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr compare_16bit
001735r 3               
001735r 3                               ; for signed numbers, NOS < TOS if Z=0 and N=0
001735r 3  F0 03                        beq @false
001737r 3  30 01                        bmi @false
001739r 3               
001739r 3                               ; true
001739r 3  88                           dey
00173Ar 3               @false:
00173Ar 3  98                           tya
00173Br 3               
00173Br 3  E8                           inx
00173Cr 3  E8                           inx
00173Dr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00173Fr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001741r 3               
001741r 3  60           z_less_than:    rts
001742r 3               
001742r 3               
001742r 3               
001742r 3               ; ## LIST ( scr# -- ) "List the given screen"
001742r 3               ; ## "list"  tested  ANS block ext
001742r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/block/LIST"""
001742r 3               
001742r 3               xt_list:
001742r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001745r 3               
001745r 3                               ; Save the screen number in SCR
001745r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_scr
001748r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_store
00174Br 3               
00174Br 3                               ; Use L from the editor-wordlist to display the screen.
00174Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_l
00174Er 3               
00174Er 3  60           z_list:         rts
00174Fr 3               
00174Fr 3               
00174Fr 3               
00174Fr 3               ; ## LITERAL ( n -- ) "Store TOS to be push on stack during runtime"
00174Fr 3               ; ## "literal"  auto  ANS core
00174Fr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/LITERAL
00174Fr 3                       ; Compile-only word to store TOS so that it is pushed on stack
00174Fr 3                       ; during runtime. This is a immediate, compile-only word. At runtime,
00174Fr 3                       ; it works by calling literal_runtime by compling JSR LITERAL_RT.
00174Fr 3                       ;
00174Fr 3                       ; Note the cmpl_ routines use TMPTOS
00174Fr 3                       ; """
00174Fr 3               xt_literal:
00174Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001752r 3               
001752r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>literal_runtime
001754r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<literal_runtime
001756r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001759r 3               
001759r 3                               ; Compile the value that is to be pushed on the Stack during
001759r 3                               ; runtime
001759r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
00175Cr 3               
00175Cr 3  60           z_literal:      rts
00175Dr 3               
00175Dr 3               literal_runtime:
00175Dr 3               
00175Dr 3                               ; During runtime, we push the value following this word back
00175Dr 3                               ; on the Data Stack. The subroutine jump that brought us
00175Dr 3                               ; here put the address to return to on the Return Stack -
00175Dr 3                               ; this points to the data we need to get. This routine is
00175Dr 3                               ; also called (LITERAL) in some Forths
00175Dr 3  CA                           dex
00175Er 3  CA                           dex
00175Fr 3               
00175Fr 3                           	; The 65c02 stores <RETURN-ADDRESS>-1 on the Return Stack,
00175Fr 3                               ; so we are actually popping the address-1 of the literal
00175Fr 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
001760r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001762r 3  68                           pla             ; MSB
001763r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001765r 3               
001765r 3                               ; Fetch the actual literal value and push it on Data stack
001765r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
001767r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y    ; LSB
001769r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00176Br 3  C8                           iny
00176Cr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y    ; MSB
00176Er 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001770r 3               
001770r 3                               ; Adjust return address and push back on the Return Stack
001770r 3  98                           tya
001771r 3  18                           clc
001772r 3  65 rr                        adc tmp1
001774r 3  A8                           tay
001775r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
001777r 3  69 00                        adc #0
001779r 3  48                           pha
00177Ar 3  5A                           phy
00177Br 3               
00177Br 3  60                           rts
00177Cr 3               
00177Cr 3               
00177Cr 3               
00177Cr 3               ; ## LOAD ( scr# -- ) "Load the Forth code in a screen/block"
00177Cr 3               ; ## "load"  auto  ANS block
00177Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/block/LOAD
00177Cr 3                       ;
00177Cr 3                       ; Note: LOAD current works because there is only one buffer.
00177Cr 3                       ; If/when multiple buffers are supported, we'll have to deal
00177Cr 3                       ; with the fact that it might re-load the old block into a
00177Cr 3                       ; different buffer.
00177Cr 3                       ; """
00177Cr 3               
00177Cr 3               xt_load:
00177Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
00177Fr 3               
00177Fr 3                               ; Save the current value of BLK on the return stack.
00177Fr 3  A0 01                        ldy #blk_offset+1
001781r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
001783r 3  48                           pha
001784r 3  88                           dey
001785r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
001787r 3  48                           pha
001788r 3               
001788r 3                               ; Set BLK to the given block/screen number.
001788r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00178Ar 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
00178Cr 3  C8                           iny
00178Dr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
00178Fr 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
001791r 3               
001791r 3                               ; Load that block into a buffer
001791r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_block
001794r 3               
001794r 3                               ; Put 1024 on the stack for the screen length.
001794r 3  CA                           dex
001795r 3  CA                           dex
001796r 3  A9 04                        lda #4
001798r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00179Ar 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
00179Cr 3               
00179Cr 3                               ; Jump to a special evluate target. This bypasses the underflow
00179Cr 3                               ; check and skips the zeroing of BLK.
00179Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr load_evaluate
00179Fr 3               
00179Fr 3                               ; Restore the value of BLK from before the LOAD command.
00179Fr 3  A0 00                        ldy #blk_offset
0017A1r 3  68                           pla
0017A2r 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
0017A4r 3  C8                           iny
0017A5r 3  68                           pla
0017A6r 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
0017A8r 3               
0017A8r 3                               ; If BLK is not zero, read it back into the buffer.
0017A8r 3                               ; A still has MSB
0017A8r 3  88                           dey
0017A9r 3  11 rr                        ora (up),y
0017ABr 3  F0 12                        beq @done
0017ADr 3               
0017ADr 3                               ; The block needs to be read back into the buffer.
0017ADr 3  CA                           dex
0017AEr 3  CA                           dex
0017AFr 3  A0 00                        ldy #blk_offset
0017B1r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
0017B3r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0017B5r 3  C8                           iny
0017B6r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
0017B8r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0017BAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_block
0017BDr 3               
0017BDr 3                               ; Drop the buffer address.
0017BDr 3  E8                           inx
0017BEr 3  E8                           inx
0017BFr 3               
0017BFr 3               @done:
0017BFr 3  60           z_load:         rts
0017C0r 3               
0017C0r 3               
0017C0r 3               
0017C0r 3               ; ## LOOP ( -- ) "Finish loop construct"
0017C0r 3               ; ## "loop"  auto  ANS core
0017C0r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/LOOP
0017C0r 3                       ; Compile-time part of LOOP. This does nothing more but push 1 on
0017C0r 3                       ; the stack and then call +LOOP.
0017C0r 3                       ;
0017C0r 3                       ; In Forth, this is
0017C0r 3                       ;       : LOOP  POSTPONE 1 POSTPONE (+LOOP) , POSTPONE UNLOOP ;
0017C0r 3                       ;       IMMEDIATE ; COMPILE-ONLY
0017C0r 3                       ; """
0017C0r 3               xt_loop:
0017C0r 3                               ; Have the finished word push 1 on the stack
0017C0r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_one
0017C2r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_one
0017C4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine     ; drop through to +LOOP
0017C7r 3               
0017C7r 3               
0017C7r 3               ; ## PLUS_LOOP ( -- ) "Finish loop construct"
0017C7r 3               ; ## "+loop"  auto  ANS core
0017C7r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PlusLOOP
0017C7r 3                       ;
0017C7r 3                       ; Compile-time part of +LOOP, also used for LOOP. Is usually
0017C7r 3                       ;       : +LOOP POSTPONE (+LOOP) , POSTPONE UNLOOP ; IMMEDIATE
0017C7r 3                       ;       COMPILE-ONLY
0017C7r 3                       ; in Forth. LOOP uses this routine as well. We jump here with the
0017C7r 3                       ; address for looping as TOS and the address for aborting the loop
0017C7r 3                       ; (LEAVE) as the second double-byte entry on the Return Stack (see
0017C7r 3                       ; DO and the Control Flow section of the manual for details).
0017C7r 3                       ; """
0017C7r 3               
0017C7r 3               xt_plus_loop:
0017C7r 3                               ; Compile the run-time part. We do this with a short loop
0017C7r 3                               ; and not a call to COMPILE, because it has to be natively
0017C7r 3                               ; coded anyway.
0017C7r 3  A0 11                        ldy #plus_loop_runtime_end-plus_loop_runtime
0017C9r 3  5A                           phy             ; save counter to adjust CP
0017CAr 3               @1:
0017CAr 3  B9 rr rr                     lda plus_loop_runtime,y
0017CDr 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
0017CFr 3  88                           dey
0017D0r 3  10 F8                        bpl @1
0017D2r 3               
0017D2r 3                               ; Adjust CP
0017D2r 3  68                           pla
0017D3r 3  18                           clc
0017D4r 3  65 rr                        adc cp
0017D6r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
0017D8r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
0017DAr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only need carry
0017DCr 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
0017DEr 3               
0017DEr 3                               ; The address we need to loop back to is TOS. Store it so
0017DEr 3                               ; the runtime part of +LOOP jumps back up there
0017DEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
0017E1r 3               
0017E1r 3                               ; Compile an UNLOOP for when we're all done. This is a series
0017E1r 3                               ; of six PLA, so we just do it here instead jumping around
0017E1r 3                               ; all over the place
0017E1r 3  A9 68                        lda #$68                ; opcode for PLA
0017E3r 3  A0 06                        ldy #6
0017E5r 3               @2:
0017E5r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
0017E7r 3  88                           dey
0017E8r 3  10 FB                        bpl @2
0017EAr 3               
0017EAr 3                               ; Adjust CP
0017EAr 3  A9 06                        lda #6
0017ECr 3  18                           clc
0017EDr 3  65 rr                        adc cp
0017EFr 3  85 rr                        sta cp
0017F1r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
0017F3r 3  69 00                        adc #0                  ; only need carry
0017F5r 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
0017F7r 3               
0017F7r 3                               ; Complete compile of DO/?DO by replacing the six
0017F7r 3                               ; dummy bytes by PHA instructions. The address where
0017F7r 3                               ; they are located is on the Data Stack
0017F7r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0017F9r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
0017FBr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0017FDr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
0017FFr 3  E8                           inx
001800r 3  E8                           inx
001801r 3               
001801r 3                               ; Because of the way that CP works, we don't have to save
001801r 3                               ; CP, but CP-1
001801r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
001803r 3  38                           sec
001804r 3  E9 01                        sbc #1
001806r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
001808r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
00180Ar 3  E9 00                        sbc #0
00180Cr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
00180Er 3               
00180Er 3                               ; now compile this in the DO/?DO routine
00180Er 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
001810r 3               
001810r 3  A9 A9                        lda #$A9        ; opcode for LDA immediate
001812r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001814r 3  C8                           iny
001815r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1      ; MSB
001817r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001819r 3  C8                           iny
00181Ar 3  A9 48                        lda #$48        ; Opcode for PHA
00181Cr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
00181Er 3  C8                           iny
00181Fr 3               
00181Fr 3  A9 A9                        lda #$A9        ; opcode for LDA immediate
001821r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001823r 3  C8                           iny
001824r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2        ; LSB
001826r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001828r 3  C8                           iny
001829r 3  A9 48                        lda #$48        ; Opcode for PHA
00182Br 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
00182Dr 3               z_loop:
00182Dr 3  60           z_plus_loop:    rts
00182Er 3               
00182Er 3               
00182Er 3               plus_loop_runtime:
00182Er 3                       ; """Runtime compile for loop control. This is used for both +LOOP and
00182Er 3                       ; LOOP which are defined at high level. Note we use a fudge factor for
00182Er 3                       ; loop control so we can test with the Overflow Flag. See
00182Er 3                       ; the Control Flow section of the manual for details.
00182Er 3                       ; The step value is TOS in the loop. This
00182Er 3                       ; must always be native compiled. In some Forths, this is a separate
00182Er 3                       ; word called (+LOOP) or (LOOP)
00182Er 3                       ; """
00182Er 3               
00182Er 3  18                           clc
00182Fr 3  68                           pla             ; LSB of index
001830r 3  75 00                        adc 0,x         ; LSB of step
001832r 3  A8                           tay             ; temporary storage of LSB
001833r 3               
001833r 3  B8                           clv
001834r 3  68                           pla             ; MSB of index
001835r 3  75 01                        adc 1,x         ; MSB of step
001837r 3  48                           pha             ; put MSB of index back on stack
001838r 3               
001838r 3  98                           tya             ; put LSB of index back on stack
001839r 3  48                           pha
00183Ar 3               
00183Ar 3  E8                           inx             ; dump step from TOS
00183Br 3  E8                           inx
00183Cr 3               
00183Cr 3                               ; If V flag is set, we're done looping and continue
00183Cr 3                               ; after the +LOOP instruction
00183Cr 3  70 03                        bvs @hack+3     ; skip over JMP instruction
00183Er 3               
00183Er 3               @hack:          ; This is why this routine must be natively compiled: We
00183Er 3                               ; compile the opcode for JMP here without an address to
00183Er 3                               ; go to, which is added by the next next instruction of
00183Er 3                               ; LOOP/+LOOP during compile time
00183Er 3  4C                           .byte $4C
00183Fr 3               
00183Fr 3               plus_loop_runtime_end:
00183Fr 3               
00183Fr 3               
00183Fr 3               ; ## LSHIFT ( x u -- u ) "Shift TOS left"
00183Fr 3               ; ## "lshift"  auto  ANS core
00183Fr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/LSHIFT"""
00183Fr 3               
00183Fr 3               xt_lshift:
00183Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001842r 3               
001842r 3                               ; max shift 16 times
001842r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001844r 3  29 0F                        and #%00001111
001846r 3  F0 08                        beq @done
001848r 3               
001848r 3  A8                           tay
001849r 3               
001849r 3               @loop:
001849r 3  16 02                        asl 2,x
00184Br 3  36 03                        rol 3,x
00184Dr 3  88                           dey
00184Er 3  D0 F9                        bne @loop
001850r 3               
001850r 3               @done:
001850r 3  E8                           inx
001851r 3  E8                           inx
001852r 3               
001852r 3  60           z_lshift:       rts
001853r 3               
001853r 3               
001853r 3               
001853r 3               ; ## M_STAR ( n n -- d ) "16 * 16 --> 32"
001853r 3               ; ## "m*"  auto  ANS core
001853r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MTimes
001853r 3                       ; Multiply two 16 bit numbers, producing a 32 bit result. All
001853r 3                       ; values are signed. Adapted from FIG Forth for Tali Forth.
001853r 3                       ;
001853r 3                       ; The original Forth is : M* OVER OVER XOR >R ABS SWAP ABS UM* R> D+- ;
001853r 3                       ; with  : D+- O< IF DNEGATE THEN ;
001853r 3                       ; """
001853r 3               
001853r 3               xt_m_star:
001853r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001856r 3               
001856r 3                               ; figure out the sign
001856r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB of n1
001858r 3  55 03                        eor 3,x         ; MSB of n2
00185Ar 3               
00185Ar 3                               ; UM* uses all kinds of temporary variables so we don't
00185Ar 3                               ; risk a conflict but just take the cycle hit and push
00185Ar 3                               ; this to the stack
00185Ar 3  48                           pha
00185Br 3               
00185Br 3                               ; get the absolute value of both numbers so we can feed
00185Br 3                               ; them to UM*, which does the real work
00185Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_abs
00185Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
001861r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_abs
001864r 3               
001864r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_star          ; ( d )
001867r 3               
001867r 3                               ; handle the sign
001867r 3  68                           pla
001868r 3  10 03                        bpl @done
00186Ar 3               
00186Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dnegate
00186Dr 3               @done:
00186Dr 3  60           z_m_star:       rts
00186Er 3               
00186Er 3               
00186Er 3               
00186Er 3               ; ## MARKER ( "name" -- ) "Create a deletion boundry"
00186Er 3               ; ## "marker"  auto  ANS core ext
00186Er 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MARKER
00186Er 3                       ; This word replaces FORGET in earlier Forths. Old entries are not
00186Er 3                       ; actually deleted, but merely overwritten by restoring CP and DP.
00186Er 3                       ; Run the named word at a later time to restore all of the wordlists
00186Er 3                       ; to their state when the word was created with marker.  Any words
00186Er 3                       ; created after the marker (including the marker) will be forgotten.
00186Er 3                       ;
00186Er 3                       ; To do this, we want to end up with something that jumps to a
00186Er 3                       ; run-time component with a link to the original CP and DP values:
00186Er 3                       ;
00186Er 3                       ;       jsr marker_runtime
00186Er 3                       ;       <Original CP MSB>
00186Er 3                       ;       <Original CP LSB>
00186Er 3                       ;       <Original DP MSB> ( for CURRENT wordlist )
00186Er 3                       ;       <Original DP LSB>
00186Er 3                       ;       < USER variables from offset 4 to 39 >
00186Er 3                       ;
00186Er 3                       ;       The user variables include:
00186Er 3                       ;       CURRENT (byte variable)
00186Er 3                       ;       <All wordlists> (currently 12) (cell array)
00186Er 3                       ;       <#ORDER> (byte variable)
00186Er 3                       ;       <All search order> (currently 9) (byte array)
00186Er 3                       ;
00186Er 3                       ; This code uses tmp1 and tmp2
00186Er 3                       ; """
00186Er 3               
00186Er 3               xt_marker:
00186Er 3                               ; Before we do anything, we need to save CP, which
00186Er 3                               ; after all is the whole point of this operation. CREATE
00186Er 3                               ; uses tmp1 and tmp2, so we take the speed hit and push stuff
00186Er 3                               ; to the stack
00186Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
001871r 3               
001871r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp
001873r 3  48                           pha
001874r 3  A5 rr                        lda dp+1
001876r 3  48                           pha
001877r 3               
001877r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
001879r 3  48                           pha
00187Ar 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
00187Cr 3  48                           pha
00187Dr 3               
00187Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_create
001880r 3               
001880r 3                               ; By default, CREATE installs a subroutine jump to DOVAR, which
001880r 3                               ; we have to replace by a jump to marker_runtime. We back up
001880r 3                               ; two bytes and then overwrite the address
001880r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp          ; LSB
001882r 3  38                           sec
001883r 3  E9 02                        sbc #2
001885r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
001887r 3               
001887r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1        ; MSB
001889r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0          ; we only care about the borrow
00188Br 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
00188Dr 3               
00188Dr 3                               ; Add the address of the runtime component
00188Dr 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>marker_runtime
00188Fr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<marker_runtime
001891r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
001894r 3               
001894r 3                               ; Add original CP as payload
001894r 3  7A                           ply                     ; MSB
001895r 3  68                           pla                     ; LSB
001896r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
001899r 3               
001899r 3                               ; Add original DP as payload
001899r 3  7A                           ply                     ; MSB
00189Ar 3  68                           pla                     ; LSB
00189Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
00189Er 3               
00189Er 3                               ; Add the user variables for the wordlists and search order.
00189Er 3                               ; We're compiling them in byte order.
00189Er 3  A0 04                        ldy #4                  ; Start at CURRENT
0018A0r 3               @marker_loop:
0018A0r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
0018A2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_a
0018A5r 3  C8                           iny
0018A6r 3  98                           tya
0018A7r 3  C9 28                        cmp #40                 ; One past the end of the search order.
0018A9r 3  D0 F5                        bne @marker_loop
0018ABr 3               
0018ABr 3  60           z_marker:       rts
0018ACr 3               
0018ACr 3               
0018ACr 3               
0018ACr 3               marker_runtime:
0018ACr 3                       ; """Restore Dictionary and memory (DP and CP) to where the were
0018ACr 3                       ; when this marker was defined. We arrive here with the return
0018ACr 3                       ; address on the Return Stack in the usual 65c02 format
0018ACr 3                       ; """
0018ACr 3               
0018ACr 3                               ; Get the address of the string address off the stack and
0018ACr 3                               ; increase by one because of the RTS mechanics
0018ACr 3  68                           pla
0018ADr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1        ; LSB of address
0018AFr 3  68                           pla
0018B0r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1      ; MSB of address
0018B2r 3               
0018B2r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1
0018B4r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
0018B6r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
0018B8r 3               @1:
0018B8r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
0018BAr 3               
0018BAr 3                               ; CP was stored first
0018BAr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
0018BCr 3  85 rr                        sta cp
0018BEr 3  C8                           iny
0018BFr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
0018C1r 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
0018C3r 3               
0018C3r 3                               ; Next was DP
0018C3r 3  C8                           iny
0018C4r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
0018C6r 3  85 rr                        sta dp
0018C8r 3  C8                           iny
0018C9r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
0018CBr 3  85 rr                        sta dp+1
0018CDr 3               
0018CDr 3                               ; Conveniently, the offset into both tmp1 and UP is 4
0018CDr 3                               ; to start restoring the wordlists and search order.
0018CDr 3  A0 04                        ldy #4
0018CFr 3               
0018CFr 3               @marker_restore_loop:
0018CFr 3                               ; Copy from the dictionary back on top of the wordlists
0018CFr 3                               ; and search order.
0018CFr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1), y
0018D1r 3  91 rr                        sta (up), y
0018D3r 3  C8                           iny
0018D4r 3  98                           tya
0018D5r 3  C9 28                        cmp #40                 ; One past the end of the search order.
0018D7r 3  D0 F6                        bne @marker_restore_loop
0018D9r 3               
0018D9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr dp_to_current       ; Move the CURRENT DP back.
0018DCr 3               
0018DCr 3                               ; The return instruction takes us back to the original caller
0018DCr 3  60                           rts
0018DDr 3               
0018DDr 3               
0018DDr 3               
0018DDr 3               ; ## MAX ( n n -- n ) "Keep larger of two numbers"
0018DDr 3               ; ## "max"  auto  ANS core
0018DDr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MAX
0018DDr 3                       ; Compare TOS and NOS and keep which one is larger. Adapted from
0018DDr 3                       ; Lance A. Leventhal "6502 Assembly Language Subroutines". Negative
0018DDr 3                       ; Flag indicates which number is larger. See also
0018DDr 3                       ; http://6502.org/tutorials/compare_instructions.html and
0018DDr 3                       ; http://www.righto.com/2012/12/the-6502-overflow-flag-explained.html
0018DDr 3                       ; """
0018DDr 3               
0018DDr 3               xt_max:
0018DDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0018E0r 3               
0018E0r 3                               ; Compare LSB. We do this first to set the carry flag
0018E0r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of TOS
0018E2r 3  D5 02                        cmp 2,x         ; LSB of NOS, this sets the carry
0018E4r 3               
0018E4r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB of TOS
0018E6r 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x         ; MSB of NOS
0018E8r 3  50 02                        bvc @no_overflow
0018EAr 3               
0018EAr 3                               ; handle overflow, because we use signed numbers
0018EAr 3  49 80                        eor #$80        ; complement negative flag
0018ECr 3               
0018ECr 3               @no_overflow:
0018ECr 3                               ; if negative, NOS is larger and needs to be kept
0018ECr 3  30 08                        bmi @keep_nos
0018EEr 3               
0018EEr 3                               ; move TOS to NOS
0018EEr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0018F0r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
0018F2r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0018F4r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
0018F6r 3               
0018F6r 3               @keep_nos:
0018F6r 3  E8                           inx
0018F7r 3  E8                           inx
0018F8r 3               
0018F8r 3  60           z_max:          rts
0018F9r 3               
0018F9r 3               
0018F9r 3               
0018F9r 3               ; ## MIN ( n n -- n ) "Keep smaller of two numbers"
0018F9r 3               ; ## "min"  auto  ANS core
0018F9r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MIN
0018F9r 3                       ; Adapted from Lance A. Leventhal "6502 Assembly Language
0018F9r 3                       ; Subroutines." Negative Flag indicateds which number is larger. See
0018F9r 3                       ; http://www.righto.com/2012/12/the-6502-overflow-flag-explained.html
0018F9r 3                       ; """
0018F9r 3               
0018F9r 3               xt_min:
0018F9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0018FCr 3               
0018FCr 3                               ; compare LSB. We do this first to set the carry flag
0018FCr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of TOS
0018FEr 3  D5 02                        cmp 2,x         ; LSB of NOS, this sets carry
001900r 3               
001900r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB of TOS
001902r 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x         ; MSB of NOS
001904r 3  50 02                        bvc @no_overflow
001906r 3               
001906r 3                               ; handle overflow because we use signed numbers
001906r 3  49 80                        eor #$80
001908r 3               
001908r 3               @no_overflow:
001908r 3                               ; if negative, NOS is larger and needs to be dumped
001908r 3  10 08                        bpl @keep_nos
00190Ar 3               
00190Ar 3                               ; move TOS to NOS
00190Ar 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00190Cr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
00190Er 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
001910r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001912r 3               
001912r 3               @keep_nos:
001912r 3  E8                           inx
001913r 3  E8                           inx
001914r 3               
001914r 3  60           z_min:          rts
001915r 3               
001915r 3               
001915r 3               
001915r 3               ; ## MINUS ( n n -- n ) "Subtract TOS from NOS"
001915r 3               ; ## "-"  auto  ANS core
001915r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Minus"""
001915r 3               xt_minus:
001915r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001918r 3               
001918r 3  38                           sec
001919r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB
00191Br 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x
00191Dr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
00191Fr 3               
00191Fr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB
001921r 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x
001923r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001925r 3               
001925r 3  E8                           inx
001926r 3  E8                           inx
001927r 3               
001927r 3  60           z_minus:        rts
001928r 3               
001928r 3               
001928r 3               ; ## MINUS_LEADING ( addr1 u1 -- addr2 u2 ) "Remove leading spaces"
001928r 3               ; ## "-leading"  auto  Tali String
001928r 3                       ; """Remove leading whitespace. This is the reverse of -TRAILING
001928r 3                       ; """
001928r 3               
001928r 3               xt_minus_leading:
001928r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00192Br 3               
00192Br 3               @loop:
00192Br 3                               ; Quit if we were given an empty string. This also terminates
00192Br 3                               ; the main loop
00192Br 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00192Dr 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
00192Fr 3  F0 0F                        beq @done
001931r 3               
001931r 3  A1 02                        lda (2,x)               ; get first character
001933r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr is_whitespace
001936r 3  90 08                        bcc @done
001938r 3               
001938r 3                               ; It's whitespace, move one down
001938r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one              ; ( addr u 1 )
00193Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_slash_string     ; ( addr+ u-1 )
00193Er 3               
00193Er 3  80 EB                        bra @loop
001940r 3               @done:
001940r 3               z_minus_leading:
001940r 3  60                           rts
001941r 3               
001941r 3               
001941r 3               
001941r 3               ; ## MINUS_TRAILING ( addr u1 -- addr u2 ) "Remove trailing spaces"
001941r 3               ; ## "-trailing"  auto  ANS string
001941r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/string/MinusTRAILING
001941r 3                       ; Remove trailing spaces
001941r 3                       ; """
001941r 3               
001941r 3               xt_minus_trailing:
001941r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001944r 3               
001944r 3                               ; if length entry is zero, return a zero and leave the
001944r 3                               ; address part untouched
001944r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of n
001946r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x         ; MSB of n
001948r 3  F0 33                        beq @done
00194Ar 3               
00194Ar 3                               ; Compute address of last char in tmp1 as
00194Ar 3                               ; addr + u1 - 1
00194Ar 3               
00194Ar 3                               ; addr + u1
00194Ar 3  18                           clc
00194Br 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB of addr
00194Dr 3  75 00                        adc 0,x
00194Fr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001951r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB of addr
001953r 3  75 01                        adc 1,x
001955r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001957r 3               
001957r 3                               ; - 1
001957r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001959r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
00195Br 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1+1
00195Dr 3               @1:
00195Dr 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1
00195Fr 3               
00195Fr 3               @loop:
00195Fr 3                               ; While spaces are found, move tmp1 backwards and
00195Fr 3                               ; decrease the count on the data stack.
00195Fr 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
001961r 3  C9 20                        cmp #AscSP
001963r 3  D0 18                        bne @done
001965r 3               
001965r 3                               ; Move back one address.
001965r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001967r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
001969r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1+1
00196Br 3               @2:
00196Br 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1
00196Dr 3               
00196Dr 3                               ; Decrement count by one.
00196Dr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00196Fr 3  D0 02                        bne @3
001971r 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
001973r 3               @3:
001973r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
001975r 3               
001975r 3                               ; Check if there are any characters left.
001975r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001977r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
001979r 3  F0 02                        beq @done       ; Count has reached zero - we're done!
00197Br 3               
00197Br 3  80 E2                        bra @loop
00197Dr 3               
00197Dr 3               @done:
00197Dr 3               z_minus_trailing:
00197Dr 3  60                           rts
00197Er 3               
00197Er 3               
00197Er 3               
00197Er 3               ; ## MOD ( n1 n2 -- n ) "Divide NOS by TOS and return the remainder"
00197Er 3               ; ## "mod"  auto  ANS core
00197Er 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MOD
00197Er 3                       ;
00197Er 3                       ; The Forth definition of this word is  : MOD /MOD DROP ;
00197Er 3                       ; so we just jump to xt_slash_mod and dump the actual result.
00197Er 3                       ; """
00197Er 3               xt_mod:
00197Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001981r 3               
001981r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_slash_mod
001984r 3               
001984r 3  E8                           inx             ; DROP
001985r 3  E8                           inx
001986r 3               z_mod:
001986r 3  60                           rts
001987r 3               
001987r 3               
001987r 3               ; ## MOVE ( addr1 addr2 u -- ) "Copy bytes"
001987r 3               ; ## "move"  auto  ANS core
001987r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/MOVE
001987r 3                       ; Copy u "address units" from addr1 to addr2. Since our address
001987r 3                       ; units are bytes, this is just a front-end for CMOVE and CMOVE>. This
001987r 3                       ; is actually the only one of these three words that is in the CORE
001987r 3                       ; set.
001987r 3                       ;
001987r 3                       ; This word must not be natively compiled.
001987r 3                       ; """
001987r 3               
001987r 3               xt_move:
001987r 3                               ; We let CMOVE and CMOVE> check if there is underflow or
001987r 3                               ; we've been told to copy zero bytes
001987r 3               
001987r 3                               ; compare MSB first
001987r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x                 ; MSB of addr2
001989r 3  D5 05                        cmp 5,x                 ; MSB of addr1
00198Br 3  F0 05                        beq @lsb                ; wasn't helpful, move to LSB
00198Dr 3  B0 0E                        bcs @to_move_up         ; we want CMOVE>
00198Fr 3               
00198Fr 3  4C rr rr                     jmp xt_cmove            ; JSR/RTS
001992r 3               
001992r 3               @lsb:
001992r 3                               ; MSB were equal, so do the whole thing over with LSB
001992r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x                 ; LSB of addr2
001994r 3  D5 04                        cmp 4,x                 ; LSB of addr1
001996r 3  F0 08                        beq @equal              ; LSB is equal as well
001998r 3  B0 03                        bcs @to_move_up         ; we want CMOVE>
00199Ar 3               
00199Ar 3  4C rr rr                     jmp xt_cmove            ; JSR/RTS
00199Dr 3               
00199Dr 3               @to_move_up:
00199Dr 3  4C rr rr                     jmp xt_cmove_up         ; JSR/RTS
0019A0r 3               @equal:
0019A0r 3                               ; drop three entries from Data Stack
0019A0r 3  8A                           txa
0019A1r 3  18                           clc
0019A2r 3  69 06                        adc #6
0019A4r 3  AA                           tax
0019A5r 3               
0019A5r 3  60           z_move:         rts
0019A6r 3               
0019A6r 3               
0019A6r 3               
0019A6r 3               ; ## NAME_TO_INT ( nt -- xt ) "Convert Name Token to Execute Token"
0019A6r 3               ; ## "name>int"  tested  Gforth
0019A6r 3                       ; """See
0019A6r 3                       ; https://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Name-token.html
0019A6r 3                       ; """
0019A6r 3               
0019A6r 3               xt_name_to_int:
0019A6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0019A9r 3               
0019A9r 3                               ; The xt starts four bytes down from the nt
0019A9r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0019ABr 3  18                           clc
0019ACr 3  69 04                        adc #4
0019AEr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3
0019B0r 3               
0019B0r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0019B2r 3  90 01                        bcc @done
0019B4r 3  1A                           inc
0019B5r 3               @done:
0019B5r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3+1
0019B7r 3               
0019B7r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
0019B9r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp3),y
0019BBr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0019BDr 3  C8                           iny
0019BEr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp3),y
0019C0r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0019C2r 3               
0019C2r 3  60           z_name_to_int:  rts
0019C3r 3               
0019C3r 3               
0019C3r 3               
0019C3r 3               ; ## NAME_TO_STRING ( nt -- addr u ) "Given a name token, return string of word"
0019C3r 3               ; ## "name>string"  tested  Gforth
0019C3r 3                       ; """http://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Name-token.html"""
0019C3r 3               
0019C3r 3               xt_name_to_string:
0019C3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0019C6r 3               
0019C6r 3  CA                           dex
0019C7r 3  CA                           dex
0019C8r 3               
0019C8r 3                               ; the length of the string is the first byte of the
0019C8r 3                               ; header pointed to by nt
0019C8r 3  A1 02                        lda (2,x)
0019CAr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0019CCr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
0019CEr 3               
0019CEr 3                               ; the string itself always starts eight bytes down
0019CEr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB
0019D0r 3  18                           clc
0019D1r 3  69 08                        adc #8
0019D3r 3  A8                           tay
0019D4r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB
0019D6r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; just need carry
0019D8r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
0019DAr 3  94 02                        sty 2,x
0019DCr 3               
0019DCr 3               z_name_to_string:
0019DCr 3  60                           rts
0019DDr 3               
0019DDr 3               
0019DDr 3               ; ## NC_LIMIT ( -- addr ) "Return address where NC-LIMIT value is kept"
0019DDr 3               ; ## "nc-limit"  tested  Tali Forth
0019DDr 3               
0019DDr 3               xt_nc_limit:
0019DDr 3  CA                           dex
0019DEr 3  CA                           dex
0019DFr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<nc_limit
0019E1r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0019E3r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>nc_limit
0019E5r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0019E7r 3               
0019E7r 3  60           z_nc_limit:     rts
0019E8r 3               
0019E8r 3               
0019E8r 3               
0019E8r 3               ; ## NEGATE ( n -- n ) "Two's complement"
0019E8r 3               ; ## "negate"  auto  ANS core
0019E8r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/NEGATE"""
0019E8r 3               xt_negate:
0019E8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0019EBr 3               
0019EBr 3  A9 00                	lda #0
0019EDr 3  38                           sec
0019EEr 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x         ; LSB
0019F0r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0019F2r 3               
0019F2r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
0019F4r 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x         ; MSB
0019F6r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0019F8r 3               
0019F8r 3  60           z_negate:       rts
0019F9r 3               
0019F9r 3
