0019F9r 3               ; ## NEVER_NATIVE ( -- ) "Flag last word as never natively compiled"
0019F9r 3               ; ## "never-native"  auto  Tali Forth
0019F9r 3               xt_never_native:
0019F9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr current_to_dp
0019FCr 3  A0 01                        ldy #1          ; offset for status byte
0019FEr 3  B1 rr                        lda (dp),y
001A00r 3  09 08                        ora #NN         ; Make sure NN flag is set
001A02r 3  29 FD                        and #$ff-AN     ; and AN flag is clear.
001A04r 3  91 rr                        sta (dp),y
001A06r 3               z_never_native:
001A06r 3  60                           rts
001A07r 3               
001A07r 3               
001A07r 3               ; ## NIP ( b a -- a ) "Delete NOS"
001A07r 3               ; ## "nip"  auto  ANS core ext
001A07r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/NIP"""
001A07r 3               xt_nip:
001A07r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001A0Ar 3               
001A0Ar 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB
001A0Cr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001A0Er 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB
001A10r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001A12r 3               
001A12r 3  E8                           inx
001A13r 3  E8                           inx
001A14r 3               
001A14r 3  60           z_nip:          rts
001A15r 3               
001A15r 3               
001A15r 3               ; ## NOT_EQUALS ( n m -- f ) "Return a true flag if TOS != NOS"
001A15r 3               ; ## "<>"  auto  ANS core ext
001A15r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/ne
001A15r 3                       ;
001A15r 3                       ; This is just a variant of EQUAL, we code it separately
001A15r 3                       ; for speed.
001A15r 3                       ; """
001A15r 3               
001A15r 3               xt_not_equals:
001A15r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001A18r 3               
001A18r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0                  ; default is true
001A1Ar 3               
001A1Ar 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x                 ; LSB
001A1Cr 3  D5 02                        cmp 2,x
001A1Er 3  D0 0A                        bne @not_equal
001A20r 3               
001A20r 3                               ; LSB is equal
001A20r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x                 ; MSB
001A22r 3  D5 03                        cmp 3,x
001A24r 3  D0 04                        bne @not_equal
001A26r 3               
001A26r 3  A9 FF                        lda #$FF
001A28r 3  80 01                        bra @done
001A2Ar 3               
001A2Ar 3               @not_equal:
001A2Ar 3  88                           dey                     ; drop thru to done
001A2Br 3               
001A2Br 3               @done:
001A2Br 3  98                           tya
001A2Cr 3  E8                           inx
001A2Dr 3  E8                           inx
001A2Er 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001A30r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001A32r 3               
001A32r 3  60           z_not_equals:   rts
001A33r 3               
001A33r 3               
001A33r 3               
001A33r 3               ; ## NOT_ROTE ( a b c -- c a b ) "Rotate upwards"
001A33r 3               ; ## "-rot"  auto  Gforth
001A33r 3                       ; """http://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Data-stack.html"""
001A33r 3               
001A33r 3               xt_not_rote:
001A33r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
001A36r 3               
001A36r 3  B4 01                        ldy 1,x         ; MSB first
001A38r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
001A3Ar 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001A3Cr 3               
001A3Cr 3  B5 05                        lda 5,x
001A3Er 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001A40r 3  94 05                        sty 5,x
001A42r 3               
001A42r 3  B4 00                        ldy 0,x         ; LSB second
001A44r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
001A46r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001A48r 3               
001A48r 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x
001A4Ar 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001A4Cr 3  94 04                        sty 4,x
001A4Er 3               
001A4Er 3  60           z_not_rote:     rts
001A4Fr 3               
001A4Fr 3               
001A4Fr 3               
001A4Fr 3               ; ## NUMBER ( addr u -- u | d ) "Convert a number string"
001A4Fr 3               ; ## "number"  auto  Tali Forth
001A4Fr 3                       ; """Convert a number string to a double or single cell number. This
001A4Fr 3                       ; is a wrapper for >NUMBER and follows the convention set out in the
001A4Fr 3                       ; "Forth Programmer's Handbook" (Conklin & Rather) 3rd edition p. 87.
001A4Fr 3                       ; Based in part on the "Starting Forth" code
001A4Fr 3                       ; https://www.forth.com/starting-forth/10-input-output-operators/
001A4Fr 3                       ; Gforth uses S>NUMBER? and S>UNUMBER? which return numbers and a flag
001A4Fr 3                       ; https://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Number-Conversion.html
001A4Fr 3                       ; Another difference to Gforth is that we follow ANS Forth that the
001A4Fr 3                       ; dot to signal a double cell number is required to be the last
001A4Fr 3                       ; character of the string.
001A4Fr 3                       ;
001A4Fr 3                       ; Number calls >NUMBER which in turn calls UM*,
001A4Fr 3                       ; which uses tmp1, tmp2, and tmp3, so we can't use them here, which is
001A4Fr 3                       ; a pain.
001A4Fr 3                       ;"""
001A4Fr 3               
001A4Fr 3               xt_number:
001A4Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001A52r 3               
001A52r 3                               ; we keep the flags for sign and double in tmpdsp because
001A52r 3                               ; we've run out of temporary variables
001A52r 3  64 rr                        stz tmpdsp      ; flag for double
001A54r 3  64 rr                        stz tmpdsp+1    ; flag for minus
001A56r 3               
001A56r 3                               ; If the first character is a minus, strip it off and set
001A56r 3                               ; the flag
001A56r 3  A1 02                        lda (2,x)
001A58r 3  C9 2D                        cmp #$2D        ; ASCII for "-"
001A5Ar 3  D0 0A                        bne @check_dot
001A5Cr 3               
001A5Cr 3                               ; It's a minus
001A5Cr 3  C6 rr                        dec tmpdsp+1
001A5Er 3  F6 02                        inc 2,x         ; start one character later
001A60r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
001A62r 3  F6 03                        inc 3,x
001A64r 3               @1:
001A64r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x         ; decrease string length by one
001A66r 3               
001A66r 3               @check_dot:
001A66r 3                               ; If the last character is a dot, strip it off and set a
001A66r 3                               ; flag. We can use tmptos as a temporary variable
001A66r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB of address
001A68r 3  18                           clc
001A69r 3  75 00                        adc 0,x         ; length of string
001A6Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
001A6Dr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
001A6Fr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only need carry
001A71r 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos+1
001A73r 3               
001A73r 3                               ; tmptos now points to the first character after the string,
001A73r 3                               ; but we need the last character
001A73r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmptos
001A75r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
001A77r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmptos+1
001A79r 3               @2:
001A79r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmptos
001A7Br 3               
001A7Br 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmptos)
001A7Dr 3  C9 2E                        cmp #'.'
001A7Fr 3  D0 04                        bne @main
001A81r 3               
001A81r 3                               ; We have a dot, which means this is a double number. Flag
001A81r 3                               ; the fact and reduce string length by one
001A81r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmpdsp
001A83r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
001A85r 3               
001A85r 3               @main:
001A85r 3                               ; Set up stack for subroutine jump to >NUMBER, which means
001A85r 3                               ; we have to go ( addr u --> ud addr u )
001A85r 3  CA                           dex
001A86r 3  CA                           dex
001A87r 3  CA                           dex
001A88r 3  CA                           dex
001A89r 3               
001A89r 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x         ; LSB of length
001A8Br 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001A8Dr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x         ; MSB, max length 255 chars
001A8Fr 3               
001A8Fr 3  B5 06                        lda 6,x         ; LSB of address
001A91r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001A93r 3  B5 07                        lda 7,x         ; MSB of address
001A95r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001A97r 3               
001A97r 3  74 04                        stz 4,x         ; clear space for ud
001A99r 3  74 05                        stz 5,x
001A9Br 3  74 06                        stz 6,x
001A9Dr 3  74 07                        stz 7,x
001A9Fr 3               
001A9Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_number        ; (ud addr u -- ud addr u )
001AA2r 3               
001AA2r 3                               ; test length of returned string, which should be zero
001AA2r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001AA4r 3  F0 15                        beq @all_converted
001AA6r 3               
001AA6r 3                               ; Something went wrong, we still have characters left over,
001AA6r 3                               ; so we print an error and abort. If the NUMBER was called
001AA6r 3                               ; by INTERPRET, we've already checked for Forth words, so
001AA6r 3                               ; we're in deep trouble one way or another
001AA6r 3  A9 3E                        lda #$3E        ; ASCII for ">"
001AA8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001AABr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
001AAEr 3  A9 3C                        lda #$3C        ; ASCII for "<"
001AB0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001AB3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
001AB6r 3               
001AB6r 3  A9 08                        lda #err_syntax
001AB8r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
001ABBr 3               
001ABBr 3               @all_converted:
001ABBr 3                               ; We can drop the string info
001ABBr 3  E8                           inx
001ABCr 3  E8                           inx
001ABDr 3  E8                           inx
001ABEr 3  E8                           inx
001ABFr 3               
001ABFr 3                               ; We have a double-cell number on the Data Stack that might
001ABFr 3                               ; actually have a minus and might actually be single-cell
001ABFr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpdsp      ; flag for double
001AC1r 3  F0 0D                        beq @single
001AC3r 3               
001AC3r 3                               ; Set status bit 5 to indicate this is a double number
001AC3r 3  A9 20                        lda #%00100000
001AC5r 3  04 rr                        tsb status
001AC7r 3               
001AC7r 3                               ; This is a double cell number. If it had a minus, we'll have
001AC7r 3                               ; to negate it
001AC7r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpdsp+1
001AC9r 3  F0 12                        beq @done       ; no minus, all done
001ACBr 3               
001ACBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dnegate
001ACEr 3               
001ACEr 3  80 0D                        bra @done
001AD0r 3               
001AD0r 3               @single:
001AD0r 3                               ; This is a single number, so we just drop the top cell
001AD0r 3  E8                           inx
001AD1r 3  E8                           inx
001AD2r 3               
001AD2r 3                               ; Clear status bit 5 to indicate this is a single number
001AD2r 3  A9 20                        lda #%00100000
001AD4r 3  14 rr                        trb status
001AD6r 3               
001AD6r 3                               ; If we had a minus, we'll have to negate it
001AD6r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmpdsp+1
001AD8r 3  F0 03                        beq @done       ; no minus, all done
001ADAr 3               
001ADAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_negate
001ADDr 3               @done:
001ADDr 3  60           z_number:       rts
001ADEr 3               
001ADEr 3               
001ADEr 3               
001ADEr 3               ; ## NUMBER_SIGN ( ud -- ud ) "Add character to pictured output string"
001ADEr 3               ; ## "#"  auto  ANS core
001ADEr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/num
001ADEr 3                       ; Add one char to the beginning of the pictured output string.
001ADEr 3                       ;
001ADEr 3                       ; Based on
001ADEr 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/numberio.fth
001ADEr 3                       ; Forth code  BASE @ UD/MOD ROT 9 OVER < IF 7 + THEN [CHAR] 0 + HOLD ;
001ADEr 3                       ; """
001ADEr 3               xt_number_sign:
001ADEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2         ; double number
001AE1r 3               
001AE1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_base
001AE4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch            ; ( ud1 base )
001AE7r 3               
001AE7r 3                               ; The following code is the ancient Forth word UD/MOD, which in
001AE7r 3                               ; various Forths (including Gforth) lives on under the hood,
001AE7r 3                               ; even though it's not an ANS standard word, it doesn't appear
001AE7r 3                               ; in the docs, it's only used here, and there are no tests for
001AE7r 3                               ; it. This is why we got rid of it. We'll be converting this
001AE7r 3                               ; mess to something more sane in the long run.
001AE7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r             ; >r
001AEAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero             ; 0
001AEDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_fetch          ; r@
001AF0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_slash_mod     ; um/mod
001AF3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot              ; rot
001AF6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot              ; rot
001AF9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from           ; r>
001AFCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_slash_mod     ; um/mod
001AFFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot              ; rot
001B02r 3                               ; end of UD/MOD ( rem ud )
001B02r 3               
001B02r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot              ; ( ud rem )
001B05r 3               
001B05r 3                               ; Convert the number that is left over to an ASCII character. We
001B05r 3                               ; use a string lookup for speed. Use either abc_str_lower for
001B05r 3                               ; lower case or abc_str_upper for upper case (prefered)
001B05r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001B07r 3  A8                           tay
001B08r 3  B9 rr rr                     lda s_abc_upper,y
001B0Br 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001B0Dr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x                 ; paranoid; now ( ud char )
001B0Fr 3               
001B0Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_hold
001B12r 3               
001B12r 3               z_number_sign:
001B12r 3  60                           rts
001B13r 3               
001B13r 3               
001B13r 3               ; ## NUMBER_SIGN_GREATER ( d -- addr u ) "Finish pictured number conversion"
001B13r 3               ; ## "#>"  auto  ANS core
001B13r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/num-end
001B13r 3                       ; Finish conversion of pictured number string, putting address and
001B13r 3                       ; length on the Data Stack.
001B13r 3                       ;
001B13r 3                       ; Original Fort is  2DROP HLD @ PAD OVER -
001B13r 3                       ; Based on
001B13r 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/numberio.fth
001B13r 3                       ; """
001B13r 3               xt_number_sign_greater:
001B13r 3               
001B13r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2         ; double number
001B16r 3               
001B16r 3                               ; The start address lives in tohold
001B16r 3  A5 rr                        lda tohold
001B18r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x         ; LSB of tohold
001B1Ar 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001B1Cr 3  A5 rr                        lda tohold+1
001B1Er 3  95 01                        sta 1,x         ; MSB of addr
001B20r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x         ; ( addr addr )
001B22r 3               
001B22r 3                               ; The length of the string is pad - addr
001B22r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_pad      ; ( addr addr pad )
001B25r 3               
001B25r 3  38                           sec
001B26r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB of pad address
001B28r 3  F5 02                        sbc 2,x
001B2Ar 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001B2Cr 3               
001B2Cr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB, which should always be zero
001B2Er 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x
001B30r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x         ; ( addr u pad )
001B32r 3               
001B32r 3  E8                           inx
001B33r 3  E8                           inx
001B34r 3               
001B34r 3               z_number_sign_greater:
001B34r 3  60                           rts
001B35r 3               
001B35r 3               
001B35r 3               ; ## NUMBER_SIGN_S ( d -- addr u ) "Completely convert pictured output"
001B35r 3               ; ## "#s"  auto  ANS core
001B35r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/numS
001B35r 3                       ; Completely convert number for pictured numerical output.
001B35r 3                       ;
001B35r 3                       ; Based on
001B35r 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/system.fth
001B35r 3                       ; Original Forth code  BEGIN # 2DUP OR 0= UNTIL
001B35r 3                       ; """
001B35r 3               
001B35r 3               xt_number_sign_s:
001B35r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001B38r 3               @loop:
001B38r 3                               ; convert a single number ("#")
001B38r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign
001B3Br 3               
001B3Br 3                               ; stop when double-celled number in TOS is zero:
001B3Br 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001B3Dr 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
001B3Fr 3  15 02                        ora 2,x
001B41r 3  15 03                        ora 3,x
001B43r 3  D0 F3                        bne @loop
001B45r 3               
001B45r 3               z_number_sign_s:
001B45r 3  60                           rts
001B46r 3               
001B46r 3               
001B46r 3               
001B46r 3               ; ## OF (C: -- of-sys) (x1 x2 -- |x1) "Conditional flow control"
001B46r 3               ; ## "of"  auto  ANS core ext
001B46r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OF"""
001B46r 3               
001B46r 3               xt_of:
001B46r 3                               ; Check if value is equal to this case.
001B46r 3                               ; Postpone over (eg. compile a jsr to it)
001B46r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_over
001B48r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_over
001B4Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001B4Dr 3               
001B4Dr 3                               ; Postpone = (EQUAL), that is, compile a jsr to it
001B4Dr 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_equal
001B4Fr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_equal
001B51r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001B54r 3               
001B54r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_if
001B57r 3               
001B57r 3                               ; If it's true, consume the original value.
001B57r 3                               ; Postpone DROP (eg. compile a jsr to it)
001B57r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_drop
001B59r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_drop
001B5Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001B5Er 3               
001B5Er 3  60           z_of:           rts
001B5Fr 3               
001B5Fr 3               
001B5Fr 3               
001B5Fr 3               ; ## ONE ( -- n ) "Push the number 1 to the Data Stack"
001B5Fr 3               ; ## "1"  auto  Tali Forth
001B5Fr 3                       ; """This is also the code for EDITOR-WORDLIST"""
001B5Fr 3               xt_editor_wordlist:
001B5Fr 3               xt_one:
001B5Fr 3  CA                           dex
001B60r 3  CA                           dex
001B61r 3  A9 01                        lda #1
001B63r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001B65r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001B67r 3               
001B67r 3               z_editor_wordlist:
001B67r 3               z_one:
001B67r 3  60                           rts
001B68r 3               
001B68r 3               
001B68r 3               ; ## ONE_MINUS ( u -- u-1 ) "Decrease TOS by one"
001B68r 3               ; ## "1-"  auto  ANS core
001B68r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OneMinus"""
001B68r 3               
001B68r 3               xt_one_minus:
001B68r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001B6Br 3               
001B6Br 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001B6Dr 3  D0 02                        bne @1
001B6Fr 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
001B71r 3               @1:
001B71r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
001B73r 3               
001B73r 3  60           z_one_minus:    rts
001B74r 3               
001B74r 3               
001B74r 3               
001B74r 3               ; ## ONE_PLUS ( u -- u+1 ) "Increase TOS by one"
001B74r 3               ; ## "1+"  auto  ANS core
001B74r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OnePlus
001B74r 3                       ;
001B74r 3                       ; Code is shared with CHAR-PLUS
001B74r 3                       ; """
001B74r 3               
001B74r 3               xt_char_plus:
001B74r 3               xt_one_plus:
001B74r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001B77r 3               
001B77r 3  F6 00                        inc 0,x
001B79r 3  D0 02                        bne @done
001B7Br 3  F6 01                        inc 1,x
001B7Dr 3               
001B7Dr 3               @done:
001B7Dr 3               z_char_plus:
001B7Dr 3  60           z_one_plus:     rts
001B7Er 3               
001B7Er 3               
001B7Er 3               
001B7Er 3               ; ## ONLY ( -- ) "Set earch order to minimum wordlist"
001B7Er 3               ; ## "only"  auto  ANS search ext
001B7Er 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/search/ONLY"""
001B7Er 3               
001B7Er 3               xt_only:
001B7Er 3                               ; Put -1 on data stack.
001B7Er 3  CA                           dex
001B7Fr 3  CA                           dex
001B80r 3  A9 FF                        lda #$FF
001B82r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001B84r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001B86r 3               
001B86r 3                               ; Invoke set-order to set the minimum search order.
001B86r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_set_order
001B89r 3               
001B89r 3  60           z_only:         rts
001B8Ar 3               
001B8Ar 3               
001B8Ar 3               
001B8Ar 3               ; ## OR ( m n -- n ) "Logically OR TOS and NOS"
001B8Ar 3               ; ## "or"  auto  ANS core
001B8Ar 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OR"
001B8Ar 3               xt_or:
001B8Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001B8Dr 3               
001B8Dr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001B8Fr 3  15 02                        ora 2,x
001B91r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001B93r 3               
001B93r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
001B95r 3  15 03                        ora 3,x
001B97r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001B99r 3               
001B99r 3  E8                           inx
001B9Ar 3  E8                           inx
001B9Br 3               
001B9Br 3  60           z_or:           rts
001B9Cr 3               
001B9Cr 3               
001B9Cr 3               ; ## ORDER ( -- ) "Print current word order list and current WID"
001B9Cr 3               ; ## "order"  auto  ANS core
001B9Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/search/ORDER
001B9Cr 3                       ; Note the search order is displayed from first search to last
001B9Cr 3                       ; searched and is therefore exactly the reverse of the order in which
001B9Cr 3                       ; Forth stacks are displayed.
001B9Cr 3                       ;
001B9Cr 3                       ; A Forth implementation of this word is:
001B9Cr 3                       ;
001B9Cr 3                       ; 	: .wid ( wid -- )
001B9Cr 3                       ; 	dup 0=  if ." Forth "  drop    else
001B9Cr 3                       ; 	dup 1 = if ." Editor " drop    else
001B9Cr 3                       ; 	dup 2 = if ." Assembler " drop else
001B9Cr 3                       ; 	dup 3 = if ." Root " drop      else
001B9Cr 3                       ; 	           . ( just print the number )
001B9Cr 3                       ; 	then then then then ;
001B9Cr 3                       ;
001B9Cr 3                       ; : ORDER ( -- )
001B9Cr 3                       ; 	cr get-order 0 ?do .wid loop
001B9Cr 3                       ; 	space space get-current .wid ;
001B9Cr 3                       ;
001B9Cr 3                       ; This is an interactive program, so speed
001B9Cr 3                       ; is not as important as size. We assume we do not have more than 255
001B9Cr 3                       ; wordlists.
001B9Cr 3                       ; """
001B9Cr 3               
001B9Cr 3               xt_order:
001B9Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
001B9Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_get_order        ; ( wid_n ... wid_1 n )
001BA2r 3               
001BA2r 3                               ; Paranoid: Check if there are no wordlists, a rather
001BA2r 3                               ; pathological case. this would mean ( 0 ) on the stack. In
001BA2r 3                               ; that case, we just drop n and run
001BA2r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x                 ; assumes no more than 255 wordlists
001BA4r 3  F0 1E                        beq @drop_done
001BA6r 3               
001BA6r 3               @have_wordlists:
001BA6r 3                               ; We arrive here with the LSB of TOS in A, the number of WIDs
001BA6r 3                               ; on the stack
001BA6r 3  A8                           tay
001BA7r 3               @loop:
001BA7r 3  E8                           inx
001BA8r 3  E8                           inx                     ; DROP, now ( wid_n ... wid_1 )
001BA9r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001BABr 3               
001BABr 3  5A                           phy
001BACr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr _print_wid_string   ; internal helper function
001BAFr 3  7A                           ply
001BB0r 3               
001BB0r 3  88                           dey
001BB1r 3  D0 F4                        bne @loop
001BB3r 3               
001BB3r 3                               ; We've printed the wordlists, now we add the current wordlist.
001BB3r 3                               ; This follows the convention of Gforth
001BB3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
001BB6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
001BB9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_get_current      ; ( wid )
001BBCr 3               
001BBCr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001BBEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr _print_wid_string
001BC1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
001BC4r 3               
001BC4r 3               @drop_done:
001BC4r 3  E8                           inx
001BC5r 3  E8                           inx
001BC6r 3               z_order:
001BC6r 3  60                           rts
001BC7r 3               
001BC7r 3               _print_wid_string:
001BC7r 3                       ; """Helper function for ORDER: Given a WID in A, print the
001BC7r 3                       ; corresponding string. If there is no such word list defined, just
001BC7r 3                       ; print the number. Assumes we will not have more than 256 WIDs; also
001BC7r 3                       ; assumes we have just loaded A so Z reflects status of byte.  In
001BC7r 3                       ; theory, we could speed this up by having the WID be the same as the
001BC7r 3                       ; number of the strings. However, ORDER is used rather infrequently and
001BC7r 3                       ; this would make changes to the strings.asm file very dangerous, so we
001BC7r 3                       ; follow the slightly more complicated route with a translation table.
001BC7r 3                       ; """
001BC7r 3                               ; If the WID is larger than 3, we have no string avaliable and
001BC7r 3                               ; just print the number.
001BC7r 3                               ; See http://6502.org/tutorials/compare_instructions.html
001BC7r 3                               ; for details
001BC7r 3  C9 04                        cmp #4
001BC9r 3  90 09                        bcc @output_string      ; less than 4, print a real string
001BCBr 3               
001BCBr 3                               ; Our WID is not less than 4, that is, 4 or larger. We just
001BCBr 3                               ; print the number
001BCBr 3  CA                           dex
001BCCr 3  CA                           dex
001BCDr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001BCFr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001BD1r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp xt_u_dot            ; JSR/RTS as this routine is not compiled
001BD4r 3               
001BD4r 3               @output_string:
001BD4r 3                               ; Get the string number based on WID 0 to 3
001BD4r 3  A8                           tay
001BD5r 3  B9 rr rr                     lda @wid_data,y
001BD8r 3               
001BD8r 3                               ; Print without a line feed
001BD8r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp print_string_no_lf  ; JSR/RTS as this routine is not compiled
001BDBr 3               
001BDBr 3               @wid_data:
001BDBr 3                       ; Table of string numbers (see strings.asm) indexed by the WID if
001BDBr 3                       ; less than 4.
001BDBr 3  03                   .byte str_wid_forth            ; WID 0: "Forth"
001BDCr 3  06                   .byte str_wid_editor           ; WID 1: "Editor"
001BDDr 3  07                   .byte str_wid_assembler        ; WID 2: "Assembler"
001BDEr 3  08                   .byte str_wid_root             ; WID 3: "Root"
001BDFr 3               
001BDFr 3               
001BDFr 3               
001BDFr 3               ; ## OUTPUT ( -- addr ) "Return the address of the EMIT vector address"
001BDFr 3               ; ## "output"  tested  Tali Forth
001BDFr 3               xt_output:
001BDFr 3                       ; """Return the address where the jump target for EMIT is stored (but
001BDFr 3                       ; not the vector itself). By default, this will hold the value of
001BDFr 3                       ; kernel_putc routine, but this can be changed by the user, hence this
001BDFr 3                       ; routine.
001BDFr 3                       ; """
001BDFr 3  CA                           dex
001BE0r 3  CA                           dex
001BE1r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<output
001BE3r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001BE5r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>output
001BE7r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001BE9r 3               
001BE9r 3  60           z_output:       rts
001BEAr 3               
001BEAr 3               
001BEAr 3               ; ## OVER ( b a -- b a b ) "Copy NOS to TOS"
001BEAr 3               ; ## "over"  auto  ANS core
001BEAr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/OVER"""
001BEAr 3               xt_over:
001BEAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001BEDr 3               
001BEDr 3  CA                           dex
001BEEr 3  CA                           dex
001BEFr 3               
001BEFr 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x         ; LSB
001BF1r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001BF3r 3  B5 05                        lda 5,x         ; MSB
001BF5r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001BF7r 3               
001BF7r 3  60           z_over:         rts
001BF8r 3               
001BF8r 3               
001BF8r 3               ; ## PAD ( -- addr ) "Return address of user scratchpad"
001BF8r 3               ; ## "pad"  auto  ANS core ext
001BF8r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PAD
001BF8r 3                       ; Return address to a temporary area in free memory for user. Must
001BF8r 3                       ; be at least 84 bytes in size (says ANS). It is located relative to
001BF8r 3                       ; the compile area pointer (CP) and therefore varies in position.
001BF8r 3                       ; This area is reserved for the user and not used by the system
001BF8r 3                       ; """
001BF8r 3               xt_pad:
001BF8r 3  CA                           dex
001BF9r 3  CA                           dex
001BFAr 3               
001BFAr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
001BFCr 3  18                           clc
001BFDr 3  69 FF                        adc #padoffset  ; assumes padoffset one byte in size
001BFFr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001C01r 3               
001C01r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
001C03r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; only need carry
001C05r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001C07r 3               
001C07r 3  60           z_pad:          rts
001C08r 3               
001C08r 3               
001C08r 3               ; ## PAGE ( -- ) "Clear the screen"
001C08r 3               ; ## "page"  tested  ANS facility
001C08r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/facility/PAGE
001C08r 3                       ; Clears a page if supported by ANS terminal codes. This is
001C08r 3                       ; Clear Screen ("ESC[2J") plus moving the cursor to the top
001C08r 3                       ; left of the screen
001C08r 3                       ; """
001C08r 3               xt_page:
001C08r 3  A9 1B                        lda #AscESC
001C0Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001C0Dr 3  A9 5B                        lda #$5B        ; ASCII for "["
001C0Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001C12r 3  A9 32                        lda #'2'
001C14r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001C17r 3  A9 4A                        lda #'J'
001C19r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
001C1Cr 3               
001C1Cr 3                               ; move cursor to top left of screen
001C1Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
001C1Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
001C22r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_at_xy
001C25r 3               
001C25r 3  60           z_page:         rts
001C26r 3               
001C26r 3               
001C26r 3               ; ## PAREN ( -- ) "Discard input up to close paren ( comment )"
001C26r 3               ; ## "("  auto  ANS core
001C26r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/p"""
001C26r 3               
001C26r 3               xt_paren:
001C26r 3                               ; Put a right paren on the stack.
001C26r 3  CA                           dex
001C27r 3  CA                           dex
001C28r 3  A9 29                        lda #41     ; Right parenthesis
001C2Ar 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001C2Cr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001C2Er 3               
001C2Er 3                               ; Call parse.
001C2Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_parse
001C31r 3               
001C31r 3                               ; Throw away the result.
001C31r 3  E8                           inx
001C32r 3  E8                           inx
001C33r 3  E8                           inx
001C34r 3  E8                           inx
001C35r 3               
001C35r 3  60           z_paren:        rts
001C36r 3               
001C36r 3               
001C36r 3               
001C36r 3               ; ## PARSE_NAME ( "name" -- addr u ) "Parse the input"
001C36r 3               ; ## "parse-name"  auto  ANS core ext
001C36r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PARSE-NAME
001C36r 3                       ; Find next word in input string, skipping leading whitespace. This is
001C36r 3                       ; a special form of PARSE and drops through to that word. See PARSE
001C36r 3                       ; for more detail. We use this word internally for the interpreter
001C36r 3                       ; because it is a lot easier to use. Reference implementations at
001C36r 3                       ; http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PARSE-NAME and
001C36r 3                       ; http://www.forth200x.org/reference-implementations/parse-name.fs
001C36r 3                       ; Roughly, the word is comparable to BL WORD COUNT. -- Note that
001C36r 3                       ; though the ANS standard talks about skipping "spaces", whitespace
001C36r 3                       ; is actually perfectly legal (see for example
001C36r 3                       ; http://forth-standard.org/standard/usage#subsubsection.3.4.1.1).
001C36r 3                       ; Otherwise, PARSE-NAME chokes on tabs.
001C36r 3                       ; """
001C36r 3               
001C36r 3               xt_parse_name:
001C36r 3                               ; To enable the compilation of the high-level Forth words
001C36r 3                               ; in forth-words.asm and user-words.asm at boot time,
001C36r 3                               ; PARSE-NAME and PARSE must be able to deal with 16-bit string
001C36r 3                               ; lengths. This is a pain on an 8-bit machine. The pointer
001C36r 3                               ; to the current location is in toin (>IN). We need to check,
001C36r 3                               ; worst case, the characters from cib+toin to cib+ciblen, and
001C36r 3                               ; we can't just use Y as an index.
001C36r 3               
001C36r 3                               ; The counter is CIBLEN-TOIN and stored in tmp1
001C36r 3  A5 rr                        lda ciblen              ; LSB of counter
001C38r 3  38                           sec
001C39r 3  E5 rr                        sbc toin
001C3Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001C3Dr 3  A5 rr                        lda ciblen+1            ; MSB
001C3Fr 3  E5 rr                        sbc toin+1
001C41r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001C43r 3               
001C43r 3                               ; Check the result for zero (TOIN is equal to CIBLEN)
001C43r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001C45r 3  05 rr                        ora tmp1+1
001C47r 3  F0 28                        beq @empty_line
001C49r 3               
001C49r 3                               ; We walk through the characters starting at CIB+TOIN, so we
001C49r 3                               ; save a temp version of that in tmp2
001C49r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib
001C4Br 3  18                           clc
001C4Cr 3  65 rr                        adc toin
001C4Er 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2                ; LSB of first character
001C50r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib+1
001C52r 3  65 rr                        adc toin+1
001C54r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1              ; MSB
001C56r 3               
001C56r 3               @skip_loop:
001C56r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp2)              ; work copy of cib
001C58r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr is_whitespace
001C5Br 3  90 1F                        bcc @char_found
001C5Dr 3               
001C5Dr 3                               ; Char is still whitespace, continue
001C5Dr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp2
001C5Fr 3  D0 02                        bne @2
001C61r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp2+1
001C63r 3               @2:
001C63r 3                               ; Adjust counter
001C63r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001C65r 3  D0 02                        bne @3
001C67r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1+1
001C69r 3               @3:
001C69r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmp1
001C6Br 3               
001C6Br 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001C6Dr 3  05 rr                        ora tmp1+1
001C6Fr 3  D0 E5                        bne @skip_loop          ; fall through if empty line
001C71r 3               
001C71r 3               @empty_line:
001C71r 3                               ; Neither the ANS Forth nor the Gforth documentation say
001C71r 3                               ; what to return as an address if a string with only
001C71r 3                               ; spaces is given. For speed reasons, we just return junk
001C71r 3                               ; NOS, with the TOS zero as per standard
001C71r 3  CA                           dex
001C72r 3  CA                           dex
001C73r 3  CA                           dex
001C74r 3  CA                           dex
001C75r 3               
001C75r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x                 ; TOS is zero
001C77r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001C79r 3               
001C79r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp z_parse_name        ; skip over PARSE
001C7Cr 3               
001C7Cr 3               @char_found:
001C7Cr 3                               ; We arrive here with tmp2 pointing to the first non-space
001C7Cr 3                               ; character. This is where the word really starts, so
001C7Cr 3                               ; we use it to calculate the new >IN by subtracting
001C7Cr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001C7Er 3  38                           sec
001C7Fr 3  E5 rr                        sbc cib
001C81r 3  85 rr                        sta toin
001C83r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
001C85r 3  E5 rr                        sbc cib+1
001C87r 3  85 rr                        sta toin+1
001C89r 3               
001C89r 3                               ; prepare Data Stack for PARSE by adding space
001C89r 3                               ; as the delimiter
001C89r 3  CA                           dex
001C8Ar 3  CA                           dex
001C8Br 3               
001C8Br 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
001C8Dr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001C8Fr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x                 ; paranoid, now ( "name" c )
001C91r 3               
001C91r 3               
001C91r 3               ; ## PARSE ( "name" c -- addr u ) "Parse input with delimiter character"
001C91r 3               ; ## "parse"  tested  ANS core ext
001C91r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PARSE
001C91r 3                       ; Find word in input string delimited by character given. Do not
001C91r 3                       ; skip leading delimiters -- this is the main difference to PARSE-NAME.
001C91r 3                       ; PARSE and PARSE-NAME replace WORD in modern systems. ANS discussion
001C91r 3                       ; http://www.forth200x.org/documents/html3/rationale.html#rat:core:PARSE
001C91r 3                       ;
001C91r 3                       ;
001C91r 3                       ;     cib  cib+toin   cib+ciblen
001C91r 3                       ;      v      v            v
001C91r 3                       ;     |###################|
001C91r 3                       ;
001C91r 3                       ;     |------>|  toin (>IN)
001C91r 3                       ;     |------------------->|  ciblen
001C91r 3                       ;
001C91r 3                       ; The input string is stored starting at the address in the Current
001C91r 3                       ; Input Buffer (CIB), the length of which is in CIBLEN. While searching
001C91r 3                       ; for the delimiter, TOIN (>IN) points to the where we currently are.
001C91r 3                       ; Since PARSE does not skip leading delimiters, we assume we are on a
001C91r 3                       ; useful string if there are any characters at all. As with
001C91r 3                       ; PARSE-NAME, we must be able to handle strings with a length of
001C91r 3                       ; 16-bit for EVALUTE, which is a pain on an 8-bit machine.
001C91r 3                       ; """
001C91r 3               
001C91r 3               xt_parse:
001C91r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001C94r 3               
001C94r 3                               ; If the input buffer is empty, we just return
001C94r 3  A5 rr                        lda ciblen
001C96r 3  05 rr                        ora ciblen+1
001C98r 3  F0 0C                        beq @abort_parse
001C9Ar 3               
001C9Ar 3                               ; If the pointer >IN is larger or equal to the length of
001C9Ar 3                               ; the input buffer (CIBLEN), the line is done. Put
001C9Ar 3                               ; differently, we only continue if >IN is smaller than
001C9Ar 3                               ; CIBLEN
001C9Ar 3  A5 rr                        lda toin+1              ; MSB
001C9Cr 3  C5 rr                        cmp ciblen+1
001C9Er 3  90 0E                        bcc @go_parse           ; unsigned comparison
001CA0r 3               
001CA0r 3  A5 rr                        lda toin                ; LSB
001CA2r 3  C5 rr                        cmp ciblen
001CA4r 3  90 08                        bcc @go_parse
001CA6r 3               
001CA6r 3               @abort_parse:
001CA6r 3                               ; Sorry, this line is over
001CA6r 3  CA                           dex
001CA7r 3  CA                           dex
001CA8r 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
001CAAr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
001CACr 3               
001CACr 3  80 7A                        bra @done
001CAEr 3               @go_parse:
001CAEr 3                               ; We actually have work to do. Save the delimiter in
001CAEr 3                               ; tmptos.
001CAEr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001CB0r 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
001CB2r 3               
001CB2r 3                               ; We can now prepare the Data Stack for the return value
001CB2r 3  CA                           dex
001CB3r 3  CA                           dex
001CB4r 3               
001CB4r 3                               ; tmp1 is CIB+TOIN, the beginning of the current string
001CB4r 3                               ; tmp2 is initially the same as tmp1, then the work index
001CB4r 3                               ; tmp3 is CIB+CIBLEN, one char past the end of the string
001CB4r 3               
001CB4r 3                               ; Calculate the beginning of the string, which is also the
001CB4r 3                               ; address to return
001CB4r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib
001CB6r 3  18                           clc
001CB7r 3  65 rr                        adc toin        ; LSB
001CB9r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001CBBr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
001CBDr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001CBFr 3               
001CBFr 3  A5 rr                        lda cib+1
001CC1r 3  65 rr                        adc toin+1      ; MSB
001CC3r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001CC5r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
001CC7r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001CC9r 3               
001CC9r 3                               ; Calculate the address where the input buffer ends plus 1, so
001CC9r 3                               ; we can compare it with TOIN, which is an index
001CC9r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib
001CCBr 3  18                           clc
001CCCr 3  65 rr                        adc ciblen
001CCEr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3
001CD0r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib+1
001CD2r 3  65 rr                        adc ciblen+1
001CD4r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp3+1
001CD6r 3               
001CD6r 3                               ; Initialize the offset we use to adjust EOL or found delimiter
001CD6r 3  64 rr                        stz tmptos+1
001CD8r 3               @loop:
001CD8r 3                               ; If we are at the end of the string, quit
001CD8r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001CDAr 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp3
001CDCr 3  D0 06                        bne @not_empty
001CDEr 3               
001CDEr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
001CE0r 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp3+1
001CE2r 3  F0 1D                        beq @eol
001CE4r 3               @not_empty:
001CE4r 3                               ; We have to do this the hard way. In fact, it's really
001CE4r 3                               ; hard since if we are dealing with a SPACE, the standard
001CE4r 3                               ; wants us to skip all whitespace, not just spaces. Otherwise,
001CE4r 3                               ; Tali would choke on tabs between words. For details, see
001CE4r 3                               ; http://forth-standard.org/standard/file#subsection.11.3.5
001CE4r 3                               ; In theory, we could make this faster by defining a delimiter
001CE4r 3                               ; that is 00 as the sign that we skip all whitespace, thereby
001CE4r 3                               ; avoiding having to test every time. However, somebody,
001CE4r 3                               ; somewhere might want to parse a zero-delimited list. Since
001CE4r 3                               ; any byte value could be chosen for that, we just test for
001CE4r 3                               ; a space every single time for the moment.
001CE4r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp2)
001CE6r 3               
001CE6r 3  A4 rr                        ldy tmptos
001CE8r 3  C0 20                        cpy #AscSP
001CEAr 3  D0 07                        bne @not_whitespace
001CECr 3               
001CECr 3                               ; The delimiter is a space, so we're looking for all
001CECr 3                               ; whitespace
001CECr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr is_whitespace
001CEFr 3  90 02                        bcc @not_whitespace
001CF1r 3  80 0C                        bra @found_delimiter
001CF3r 3               
001CF3r 3               @not_whitespace:
001CF3r 3                               ; The delimiter is not a space, so we're looking for
001CF3r 3                               ; whatever it is
001CF3r 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmptos
001CF5r 3  F0 08                        beq @found_delimiter
001CF7r 3               
001CF7r 3                               ; Not a delimiter, next character
001CF7r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp2
001CF9r 3  D0 DD                        bne @loop
001CFBr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp2+1
001CFDr 3  80 D9                        bra @loop
001CFFr 3               
001CFFr 3               @found_delimiter:
001CFFr 3                               ; Increase the offset: If we've found a delimiter, we want
001CFFr 3                               ; TOIN to point to the character after it, not the delimiter
001CFFr 3                               ; itself
001CFFr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmptos+1
001D01r 3               @eol:
001D01r 3                               ; The length of the new string is tmp2-tmp1
001D01r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001D03r 3  38                           sec
001D04r 3  E5 rr                        sbc tmp1
001D06r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001D08r 3               
001D08r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
001D0Ar 3  E5 rr                        sbc tmp1+1
001D0Cr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001D0Er 3               
001D0Er 3                               ; The new offset is tmp2-cib
001D0Er 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
001D10r 3  38                           sec
001D11r 3  E5 rr                        sbc cib
001D13r 3  85 rr                        sta toin
001D15r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
001D17r 3  E5 rr                        sbc cib+1
001D19r 3  85 rr                        sta toin+1
001D1Br 3               
001D1Br 3                               ; Add in the delimiter
001D1Br 3  A5 rr                        lda toin
001D1Dr 3  18                           clc
001D1Er 3  65 rr                        adc tmptos+1
001D20r 3  85 rr                        sta toin
001D22r 3  A5 rr                        lda toin+1
001D24r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; we only need the carry
001D26r 3  85 rr                        sta toin+1
001D28r 3               @done:
001D28r 3               z_parse_name:
001D28r 3  60           z_parse:        rts
001D29r 3               
001D29r 3               
001D29r 3               
001D29r 3               ; ## PICK ( n n u -- n n n ) "Move element u of the stack to TOS"
001D29r 3               ; ## "pick"  auto  ANS core ext
001D29r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PICK
001D29r 3                       ; Take the u-th element out of the stack and put it on TOS,
001D29r 3                       ; overwriting the original TOS. 0 PICK is equivalent to DUP, 1 PICK to
001D29r 3                       ; OVER. Note that using PICK is considered poor coding form. Also note
001D29r 3                       ; that FIG Forth has a different behavior for PICK than ANS Forth.
001D29r 3                       ; """
001D29r 3               
001D29r 3               xt_pick:
001D29r 3                               ; Checking for underflow is difficult because it depends on
001D29r 3                               ; which element we want to grab. We could probably figure
001D29r 3                               ; something out, but it wouldn't work with underflow stripping
001D29r 3                               ; Since using PICK is considered poor form anyway, we just
001D29r 3                               ; leave it as it is
001D29r 3  16 00                        asl 0,x         ; we assume u < 128 (stack is small)
001D2Br 3  8A                           txa
001D2Cr 3  75 00                        adc 0,x
001D2Er 3  A8                           tay
001D2Fr 3               
001D2Fr 3  B9 02 00                     lda 0002,y
001D32r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001D34r 3  B9 03 00                     lda 0003,y
001D37r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001D39r 3               
001D39r 3  60           z_pick:         rts
001D3Ar 3               
001D3Ar 3               
001D3Ar 3               
001D3Ar 3               ; ## PLUS ( n n -- n ) "Add TOS and NOS"
001D3Ar 3               ; ## "+"  auto  ANS core
001D3Ar 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Plus"""
001D3Ar 3               xt_plus:
001D3Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001D3Dr 3               
001D3Dr 3  18                           clc
001D3Er 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB
001D40r 3  75 02                        adc 2,x
001D42r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001D44r 3               
001D44r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB. No CLC, conserve carry bit
001D46r 3  75 03                        adc 3,x
001D48r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001D4Ar 3               
001D4Ar 3  E8                           inx
001D4Br 3  E8                           inx
001D4Cr 3               
001D4Cr 3  60           z_plus:         rts
001D4Dr 3               
001D4Dr 3               
001D4Dr 3               ; ## PLUS_STORE ( n addr -- ) "Add number to value at given address"
001D4Dr 3               ; ## "+!"  auto  ANS core
001D4Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/PlusStore"""
001D4Dr 3               xt_plus_store:
001D4Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
001D50r 3               
001D50r 3                               ; move address to tmp1 so we can work with it
001D50r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001D52r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001D54r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
001D56r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001D58r 3               
001D58r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; LSB
001D5Ar 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
001D5Cr 3  18                           clc
001D5Dr 3  75 02                        adc 2,x
001D5Fr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001D61r 3               
001D61r 3  C8                           iny             ; MSB
001D62r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
001D64r 3  75 03                        adc 3,x
001D66r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
001D68r 3               
001D68r 3  E8                           inx
001D69r 3  E8                           inx
001D6Ar 3  E8                           inx
001D6Br 3  E8                           inx
001D6Cr 3               
001D6Cr 3  60           z_plus_store:   rts
001D6Dr 3               
001D6Dr 3               
001D6Dr 3               ; ## POSTPONE ( -- ) "Change IMMEDIATE status (it's complicated)"
001D6Dr 3               ; ## "postpone"  auto   ANS core
001D6Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/POSTPONE
001D6Dr 3                       ; Add the compilation behavior of a word to a new word at
001D6Dr 3                       ; compile time. If the word that follows it is immediate, include
001D6Dr 3                       ; it so that it will be compiled when the word being defined is
001D6Dr 3                       ; itself used for a new word. Tricky, but very useful.
001D6Dr 3                       ;
001D6Dr 3                       ; Because POSTPONE expects a word (not an xt) in the input stream (not
001D6Dr 3                       ; on the Data Stack). This means we cannot build words with
001D6Dr 3                       ; "jsr xt_postpone, jsr <word>" directly.
001D6Dr 3                       ; """
001D6Dr 3               
001D6Dr 3               xt_postpone:
001D6Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_parse_name               ; ( -- addr n )
001D70r 3               
001D70r 3                               ; if there was no word provided, complain and quit
001D70r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001D72r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
001D74r 3  D0 05                        bne @1
001D76r 3               
001D76r 3  A9 05                        lda #err_noname
001D78r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
001D7Br 3               @1:
001D7Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_find_name                ; ( -- nt | 0 )
001D7Er 3               
001D7Er 3                               ; if word not in Dictionary, complain and quit
001D7Er 3  D0 05                        bne @2
001D80r 3  A9 05                        lda #err_noname
001D82r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
001D85r 3               
001D85r 3               @2:
001D85r 3                               ; keep a copy of nt for later
001D85r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001D87r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001D89r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
001D8Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001D8Dr 3               
001D8Dr 3                               ; We need the xt instead of the nt
001D8Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_name_to_int              ; ( nt -- xt )
001D90r 3               
001D90r 3                               ; See if this is an immediate word. This is easier
001D90r 3                               ; with nt than with xt. The status byte of the word
001D90r 3                               ; is nt+1
001D90r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1
001D92r 3  D0 02                        bne @3
001D94r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
001D96r 3               @3:
001D96r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
001D98r 3  29 04                        and #IM         ; mask all but Intermediate flag
001D9Ar 3  F0 05                        beq @not_immediate
001D9Cr 3               
001D9Cr 3                               ; We're immediate, so instead of executing it right now, we
001D9Cr 3                               ; compile it. xt is TOS, so this is easy. The RTS at the end
001D9Cr 3                               ; takes us back to the original caller
001D9Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_compile_comma
001D9Fr 3  80 0A                        bra @done
001DA1r 3               
001DA1r 3               @not_immediate:
001DA1r 3                               ; This is not an immediate word, so we enact "deferred
001DA1r 3                               ; compilation" by including ' <NAME> COMPILE, which we do by
001DA1r 3                               ; compiling the run-time routine of LITERAL, the xt itself, and
001DA1r 3                               ; a subroutine jump to COMPILE,
001DA1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_literal
001DA4r 3               
001DA4r 3                               ; Last, compile COMPILE,
001DA4r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>xt_compile_comma
001DA6r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<xt_compile_comma
001DA8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
001DABr 3               @done:
001DABr 3  60           z_postpone:     rts
001DACr 3               
001DACr 3               
001DACr 3               
001DACr 3               ; ## PREVIOUS ( -- ) "Remove the first wordlist in the search order"
001DACr 3               ; ## "previous"  auto  ANS search ext
001DACr 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/search/PREVIOUS"""
001DACr 3               
001DACr 3               xt_previous:
001DACr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_get_order
001DAFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_nip
001DB2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one_minus
001DB5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_set_order
001DB8r 3               
001DB8r 3  60           z_previous:     rts
001DB9r 3               
001DB9r 3               
001DB9r 3               
001DB9r 3               ; ## QUESTION ( addr -- ) "Print content of a variable"
001DB9r 3               ; ## "?"  tested  ANS tools
001DB9r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/tools/q
001DB9r 3                       ;
001DB9r 3                       ; Only used interactively. Since humans are so slow, we
001DB9r 3                       ; save size and just go for the subroutine jumps
001DB9r 3                       ; """
001DB9r 3               xt_question:
001DB9r 3                               ; FETCH takes care of underflow check
001DB9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch
001DBCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dot
001DBFr 3               
001DBFr 3  60           z_question:     rts
001DC0r 3               
001DC0r 3               
001DC0r 3               ; ## QUESTION_DUP ( n -- 0 | n n ) "Duplicate TOS non-zero"
001DC0r 3               ; ## "?dup"  auto  ANS core
001DC0r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/qDUP"""
001DC0r 3               
001DC0r 3               xt_question_dup:
001DC0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
001DC3r 3               
001DC3r 3                               ; Check if TOS is zero
001DC3r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001DC5r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
001DC7r 3  F0 0A                        beq @done
001DC9r 3               
001DC9r 3                               ; not zero, duplicate
001DC9r 3  CA                           dex
001DCAr 3  CA                           dex
001DCBr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
001DCDr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001DCFr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
001DD1r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001DD3r 3               @done:
001DD3r 3  60           z_question_dup: rts
001DD4r 3               
001DD4r 3               
001DD4r 3               
001DD4r 3               ; ## R_FETCH ( -- n ) "Get copy of top of Return Stack"
001DD4r 3               ; ## "r@"  auto  ANS core
001DD4r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/RFetch
001DD4r 3                       ; This word is Compile Only in Tali Forth, though Gforth has it
001DD4r 3                       ; work normally as well
001DD4r 3                       ;
001DD4r 3                       ; An alternative way to write this word
001DD4r 3                       ; would be to access the elements on the stack directly like 2R@
001DD4r 3                       ; does, these versions should be compared at some point.
001DD4r 3                       ; """
001DD4r 3               xt_r_fetch:
001DD4r 3                               ; get the return address
001DD4r 3  7A                           ply             ; LSB
001DD5r 3  84 rr                        sty tmp1
001DD7r 3  7A                           ply             ; MSB
001DD8r 3               
001DD8r 3                               ; --- CUT FOR NATIVE COMPILE ---
001DD8r 3               
001DD8r 3                               ; get the actual top of Return Stack
001DD8r 3  CA                           dex
001DD9r 3  CA                           dex
001DDAr 3               
001DDAr 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
001DDBr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001DDDr 3  68                           pla             ; MSB
001DDEr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001DE0r 3               
001DE0r 3                               ; now we have to put that value back
001DE0r 3  48                           pha
001DE1r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001DE3r 3  48                           pha
001DE4r 3               
001DE4r 3                               ; --- CUT FOR NATIVE COMPILE ---
001DE4r 3               
001DE4r 3                               ; restore return value
001DE4r 3  5A                           phy             ; MSB
001DE5r 3  A4 rr                        ldy tmp1
001DE7r 3  5A                           phy             ; LSB
001DE8r 3               
001DE8r 3  60           z_r_fetch:      rts
001DE9r 3               
001DE9r 3               
001DE9r 3               ; ## R_FROM ( -- n )(R: n --) "Move top of Return Stack to TOS"
001DE9r 3               ; ## "r>"  auto  ANS core
001DE9r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Rfrom
001DE9r 3                       ; Move Top of Return Stack to Top of Data Stack.
001DE9r 3                       ;
001DE9r 3                       ; We have to move
001DE9r 3                       ; the RTS address out of the way first. This word is handled
001DE9r 3                       ; differently for native and and subroutine compilation, see COMPILE,
001DE9r 3                       ; This is a compile-only word
001DE9r 3                       ; """
001DE9r 3               
001DE9r 3               xt_r_from:
001DE9r 3                               ; Rescue the address of the return jump that is currently
001DE9r 3                               ; on top of the Return Stack. If this word is natively
001DE9r 3                               ; compiled, this is a total waste of time
001DE9r 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
001DEAr 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
001DECr 3  7A                           ply             ; MSB
001DEDr 3               
001DEDr 3                               ; --- CUT FOR NATIVE CODING ---
001DEDr 3               
001DEDr 3  CA                           dex
001DEEr 3  CA                           dex
001DEFr 3               
001DEFr 3                               ; now we can access the actual data
001DEFr 3               
001DEFr 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
001DF0r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001DF2r 3  68                           pla             ; MSB
001DF3r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
001DF5r 3               
001DF5r 3                               ; --- CUT FOR NATIVE CODING ---
001DF5r 3               
001DF5r 3                               ; restore the return address
001DF5r 3  5A                           phy             ; MSB
001DF6r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmptos
001DF8r 3  48                           pha             ; LSB
001DF9r 3               
001DF9r 3  60           z_r_from:       rts
001DFAr 3               
001DFAr 3               
001DFAr 3               ; ## R_TO_INPUT ( -- ) ( R: n n n n -- ) "Restore input state from Return Stack"
001DFAr 3               ; ## "r>input"  tested  Tali Forth
001DFAr 3                       ; """Restore the current input state as defined by insrc, cib, ciblen,
001DFAr 3                       ; and toin from the Return Stack.
001DFAr 3                       ;
001DFAr 3                       ; See INPUT_TO_R for a discussion of this word. Uses tmp1
001DFAr 3                       ; """
001DFAr 3               
001DFAr 3               xt_r_to_input:
001DFAr 3               
001DFAr 3                               ; We arrive here with the return address on the top of the
001DFAr 3                               ; 65c02's stack. We need to move it out of the way first
001DFAr 3  68                           pla
001DFBr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001DFDr 3  68                           pla
001DFEr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001E00r 3               
001E00r 3                               ; This assumes that insrc is the first of eight bytes and
001E00r 3                               ; toin+1 the last in the sequence we want to save from the Zero
001E00r 3                               ; Page. Since we went in reverse order, insrc is now on the top
001E00r 3                               ; of the Return Stack.
001E00r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
001E02r 3               @loop:
001E02r 3  68                           pla
001E03r 3  99 rr rr                     sta insrc,y
001E06r 3  C8                           iny
001E07r 3  C0 08                        cpy #8
001E09r 3  D0 F7                        bne @loop
001E0Br 3               
001E0Br 3                               ; Restore address for return jump
001E0Br 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
001E0Dr 3  48                           pha
001E0Er 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
001E10r 3  48                           pha
001E11r 3               
001E11r 3  60           z_r_to_input: 	rts
001E12r 3               
001E12r 3               
001E12r 3               
001E12r 3               ; ## RECURSE ( -- ) "Copy recursive call to word being defined"
001E12r 3               ; ## "recurse"  auto  ANS core
001E12r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/RECURSE
001E12r 3                       ;
001E12r 3                       ; This word may not be natively compiled
001E12r 3                       ; """
001E12r 3               
001E12r 3               xt_recurse:
001E12r 3                               ; The whole routine amounts to compiling a reference to
001E12r 3                               ; the word that is being compiled. First, we save the JSR
001E12r 3                               ; instruction
001E12r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0
001E14r 3               
001E14r 3  A9 20                        lda #$20        ; opcode for JSR
001E16r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E18r 3  C8                           iny
001E19r 3               
001E19r 3                               ; Next, we save the LSB and MSB of the xt of the word
001E19r 3                               ; we are currently working on. We first need to see if
001E19r 3                               ; WORKWORD has the nt (: started the word) or the
001E19r 3                               ; xt (:NONAME started the word). Bit 6 in status tells us.
001E19r 3  24 rr                        bit status
001E1Br 3  70 0C                        bvs @nt_in_workword
001E1Dr 3               
001E1Dr 3                               ; This is a special :NONAME word. Just copy the xt
001E1Dr 3                               ; from WORKWORD into the dictionary.
001E1Dr 3  A5 rr                        lda workword
001E1Fr 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E21r 3  C8                           iny
001E22r 3  A5 rr                        lda workword+1
001E24r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E26r 3  C8                           iny
001E27r 3  80 1B                        bra @update_cp
001E29r 3               
001E29r 3               @nt_in_workword:
001E29r 3                               ; This is a regular : word, so the xt is four bytes down
001E29r 3                               ; from the nt which we saved in WORKWORD. We could probably
001E29r 3                               ; use NAME>INT here but this is going to be faster, and
001E29r 3                               ; fast counts with recursion
001E29r 3  A5 rr                        lda workword            ; LSB
001E2Br 3  18                           clc
001E2Cr 3  69 04                        adc #4
001E2Er 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
001E30r 3  A5 rr                        lda workword+1          ; MSB
001E32r 3  69 00                        adc #0
001E34r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
001E36r 3               
001E36r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
001E38r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E3Ar 3  5A                           phy
001E3Br 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
001E3Dr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
001E3Fr 3  7A                           ply
001E40r 3  C8                           iny
001E41r 3  91 rr                        sta (cp),y
001E43r 3  C8                           iny
001E44r 3               
001E44r 3               @update_cp:
001E44r 3  98                           tya
001E45r 3  18                           clc
001E46r 3  65 rr                        adc cp
001E48r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
001E4Ar 3  90 02                        bcc @done
001E4Cr 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
001E4Er 3               @done:
001E4Er 3  60           z_recurse:      rts
001E4Fr 3               
001E4Fr 3               
001E4Fr 3               
001E4Fr 3               ; ## REFILL ( -- f ) "Refill the input buffer"
001E4Fr 3               ; ## "refill"  tested  ANS core ext
001E4Fr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/REFILL
001E4Fr 3                       ; Attempt to fill the input buffer from the input source, returning
001E4Fr 3                       ; a true flag if successful. When the input source is the user input
001E4Fr 3                       ; device, attempt to receive input into the terminal input buffer. If
001E4Fr 3                       ; successful, make the result the input buffer, set >IN to zero, and
001E4Fr 3                       ; return true. Receipt of a line containing no characters is considered
001E4Fr 3                       ; successful. If there is no input available from the current input
001E4Fr 3                       ; source, return false. When the input source is a string from EVALUATE,
001E4Fr 3                       ; return false and perform no other action." See
001E4Fr 3                       ; https://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/The-Input-Stream.html
001E4Fr 3                       ; and Conklin & Rather p. 156. Note we don't have to care about blocks
001E4Fr 3                       ; because REFILL is never used on blocks - Tali is able to evaluate the
001E4Fr 3                       ; entire block as a 1024 byte string.
001E4Fr 3                       ; """"
001E4Fr 3               
001E4Fr 3               xt_refill:
001E4Fr 3                               ; Get input source from SOURCE-ID. This is an
001E4Fr 3                               ; optimized version of a subroutine jump to SOURCE-ID
001E4Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda insrc               ; cheat: We only check LSB
001E51r 3  D0 2D                        bne @src_not_kbd
001E53r 3               
001E53r 3                               ; SOURCE-ID of zero means we're getting stuff from the keyboard
001E53r 3                               ; with ACCEPT, which wants the address of the current input
001E53r 3                               ; buffer NOS and the max number of characters to accept TOS
001E53r 3  CA                           dex
001E54r 3  CA                           dex
001E55r 3  CA                           dex
001E56r 3  CA                           dex
001E57r 3               
001E57r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib                 ; address of CIB is NOS
001E59r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
001E5Br 3  A5 rr                        lda cib+1
001E5Dr 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
001E5Fr 3               
001E5Fr 3  64 rr                        stz ciblen              ; go in with empty buffer
001E61r 3  64 rr                        stz ciblen+1
001E63r 3               
001E63r 3  A9 FF                        lda #bsize              ; max number of chars is TOS
001E65r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
001E67r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x                 ; cheat: We only accept max 255
001E69r 3               
001E69r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_accept           ; ( addr n1 -- n2)
001E6Cr 3               
001E6Cr 3                               ; ACCEPT returns the number of characters accepted, which
001E6Cr 3                               ; belong in CIBLEN
001E6Cr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
001E6Er 3  85 rr                        sta ciblen
001E70r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
