0023A2r 3  AA                           tax
0023A3r 3               
0023A3r 3                               ; Move addr down from TOS-4 to TOS-2
0023A3r 3  B5 08                        lda 8,x
0023A5r 3  95 04                        sta 4,x
0023A7r 3  B5 09                        lda 9,x
0023A9r 3  95 05                        sta 5,x
0023ABr 3               
0023ABr 3                               ; Copy u from TOS-3 to TOS
0023ABr 3  B5 06                        lda 6,x
0023ADr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0023AFr 3  B5 07                        lda 7,x
0023B1r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0023B3r 3               
0023B3r 3                               ; Put HERE into TOS-1 and TOS-4
0023B3r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
0023B5r 3  95 08                        sta 8,x
0023B7r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
0023B9r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
0023BBr 3  95 09                        sta 9,x
0023BDr 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
0023BFr 3               
0023BFr 3                               ; Copy the string into the dictionary.
0023BFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_move
0023C2r 3               
0023C2r 3                               ; Update cp.
0023C2r 3  18                           clc
0023C3r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
0023C5r 3  75 00                        adc 0,x
0023C7r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
0023C9r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
0023CBr 3  75 01                        adc 1,x
0023CDr 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
0023CFr 3               
0023CFr 3                               ; Update the address of the jump-over jmp instruction.
0023CFr 3                               ; First determine location of jmp instructions address.
0023CFr 3                               ; It should be 2 bytes before the start of the string.
0023CFr 3               
0023CFr 3                               ; Compute it into tmp1, which is no longer being used.
0023CFr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
0023D1r 3  38                           sec
0023D2r 3  E9 02                        sbc #2
0023D4r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
0023D6r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
0023D8r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0          ; Propagate borrow
0023DAr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
0023DCr 3               
0023DCr 3                               ; Update the address of the jump to HERE.
0023DCr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
0023DEr 3  92 rr                        sta (tmp1)
0023E0r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
0023E2r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
0023E4r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
0023E6r 3               
0023E6r 3                               ; Stack is now ( addr2 u ) where addr2 is the new
0023E6r 3                               ; location in the dictionary.
0023E6r 3               
0023E6r 3               sliteral_const_str:
0023E6r 3                               ; Compile a subroutine jump to the runtime of SLITERAL that
0023E6r 3                               ; pushes the new ( addr u ) pair to the Data Stack.
0023E6r 3                               ; When we're done, the code will look like this:
0023E6r 3               
0023E6r 3                               ; xt -->    jmp a
0023E6r 3                               ;           <string data bytes>
0023E6r 3                               ;  a -->    jsr sliteral_runtime
0023E6r 3                               ;           <string address>
0023E6r 3                               ;           <string length>
0023E6r 3                               ; rts -->
0023E6r 3               
0023E6r 3                               ; This means we'll have to adjust the return address for two
0023E6r 3                               ; cells, not just one
0023E6r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>sliteral_runtime
0023E8r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<sliteral_runtime
0023EAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
0023EDr 3               
0023EDr 3                               ; We want to have the address end up as NOS and the length
0023EDr 3                               ; as TOS, so we store the address first
0023EDr 3  B4 03                        ldy 3,x                ; address MSB
0023EFr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x                ; address LSB
0023F1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
0023F4r 3               
0023F4r 3  B4 01                        ldy 1,x                ; length MSB
0023F6r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x                ; length LSB
0023F8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
0023FBr 3               
0023FBr 3                               ; clean up and leave
0023FBr 3  E8                           inx
0023FCr 3  E8                           inx
0023FDr 3  E8                           inx
0023FEr 3  E8                           inx
0023FFr 3               
0023FFr 3  60           z_sliteral:     rts
002400r 3               
002400r 3               
002400r 3               sliteral_runtime:
002400r 3               
002400r 3                       ; """Run time behaviour of SLITERAL: Push ( addr u ) of string to
002400r 3                       ; the Data Stack. We arrive here with the return address as the
002400r 3                       ; top of Return Stack, which points to the address of the string
002400r 3                       ; """
002400r 3  CA                           dex
002401r 3  CA                           dex
002402r 3  CA                           dex
002403r 3  CA                           dex
002404r 3               
002404r 3                               ; Get the address of the string address off the stack and
002404r 3                               ; increase by one because of the RTS mechanics
002404r 3  68                           pla
002405r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1        ; LSB of address
002407r 3  68                           pla
002408r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1      ; MSB of address
00240Ar 3               
00240Ar 3                               ; Walk through both and save them
00240Ar 3  A0 01                        ldy #1          ; adjust for JSR/RTS mechanics on 65c02
00240Cr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
00240Er 3  95 02                        sta 2,x         ; LSB of address
002410r 3  C8                           iny
002411r 3               
002411r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
002413r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x         ; MSB of address
002415r 3  C8                           iny
002416r 3               
002416r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
002418r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x         ; LSB of length
00241Ar 3  C8                           iny
00241Br 3               
00241Br 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
00241Dr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x         ; MSB of length
00241Fr 3               
00241Fr 3                               ; restore return address
00241Fr 3  18                           clc
002420r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
002422r 3  69 04                        adc #4
002424r 3  A8                           tay             ; LSB
002425r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
002427r 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; we only need carry
002429r 3  48                           pha             ; MSB
00242Ar 3  5A                           phy
00242Br 3               
00242Br 3  60                           rts
00242Cr 3               
00242Cr 3               
00242Cr 3               
00242Cr 3               ; ## SM_SLASH_REM ( d n1 -- n2 n3 ) "Symmetic signed division"
00242Cr 3               ; ## "sm/rem"  auto  ANS core
00242Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/SMDivREM
00242Cr 3                       ; Symmetic signed division. Compare FM/MOD. Based on F-PC 3.6
00242Cr 3                       ; by Ulrich Hoffmann. See http://www.xlerb.de/uho/ansi.seq
00242Cr 3                       ;
00242Cr 3                       ; Forth:
00242Cr 3                       ; OVER >R 2DUP XOR 0< >R ABS >R DABS R> UM/MOD R> ?NEGATE SWAP
00242Cr 3                       ; R> ?NEGATE SWAP
00242Cr 3                       ; """
00242Cr 3               
00242Cr 3               xt_sm_slash_rem:
00242Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3 ; contains double number
00242Fr 3               
00242Fr 3                               ; push MSB of high cell of d to Data Stack so we can check
00242Fr 3                               ; its sign later
00242Fr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
002431r 3  48                           pha
002432r 3               
002432r 3                               ; XOR the MSB of the high cell of d and n1 so we figure out
002432r 3                               ; its sign later as well
002432r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002434r 3  55 03                        eor 3,x
002436r 3  48                           pha
002437r 3               
002437r 3                               ; Prepare division by getting absolute of n1 and d
002437r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_abs
00243Ar 3  E8                           inx             ; pretend we pushed n1 to R
00243Br 3  E8                           inx
00243Cr 3               
00243Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dabs
00243Fr 3  CA                           dex
002440r 3  CA                           dex
002441r 3               
002441r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_slash_mod     ; UM/MOD
002444r 3               
002444r 3                               ; if the XOR compiled above is negative, negate the
002444r 3                               ; quotient (n3)
002444r 3  68                           pla
002445r 3  10 03                        bpl @1
002447r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_negate
00244Ar 3               @1:
00244Ar 3                               ; if d was negative, negate the remainder (n2)
00244Ar 3  68                           pla
00244Br 3  10 07                        bpl @done
00244Dr 3               
00244Dr 3  E8                           inx             ; pretend we pushed quotient to R
00244Er 3  E8                           inx
00244Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_negate
002452r 3  CA                           dex
002453r 3  CA                           dex
002454r 3               
002454r 3               @done:
002454r 3  60           z_sm_slash_rem: rts
002455r 3               
002455r 3               
002455r 3               
002455r 3               ; ## SOURCE ( -- addr u ) "Return location and size of input buffer""
002455r 3               ; ## "source"  auto  ANS core
002455r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/SOURCE"""
002455r 3               xt_source:
002455r 3                               ; add address
002455r 3  CA                           dex
002456r 3  CA                           dex
002457r 3  A5 rr                        lda cib
002459r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00245Br 3  A5 rr                        lda cib+1
00245Dr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00245Fr 3               
00245Fr 3                               ; add size
00245Fr 3  CA                           dex
002460r 3  CA                           dex
002461r 3  A5 rr                        lda ciblen
002463r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002465r 3  A5 rr                        lda ciblen+1
002467r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002469r 3               
002469r 3  60           z_source:       rts
00246Ar 3               
00246Ar 3               
00246Ar 3               ; ## SOURCE_ID ( -- n ) "Return source identifier"
00246Ar 3               ; ## "source-id"  tested  ANS core ext
00246Ar 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/SOURCE-ID Identify the
00246Ar 3                       ; input source unless it is a block (s. Conklin & Rather p. 156). This
00246Ar 3                       ; will give the input source: 0 is keyboard, -1 ($FFFF) is character
00246Ar 3                       ; string, and a text file gives the fileid.
00246Ar 3                       ; """
00246Ar 3               xt_source_id:
00246Ar 3  CA                           dex
00246Br 3  CA                           dex
00246Cr 3               
00246Cr 3  A5 rr                        lda insrc
00246Er 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002470r 3  A5 rr                        lda insrc+1
002472r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002474r 3               
002474r 3  60           z_source_id:    rts
002475r 3               
002475r 3               
002475r 3               ; ## SPACE ( -- ) "Print a single space"
002475r 3               ; ## "space"  auto  ANS core
002475r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/SPACE"""
002475r 3               xt_space:
002475r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
002477r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
00247Ar 3               
00247Ar 3  60           z_space:        rts
00247Br 3               
00247Br 3               
00247Br 3               ; ## SPACES ( u -- ) "Print a number of spaces"
00247Br 3               ; ## "spaces"  auto  ANS core
00247Br 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/SPACES"""
00247Br 3               
00247Br 3               xt_spaces:
00247Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
00247Er 3               
00247Er 3                               ; catch any zero in TOS fast
00247Er 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002480r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002482r 3  F0 2A                        beq @done
002484r 3               
002484r 3                               ; Usually we're only going to print far less than 256 spaces,
002484r 3                               ; so we create a quick loop for that. Short loop could be realized
002484r 3                               ; as a separate subroutine, but unless we're really pressed for
002484r 3                               ; memory at some point, this is faster
002484r 3  B4 01                        ldy 1,x
002486r 3  D0 0C                        bne @lots_of_spaces
002488r 3               
002488r 3  B4 00                        ldy 0,x
00248Ar 3               @quick_loop:
00248Ar 3                               ; we reach here knowing that there must be a number that is not
00248Ar 3                               ; zero in the TOS
00248Ar 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
00248Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
00248Fr 3  88                           dey
002490r 3  F0 1C                        beq @done
002492r 3  80 F6                        bra @quick_loop
002494r 3               
002494r 3               @lots_of_spaces:
002494r 3                               ; We go through the first loop once to get rid of the lower
002494r 3                               ; counter byte. This could be zero
002494r 3  B4 00                        ldy 0,x
002496r 3               
002496r 3               @first_slow_loop:
002496r 3  F0 08                        beq @slow_outer_loop
002498r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
00249Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
00249Dr 3  88                           dey
00249Er 3  80 F6                        bra @first_slow_loop
0024A0r 3               
0024A0r 3               @slow_outer_loop:
0024A0r 3                               ; we arrive here knowing that the MSB of TOS cannot be a zero
0024A0r 3  A0 00                        ldy #00
0024A2r 3               
0024A2r 3               @slow_inner_loop:
0024A2r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
0024A4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
0024A7r 3  88                           dey
0024A8r 3  D0 F8                        bne @slow_inner_loop
0024AAr 3               
0024AAr 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
0024ACr 3  D0 F2                        bne @slow_outer_loop
0024AEr 3               
0024AEr 3               @done:
0024AEr 3  E8                           inx             ; drop
0024AFr 3  E8                           inx
0024B0r 3               
0024B0r 3  60           z_spaces:       rts
0024B1r 3               
0024B1r 3               
0024B1r 3               
0024B1r 3               ; ## STAR ( n n -- n ) "16*16 --> 16 "
0024B1r 3               ; ## "*"  auto  ANS core
0024B1r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Times
0024B1r 3                       ; Multiply two signed 16 bit numbers, returning a 16 bit result.
0024B1r 3                       ;
0024B1r 3                       ; This is nothing  more than UM* DROP
0024B1r 3                       ; """
0024B1r 3               
0024B1r 3               xt_star:
0024B1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0024B4r 3               
0024B4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_star
0024B7r 3  E8                           inx
0024B8r 3  E8                           inx
0024B9r 3               
0024B9r 3  60           z_star:         rts
0024BAr 3               
0024BAr 3               
0024BAr 3               
0024BAr 3               ; ## STAR_SLASH  ( n1 n2 n3 -- n4 ) "n1 * n2 / n3 -->  n"
0024BAr 3               ; ## "*/"  auto  ANS core
0024BAr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TimesDiv
0024BAr 3                       ; Multiply n1 by n2 and divide by n3, returning the result
0024BAr 3                       ; without a remainder. This is */MOD without the mod.
0024BAr 3                       ;
0024BAr 3                       ; This word
0024BAr 3                       ; can be defined in Forth as : */  */MOD SWAP DROP ; which is
0024BAr 3                       ; pretty much what we do here
0024BAr 3                       ; """
0024BAr 3               xt_star_slash:
0024BAr 3                               ; We let */MOD check for underflow
0024BAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_star_slash_mod
0024BDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
0024C0r 3  E8                           inx
0024C1r 3  E8                           inx
0024C2r 3               z_star_slash:
0024C2r 3  60                           rts
0024C3r 3               
0024C3r 3               
0024C3r 3               ; ## STAR_SLASH_MOD  ( n1 n2 n3 -- n4 n5 ) "n1 * n2 / n3 --> n-mod n"
0024C3r 3               ; ## "*/mod"  auto  ANS core
0024C3r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TimesDivMOD
0024C3r 3                       ; Multiply n1 by n2 producing the intermediate double-cell result d.
0024C3r 3                       ; Divide d by n3 producing the single-cell remainder n4 and the
0024C3r 3                       ; single-cell quotient n5.
0024C3r 3                       ;
0024C3r 3                       ; In Forth, this is
0024C3r 3                       ; : */MOD  >R M* >R SM/REM ;  Note that */ accesses this routine.
0024C3r 3                       ; """
0024C3r 3               xt_star_slash_mod:
0024C3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
0024C6r 3               
0024C6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r
0024C9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_m_star
0024CCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from
0024CFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_sm_slash_rem
0024D2r 3               
0024D2r 3               z_star_slash_mod:
0024D2r 3  60                           rts
0024D3r 3               
0024D3r 3               
0024D3r 3               ; ## STATE ( -- addr ) "Return the address of compilation state flag"
0024D3r 3               ; ## "state"  auto  ANS core
0024D3r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/STATE
0024D3r 3                       ; STATE is true when in compilation state, false otherwise. Note
0024D3r 3                       ; we do not return the state itself, but only the address where
0024D3r 3                       ; it lives. The state should not be changed directly by the user; see
0024D3r 3                       ; http://forth.sourceforge.net/standard/dpans/dpans6.htm#6.1.2250
0024D3r 3                       ; """
0024D3r 3               xt_state:
0024D3r 3  CA                           dex
0024D4r 3  CA                           dex
0024D5r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<state
0024D7r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0024D9r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>state
0024DBr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0024DDr 3               
0024DDr 3  60           z_state:        rts
0024DEr 3               
0024DEr 3               
0024DEr 3               ; ## STORE ( n addr -- ) "Store TOS in memory"
0024DEr 3               ; ## "!"  auto  ANS core
0024DEr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Store"""
0024DEr 3               xt_store:
0024DEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0024E1r 3               
0024E1r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB
0024E3r 3  81 00                        sta (0,x)
0024E5r 3               
0024E5r 3  F6 00                        inc 0,x
0024E7r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
0024E9r 3  F6 01                        inc 1,x
0024EBr 3               @1:
0024EBr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB
0024EDr 3  81 00                        sta (0,x)
0024EFr 3               
0024EFr 3  E8                           inx             ; 2DROP
0024F0r 3  E8                           inx
0024F1r 3  E8                           inx
0024F2r 3  E8                           inx
0024F3r 3               
0024F3r 3  60           z_store:        rts
0024F4r 3               
0024F4r 3               
0024F4r 3               ; ## STRIP_UNDERFLOW ( -- addr ) "Return address where underflow status is kept"
0024F4r 3               ; ## "strip-underflow"  tested  Tali Forth
0024F4r 3                       ; """`STRIP-UNDERFLOW` is a flag variable that determines if underflow
0024F4r 3                       ; checking should be removed during the compilation of new words.
0024F4r 3                       ; Default is false.
0024F4r 3                       ; """
0024F4r 3               xt_strip_underflow:
0024F4r 3  CA                           dex
0024F5r 3  CA                           dex
0024F6r 3               
0024F6r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<uf_strip
0024F8r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0024FAr 3  A9 rr                        lda #>uf_strip
0024FCr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0024FEr 3               
0024FEr 3               z_strip_underflow:
0024FEr 3  60                           rts
0024FFr 3               
0024FFr 3               
0024FFr 3               ; ## SWAP ( b a -- a b ) "Exchange TOS and NOS"
0024FFr 3               ; ## "swap"  auto  ANS core
0024FFr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/SWAP"""
0024FFr 3               xt_swap:
0024FFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002502r 3               
002502r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB
002504r 3  B4 02                        ldy 2,x
002506r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002508r 3  94 00                        sty 0,x
00250Ar 3               
00250Ar 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB
00250Cr 3  B4 03                        ldy 3,x
00250Er 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
002510r 3  94 01                        sty 1,x
002512r 3               
002512r 3  60           z_swap:         rts
002513r 3               
002513r 3               
002513r 3               ; ## THEN (C: orig -- ) ( -- ) "Conditional flow control"
002513r 3               ; ## "then"  auto  ANS core
002513r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/THEN"""
002513r 3               xt_then:
002513r 3                               ; Get the address to jump to.
002513r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_here
002516r 3               
002516r 3                               ; Stuff HERE in for the branch address back
002516r 3                               ; at the IF or ELSE (origination address is on stack).
002516r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
002519r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_store
00251Cr 3               
00251Cr 3  60           z_then:         rts
00251Dr 3               
00251Dr 3               
00251Dr 3               ; ## THRU ( scr# scr# -- ) "Load screens in the given range"
00251Dr 3               ; ## "thru"  tested  ANS block ext
00251Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/block/THRU"""
00251Dr 3               
00251Dr 3               xt_thru:
00251Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002520r 3               
002520r 3                               ; We need to loop here, and can't use the data stack
002520r 3                               ; because the LOADed screens might use it.  We'll
002520r 3                               ; need to use the same trick that DO loops use, holding
002520r 3                               ; the limit and current index on the return stack.
002520r 3               
002520r 3                               ; Put the ending screen number on the return stack
002520r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002522r 3  48                           pha
002523r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002525r 3  48                           pha
002526r 3  E8                           inx
002527r 3  E8                           inx
002528r 3               @thru_loop:
002528r 3                               ; Put the starting screen number on the stack,
002528r 3                               ; but keep a copy
002528r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
00252Ar 3  48                           pha
00252Br 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00252Dr 3  48                           pha
00252Er 3               
00252Er 3                               ; Load this screen.
00252Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_load
002531r 3               
002531r 3                               ; Get the number and limit back off the stack.  Rather than
002531r 3                               ; waste time making room on the stack, just use tmp1 and tmp2.
002531r 3               
002531r 3                               ; Get the screen we just loaded.
002531r 3  68                           pla
002532r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002534r 3  68                           pla
002535r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
002537r 3               
002537r 3                               ; Get the ending screen.
002537r 3  68                           pla
002538r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
00253Ar 3  68                           pla
00253Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
00253Dr 3               
00253Dr 3                               ; See if we just loaded the last screen.
00253Dr 3                               ; A already has the MSB of the last screen in it.
00253Dr 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp1+1
00253Fr 3  D0 08                        bne @next_screen
002541r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2        ; Compare the LSB
002543r 3  C5 rr                        cmp tmp1
002545r 3  D0 02                        bne @next_screen
002547r 3  80 18                        bra @done       ; We just did the last screen.
002549r 3               
002549r 3               @next_screen:
002549r 3                               ; Put the ending screen back on the data stack.
002549r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2+1
00254Br 3  48                           pha
00254Cr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp2
00254Er 3  48                           pha
00254Fr 3               
00254Fr 3                               ; Increment the current screen.
00254Fr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1
002551r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
002553r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
002555r 3               @1:
002555r 3                               ; Put the current screen on the stack to prepare for
002555r 3                               ; the next loop.
002555r 3  CA                           dex
002556r 3  CA                           dex
002557r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
002559r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00255Br 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
00255Dr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00255Fr 3  80 C7                        bra @thru_loop
002561r 3               @done:
002561r 3  60           z_thru:         rts
002562r 3               
002562r 3               
002562r 3               
002562r 3               ; ## TICK ( "name" -- xt ) "Return a word's execution token (xt)"
002562r 3               ; ## "'"  auto  ANS core
002562r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Tick"""
002562r 3               
002562r 3               xt_tick:
002562r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_parse_name       ; ( -- addr u )
002565r 3               
002565r 3                               ; if we got a zero, there was a problem getting the
002565r 3                               ; name of the word
002565r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002567r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002569r 3  D0 05                        bne @1
00256Br 3               
00256Br 3  A9 05                        lda #err_noname
00256Dr 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
002570r 3               @1:
002570r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_find_name        ; ( addr u -- nt )
002573r 3               
002573r 3                               ; If we didn't find the word in the Dictionary, abort
002573r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002575r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002577r 3  D0 05                        bne @2
002579r 3               
002579r 3  A9 08                        lda #err_syntax
00257Br 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
00257Er 3               @2:
00257Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_name_to_int      ; ( nt -- xt )
002581r 3               
002581r 3  60           z_tick:         rts
002582r 3               
002582r 3               
002582r 3               
002582r 3               ; ## TO ( n "name" -- ) or ( "name") "Change a value"
002582r 3               ; ## "to"  auto  ANS core ext
002582r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TO
002582r 3                       ; Gives a new value to a, uh, VALUE.
002582r 3                       ;
002582r 3                       ; One possible Forth
002582r 3                       ; implementation is  ' >BODY !  but given the problems we have
002582r 3                       ; with >BODY on STC Forths, we do this the hard way. Since
002582r 3                       ; Tali Forth uses the same code for CONSTANTs and VALUEs, you
002582r 3                       ; could use this to redefine a CONSTANT, but that is a no-no.
002582r 3                       ;
002582r 3                       ; Note that the standard has different behaviors for TO depending
002582r 3                       ; on the state (https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TO).
002582r 3                       ; This makes TO state-dependent (which is bad) and also rather
002582r 3                       ; complex (see the Gforth implementation for comparison). This
002582r 3                       ; word may not be natively compiled and must be immediate. Frankly,
002582r 3                       ; it would have made more sense to have two words for this.
002582r 3                       ; """
002582r 3               
002582r 3               xt_to:
002582r 3                               ; One way or the other, we need the xt of the word after this
002582r 3                               ; one. At this point, we don't know if we are interpreted or
002582r 3                               ; compile, so we don't know if there is a value n on the stack,
002582r 3                               ; so we can't do an underflow check yet
002582r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_tick             ; ( [n] xt )
002585r 3               
002585r 3                               ; The PFA (DFA in this case) is three bytes down,
002585r 3                               ; after the jump to DOCONST
002585r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x                 ; LSB
002587r 3  18                           clc
002588r 3  69 03                        adc #3
00258Ar 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
00258Cr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x                 ; MSB
00258Er 3  69 00                        adc #0                  ; we just want the carry
002590r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
002592r 3               
002592r 3  E8                           inx
002593r 3  E8                           inx                     ; ( [n] )
002594r 3               
002594r 3                               ; Now it gets ugly. See which state we are in
002594r 3  A5 rr                        lda state
002596r 3  05 rr                        ora state+1
002598r 3  F0 34                        beq @interpret
00259Ar 3               
00259Ar 3                               ; Well, we're compiling. We want to end up with simple
00259Ar 3                               ; code that just takes the number that is TOS and saves
00259Ar 3                               ; it in the address of the xt we were just given. So we
00259Ar 3                               ; want to compile this routine:
00259Ar 3                               ;
00259Ar 3                               ;       lda 0,x                 - B5 00
00259Ar 3                               ;       sta <ADDR_LSB>          - 8D LSB MSB
00259Ar 3                               ;       lda 1,x                 - B5 01
00259Ar 3                               ;       sta <ADDR_LSB>          - 8D LSB MSB
00259Ar 3                               ;       inx                     - E8
00259Ar 3                               ;       inx                     - E8
00259Ar 3                               ;
00259Ar 3                               ; which at least is nice and short. Other than that, we pretty
00259Ar 3                               ; much have to do this the hard and long way, because with the
00259Ar 3                               ; LSBs and MSBs, we can't really put the numbers in a data
00259Ar 3                               ; range and store them with a loop. Sigh.
00259Ar 3               
00259Ar 3  A0 00                        ldy #$00                ; Code for LDA 0,X
00259Cr 3  A9 B5                        lda #$B5
00259Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
0025A1r 3               
0025A1r 3  A9 8D                        lda #$8D                ; Code for STA abs
0025A3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_a
0025A6r 3               
0025A6r 3  A4 rr                        ldy tmp1+1              ; MSB goes in Y
0025A8r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
0025AAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
0025ADr 3               
0025ADr 3  A0 01                        ldy #$01                ; Code for LDA 1,X
0025AFr 3  A9 B5                        lda #$B5
0025B1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
0025B4r 3               
0025B4r 3  A9 8D                        lda #$8D                ; Code for STA abs
0025B6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_a
0025B9r 3               
0025B9r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1                ; Calculate MSB
0025BBr 3  D0 02                        bne @1
0025BDr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
0025BFr 3               @1:
0025BFr 3  A4 rr                        ldy tmp1+1              ; MSB goes in Y
0025C1r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
0025C3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
0025C6r 3               
0025C6r 3  A0 E8                        ldy #$E8                ; Code for INX
0025C8r 3  98                           tya
0025C9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_word
0025CCr 3               
0025CCr 3  80 0F                        bra @done
0025CEr 3               
0025CEr 3               @interpret:
0025CEr 3                               ; We're interpreting, so we arrive here with n
0025CEr 3                               ; on the stack. This is an annoying place to put
0025CEr 3                               ; the underflow check because we can't
0025CEr 3                               ; automatically strip it out
0025CEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0025D1r 3               
0025D1r 3                               ; We skip over the jump to DOCONST and store the number
0025D1r 3                               ; in the Program Field Area (PDF, in this case more a
0025D1r 3                               ; Data Field Area
0025D1r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0025D3r 3  92 rr                        sta (tmp1)              ; LSB
0025D5r 3               
0025D5r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
0025D7r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x                 ; MSB
0025D9r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y            ; fall through to common
0025DBr 3               
0025DBr 3  E8                           inx                     ; DROP
0025DCr 3  E8                           inx
0025DDr 3               @done:
0025DDr 3  60           z_to:           rts
0025DEr 3               
0025DEr 3               
0025DEr 3               
0025DEr 3               ; ## TO_BODY ( xt -- addr ) "Return a word's Code Field Area (CFA)"
0025DEr 3               ; ## ">body"  auto  ANS core
0025DEr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/toBODY
0025DEr 3                       ; Given a word's execution token (xt), return the address of the
0025DEr 3                       ; start of that word's parameter field (PFA). This is defined as the
0025DEr 3                       ; address that HERE would return right after CREATE.
0025DEr 3                       ;
0025DEr 3                       ; This is a
0025DEr 3                       ; difficult word for STC Forths, because most words don't actually
0025DEr 3                       ; have a Code Field Area (CFA) to skip. We solve this by having CREATE
0025DEr 3                       ; add a flag, "has CFA" (HC), in the header so >BODY know to skip
0025DEr 3                       ; the subroutine jumps to DOVAR, DOCONST, or DODOES
0025DEr 3                       ; """
0025DEr 3               
0025DEr 3               xt_to_body:
0025DEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0025E1r 3               
0025E1r 3                               ; Ideally, xt already points to the CFA. We just need to check
0025E1r 3                               ; the HC flag for special cases
0025E1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup              ; ( xt xt )
0025E4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_int_to_name      ; ( xt nt )
0025E7r 3               
0025E7r 3                               ; The status byte is nt+1
0025E7r 3  F6 00                        inc 0,x
0025E9r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
0025EBr 3  F6 01                        inc 1,x
0025EDr 3               @1:
0025EDr 3  A1 00                        lda (0,x)               ; get status byte
0025EFr 3  29 20                        and #HC
0025F1r 3  F0 0D                        beq @no_cfa
0025F3r 3               
0025F3r 3                               ; We've got a DOVAR, DOCONST, DODEFER, DODOES or whatever,
0025F3r 3                               ; so we add three to xt, which is NOS
0025F3r 3  18                           clc
0025F4r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB
0025F6r 3  69 03                        adc #3
0025F8r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
0025FAr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB
0025FCr 3  69 00                        adc #0          ; we conly care about the carry
0025FEr 3  95 03                        sta 3,x         ; Fall through to @no_cfa
002600r 3               @no_cfa:
002600r 3  E8                           inx             ; get rid of the nt
002601r 3  E8                           inx
002602r 3               @done:
002602r 3  60           z_to_body:      rts
002603r 3               
002603r 3               
002603r 3               
002603r 3               ; ## TO_IN ( -- addr ) "Return address of the input pointer"
002603r 3               ; ## ">in"  auto  ANS core
002603r 3               xt_to_in:
002603r 3  CA                           dex
002604r 3  CA                           dex
002605r 3               
002605r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<toin
002607r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002609r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>toin      ; paranoid, should be zero
00260Br 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00260Dr 3               
00260Dr 3  60           z_to_in:        rts
00260Er 3               
00260Er 3               
00260Er 3               ; ## TO_NUMBER ( ud addr u -- ud addr u ) "Convert a number"
00260Er 3               ; ## ">number"  auto  ANS core
00260Er 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/toNUMBER
00260Er 3                       ; Convert a string to a double number. Logic here is based on the
00260Er 3                       ; routine by Phil Burk of the same name in pForth, see
00260Er 3                       ; https://github.com/philburk/pforth/blob/master/fth/numberio.fth
00260Er 3                       ; for the original Forth code. We arrive here from NUMBER which has
00260Er 3                       ; made sure that we don't have to deal with a sign and we don't have
00260Er 3                       ; to deal with a dot as a last character that signalizes double -
00260Er 3                       ; this should be a pure number string.
00260Er 3                       ;
00260Er 3                       ; This routine calles UM*, which uses tmp1, tmp2 and tmp3, so we
00260Er 3                       ; cannot access any of those.
00260Er 3                       ;
00260Er 3                       ; For the math routine, we move the inputs to the scratchpad to
00260Er 3                       ; avoid having to fool around with the Data Stack.
00260Er 3                       ;
00260Er 3                       ;     +-----+-----+-----+-----+-----+-----+-----+-----+
00260Er 3                       ;     |   UD-LO   |   UD-HI   |     N     | UD-HI-LO  |
00260Er 3                       ;     |           |           |           |           |
00260Er 3                       ;     |  S    S+1 | S+2   S+3 | S+4   S+5 | S+6   S+7 |
00260Er 3                       ;     +-----+-----+-----+-----+-----+-----+-----+-----+
00260Er 3                       ;
00260Er 3                       ; The math routine works by converting one character to its
00260Er 3                       ; numerical value (N) via DIGIT? and storing it in S+4 for
00260Er 3                       ; the moment. We then multiply the UD-HI value with the radix
00260Er 3                       ; (from BASE) using UM*, which returns a double-cell result. We
00260Er 3                       ; discard the high cell of that result (UD-HI-HI) and store the
00260Er 3                       ; low cell (UD-HI-LO) in S+6 for now. -- The second part is
00260Er 3                       ; multiplying UD-LO with the radix. The high cell (UD-LO-HI)
00260Er 3                       ; gets put in S+2, the low cell (HD-LO-LO) in S. We then use
00260Er 3                       ; a version of D+ to add ( S S+2 ) and ( S+4 S+6) together,
00260Er 3                       ; storing the result back in S and S+2, before we start another
00260Er 3                       ; round with it as the new UD-LO and UD-HI.
00260Er 3                       ; """
00260Er 3               
00260Er 3               
00260Er 3               xt_to_number:
00260Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_4
002611r 3               
002611r 3                               ; Fill the scratchpad. We arrive with ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u ).
002611r 3                               ; After this step, the original ud-lo and ud-hi will still be on
002611r 3                               ; the Data Stack, but will be ignored and later overwritten
002611r 3                               ; If >NUMBER is called by NUMBER, these should be all zeros
002611r 3  B5 06                        lda 6,x         ; ud-lo LSB
002613r 3  85 rr                        sta scratch
002615r 3  B5 07                        lda 7,x         ; ud-lo MSB
002617r 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+1
002619r 3               
002619r 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x         ; ud-hi LSB
00261Br 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+2
00261Dr 3  B5 05                        lda 5,x         ; ud-hi MSB
00261Fr 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+3
002621r 3               
002621r 3                               ; Push down one on the Data Stack to use TOS for character
002621r 3                               ; conversion ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u x )
002621r 3  CA                           dex
002622r 3  CA                           dex
002623r 3               
002623r 3               @loop:
002623r 3                               ; Get one character based on address
002623r 3  A1 04                        lda (4,x)
002625r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x                 ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u char )
002627r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x                 ; paranoid
002629r 3               
002629r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_digit_question   ; ( char -- n -1 | char 0 )
00262Cr 3               
00262Cr 3                               ; This gives us ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u char f | n f ), so we
00262Cr 3                               ; check the flag. If it is zero, we return what we have and
00262Cr 3                               ; let the caller (usually NUMBER) complain
00262Cr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
00262Er 3  D0 04                        bne @digit_ok
002630r 3               
002630r 3  E8                           inx
002631r 3  E8                           inx
002632r 3  80 67                        bra @done       ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u char )
002634r 3               
002634r 3               @digit_ok:
002634r 3                               ; Conversion was successful. We arrive here with
002634r 3                               ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u n -1 ) and can start the
002634r 3                               ; math routine
002634r 3               
002634r 3                               ; Save n so we don't have to fool around with the
002634r 3                               ; Data Stack
002634r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
002636r 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+4
002638r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
00263Ar 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+5
00263Cr 3               
00263Cr 3                               ; Now multiply ud-hi (the one in the scratchpad, not the
00263Cr 3                               ; original one on the Data Stack) with the radix from BASE.
00263Cr 3                               ; We can clobber TOS and NOS because we saved n
00263Cr 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch+2
00263Er 3  95 02                        sta 2,x         ; NOS
002640r 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch+3
002642r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
002644r 3               
002644r 3  A5 rr                        lda base
002646r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x         ; TOS
002648r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x         ; now ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u ud-hi base)
00264Ar 3               
00264Ar 3                               ; UM* returns a double-celled number
00264Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_star  ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u ud-hi-lo ud-hi-hi )
00264Dr 3               
00264Dr 3                               ; Move ud-hi-lo to safety
00264Dr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; ud-hi-lo
00264Fr 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+6
002651r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
002653r 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+7
002655r 3               
002655r 3                               ; Now we multiply ud-lo, overwriting the stack entries
002655r 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch
002657r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002659r 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch+1
00265Br 3  95 03                        sta 3,x         ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u ud-lo ud-hi-hi )
00265Dr 3               
00265Dr 3  A5 rr                        lda base
00265Fr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002661r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x         ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u ud-lo base )
002663r 3               
002663r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_um_star  ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u ud-lo-lo ud-lo-hi )
002666r 3               
002666r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002668r 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+2
00266Ar 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
00266Cr 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+3
00266Er 3               
00266Er 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
002670r 3  85 rr                        sta scratch
002672r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
002674r 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+1
002676r 3               
002676r 3                               ; We add ud-lo and n, as well as ud-hi and ud-hi-lo,
002676r 3                               ; both in the scratch pad
002676r 3  18                           clc
002677r 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch     ; ud-lo LSB
002679r 3  65 rr                        adc scratch+4   ; n LSB
00267Br 3  85 rr                        sta scratch     ; this is the new ud-lo
00267Dr 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch+1   ; ud-lo MSB
00267Fr 3  65 rr                        adc scratch+5   ; n MSB
002681r 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+1
002683r 3               
002683r 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch+2   ; LSB
002685r 3  65 rr                        adc scratch+6
002687r 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+2   ; this is the new ud-hi
002689r 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch+3   ; MSB
00268Br 3  65 rr                        adc scratch+7
00268Dr 3  85 rr                        sta scratch+3
00268Fr 3               
00268Fr 3                               ; Clean up: Get rid of one of the two top elements on
00268Fr 3                               ; the Data Stack. We don't really care which one
00268Fr 3  E8                           inx
002690r 3  E8                           inx             ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u ud-lo-lo )
002691r 3               
002691r 3                               ; One character down. Move address up
002691r 3  F6 04                        inc 4,x
002693r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
002695r 3  F6 05                        inc 5,x
002697r 3               @1:
002697r 3                               ; Decrease counter
002697r 3  D6 02                        dec 2,x
002699r 3  D0 88                        bne @loop
00269Br 3               
00269Br 3               @done:
00269Br 3                               ; Counter has reached zero or we have an error. In both
00269Br 3                               ; cases, we clean up the Data Stack and return. Error gives
00269Br 3                               ; us ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u char ), regular end is
00269Br 3                               ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u ud-lo )
00269Br 3  E8                           inx
00269Cr 3  E8                           inx             ; ( ud-lo ud-hi addr u )
00269Dr 3               
00269Dr 3                               ; The new ud-lo and ud-hi are still on the scratch pad
00269Dr 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch     ; new ud-lo
00269Fr 3  95 06                        sta 6,x
0026A1r 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch+1
0026A3r 3  95 07                        sta 7,x
0026A5r 3               
0026A5r 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch+2
0026A7r 3  95 04                        sta 4,x
0026A9r 3  A5 rr                        lda scratch+3
0026ABr 3  95 05                        sta 5,x
0026ADr 3               
0026ADr 3  60           z_to_number:    rts
0026AEr 3               
0026AEr 3               
0026AEr 3               
0026AEr 3               ; ## TO_ORDER ( wid -- ) "Add wordlist at beginning of search order"
0026AEr 3               ; ## ">order"  tested  Gforth search
0026AEr 3                       ; """https://www.complang.tuwien.ac.at/forth/gforth/Docs-html/Word-Lists.html"""
0026AEr 3               
0026AEr 3               xt_to_order:
0026AEr 3                               ; Put the wid on the return stack for now.
0026AEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r
0026B1r 3               
0026B1r 3                               ; Get the current search order.
0026B1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_get_order
0026B4r 3               
0026B4r 3                               ; Get back the wid and add it to the list.
0026B4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from
0026B7r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
0026BAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one_plus
0026BDr 3               
0026BDr 3                               ; Set the search order with the new list.
0026BDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_set_order
0026C0r 3               
0026C0r 3  60           z_to_order:     rts
0026C1r 3               
0026C1r 3               
0026C1r 3               
0026C1r 3               ; ## TO_R ( n -- )(R: -- n) "Push TOS to the Return Stack"
0026C1r 3               ; ## ">r"  auto  ANS core
0026C1r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/toR
0026C1r 3                       ; This word is handled differently for native and for
0026C1r 3                       ; subroutine coding, see `COMPILE,`. This is a complile-only
0026C1r 3                       ; word.
0026C1r 3                       ; """
0026C1r 3               xt_to_r:
0026C1r 3                               ; Save the return address. If this word is natively
0026C1r 3                               ; coded, this is a complete waste of cycles, but
0026C1r 3                               ; required for subroutine coding
0026C1r 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
0026C2r 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
0026C4r 3  7A                           ply             ; MSB
0026C5r 3               
0026C5r 3                               ; --- CUT HERE FOR NATIVE CODING ---
0026C5r 3               
0026C5r 3                               ; We check for underflow in the second step, so we can
0026C5r 3                               ; strip off the stack thrashing for native compiling first
0026C5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
0026C8r 3               
0026C8r 3                               ; now we can do the actual work
0026C8r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB
0026CAr 3  48                           pha
0026CBr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB
0026CDr 3  48                           pha
0026CEr 3               
0026CEr 3  E8                           inx
0026CFr 3  E8                           inx
0026D0r 3               
0026D0r 3                               ; --- CUT HERE FOR NATIVE CODING ---
0026D0r 3               
0026D0r 3                               ; restore return address
0026D0r 3  5A                           phy             ; MSB
0026D1r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmptos
0026D3r 3  48                           pha             ; LSB
0026D4r 3               
0026D4r 3  60           z_to_r:         rts
0026D5r 3               
0026D5r 3               
0026D5r 3               ; ## TRUE ( -- f ) "Push TRUE flag to Data Stack"
0026D5r 3               ; ## "true"  auto  ANS core ext
0026D5r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TRUE"""
0026D5r 3               xt_true:
0026D5r 3  CA                           dex
0026D6r 3  CA                           dex
0026D7r 3  A9 FF                        lda #$FF
0026D9r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0026DBr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0026DDr 3               
0026DDr 3  60           z_true:         rts
0026DEr 3               
0026DEr 3               
0026DEr 3               ; ## TUCK ( b a -- a b a ) "Copy TOS below NOS"

0026DEr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TUCK"""
0026DEr 3               xt_tuck:

0026E1r 3

0026E5r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
0026E7r 3  95 04                        sta 4,x
0026E9r 3  94 02                        sty 2,x
0026EBr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0026EDr 3               
0026EDr 3  B4 05                        ldy 5,x         ; MSB
0026EFr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
0026F1r 3  95 05                        sta 5,x
0026F3r 3  94 03                        sty 3,x         ; bba
0026F5r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x         ; baa
0026F7r 3               
0026F7r 3  60           z_tuck:         rts

002701r 3               xt_two_drop:

002709r 3               ; ## TWO_DUP ( a b -- a b a b ) "Duplicate first two stack elements"
002709r 3               ; ## "2dup"  auto  ANS core
002709r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TwoDUP"""
002709r 3               xt_two_dup:
002709r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00270Cr 3               
00270Cr 3  CA                           dex
00270Dr 3  CA                           dex
00270Er 3  CA                           dex
00270Fr 3  CA                           dex
002710r 3               
002710r 3  B5 04                        lda 4,x         ; TOS
002712r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002714r 3  B5 05                        lda 5,x
002716r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x

002720r 3

002721r 3               
002721r 3               ; ## TWO_FETCH ( addr -- n1 n2 ) "Fetch the cell pair n1 n2 stored at addr"
002721r 3               ; ## "2@"  auto  ANS core
002721r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TwoFetch
002721r 3                       ; Note n2 stored at addr and n1 in the next cell -- in our case,
002721r 3                       ; the next two bytes. This is equvalent to  `DUP CELL+ @ SWAP @`
002721r 3                       ; """
002721r 3               xt_two_fetch:
002721r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002724r 3               
002724r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002726r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002728r 3  B4 01                        ldy 1,x
00272Ar 3  84 rr                        sty tmp1+1
00272Cr 3               
00272Cr 3  CA                           dex             ; reuse one stack element
00272Dr 3  CA                           dex
00272Er 3               
00272Er 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)      ; copy LSB
002730r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002732r 3  A0 01                        ldy #1          ; copy next
002734r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
002736r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002738r 3  C8                           iny             ; copy next
002739r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
00273Br 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
00273Dr 3  C8                           iny             ; copy next
00273Er 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y
002740r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
002742r 3               
002742r 3  60           z_two_fetch:    rts
002743r 3               
002743r 3               ; ## TWO_OVER ( d1 d2 -- d1 d2 d1 ) "Copy double word NOS to TOS"
002743r 3               ; ## "2over"  auto  ANS core
002743r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TwoOVER"""
002743r 3               xt_two_over:
002743r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_4
002746r 3               
002746r 3  CA                           dex
002747r 3  CA                           dex
002748r 3  CA                           dex
002749r 3  CA                           dex
00274Ar 3               
00274Ar 3  B5 08                        lda 8,x
00274Cr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00274Er 3               
00274Er 3  B5 09                        lda 9,x
002750r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002752r 3               
002752r 3  B5 0A                        lda 10,x
002754r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002756r 3               
002756r 3  B5 0B                        lda 11,x
002758r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
00275Ar 3               
00275Ar 3  60           z_two_over:     rts

00275Br 3               ; ## TWO_R_FETCH ( -- n n ) "Copy top two entries from Return Stack"
00275Br 3               ; ## "2r@"  auto  ANS core ext
00275Br 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TwoRFetch
00275Br 3                       ;
00275Br 3                       ; This is R> R> 2DUP >R >R SWAP but we can do it a lot faster in
00275Br 3                       ; assembler. We use trickery to access the elements on the Return
00275Br 3                       ; Stack instead of pulling the return address first and storing
00275Br 3                       ; it somewhere else like for 2R> and 2>R. In this version, we leave
00275Br 3                       ; it as Never Native; at some point, we should compare versions to
00275Br 3                       ; see if an Always Native version would be better
00275Br 3                       ; """
00275Br 3               xt_two_r_fetch:
00275Br 3               		; make room on the Data Stack
00275Br 3  CA                           dex
00275Cr 3  CA                           dex
00275Dr 3  CA                           dex
00275Er 3  CA                           dex
00275Fr 3               
00275Fr 3                               ; Get four bytes off of Return Stack. This assumes that
00275Fr 3                               ; we took a subroutine jump here so the first two entries
00275Fr 3                               ; are the return address
00275Fr 3  8A                           txa
002760r 3  BA                           tsx
002761r 3  DA                           phx             ; 65c02 has no TXY, so do it the hard way
002762r 3  7A                           ply
002763r 3  AA                           tax
002764r 3               
002764r 3                               ; The Return Stack addreses $0101 and $0102 are occupied by
002764r 3                               ; the return address for this word. This is a whole lot
002764r 3                               ; easier on the 65816
002764r 3  B9 03 01                     lda $0103,y     ; LSB of top entry
002767r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002769r 3  B9 04 01                     lda $0104,y     ; MSB of top entry
00276Cr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
00276Er 3  B9 05 01                     lda $0105,y     ; LSB of bottom entry
002771r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002773r 3  B9 06 01                     lda $0106,y     ; MSB of top entry
002776r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
002778r 3               
002778r 3  60           z_two_r_fetch:  rts
002779r 3               
002779r 3               
002779r 3               ; ## TWO_R_FROM ( -- n1 n2 ) (R: n1 n2 -- ) "Pull two cells from Return Stack"
002779r 3               ; ## "2r>"  auto  ANS core ext
002779r 3               	    ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TwoRfrom
002779r 3                       ; Pull top two entries from Return Stack.
002779r 3                       ;
002779r 3                       ; Is the same as
002779r 3                       ; R> R> SWAP. As with R>, the problem with the is word is that
002779r 3                       ; the top value on the ReturnStack for a STC Forth is the
002779r 3                       ; return address, which we need to get out of the way first.
002779r 3                       ; Native compile needs to be handled as a special case.
002779r 3                       ; """
002779r 3               xt_two_r_from:
002779r 3                               ; save the return address
002779r 3  68                           pla                     ; LSB
00277Ar 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
00277Cr 3  68                           pla                     ; MSB
00277Dr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
00277Fr 3               
00277Fr 3                               ; --- CUT HERE FOR NATIVE CODING ---
00277Fr 3               
00277Fr 3               		; make room on stack
00277Fr 3  CA                           dex
002780r 3  CA                           dex
002781r 3  CA                           dex
002782r 3  CA                           dex
002783r 3               
002783r 3                               ; In theory, we should test for underflow on the Return
002783r 3                               ; Stack. However, given the traffic there with an STC
002783r 3                               ; Forth, that's probably not really useful
002783r 3               
002783r 3                               ; now we can access the data
002783r 3  68                           pla                     ; LSB
002784r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002786r 3  68                           pla                     ; MSB
002787r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002789r 3               
002789r 3  68                           pla                     ; LSB
00278Ar 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
00278Cr 3  68                           pla                     ; MSB
00278Dr 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
00278Fr 3               
00278Fr 3                               ; --- CUT HERE FOR NATIVE CODING ---
00278Fr 3               
00278Fr 3                               ; restore return address
00278Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1              ; MSB
002791r 3  48                           pha
002792r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1                ; LSB
002794r 3  48                           pha
002795r 3               
002795r 3  60           z_two_r_from:   rts
002796r 3               
002796r 3               
002796r 3               ; ## TWO_SLASH ( n -- n ) "Divide TOS by two"
002796r 3               ; ## "2/"  auto  ANS core
002796r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TwoDiv"""
002796r 3               xt_two_slash:
002796r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002799r 3               
002799r 3                               ; We can't just LSR the LSB and ROR the MSB because that
002799r 3                               ; would do bad things to the sign
002799r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
00279Br 3  0A                           asl                     ; save the sign
00279Cr 3  76 01                        ror 1,x
00279Er 3  76 00                        ror 0,x
0027A0r 3               
0027A0r 3  60           z_two_slash:    rts
0027A1r 3

0027A1r 3                       ; """
0027A1r 3               xt_two_star:
0027A1r 3               xt_cells:

0027A4r 3               
0027A4r 3  16 00                        asl 0,x
0027A6r 3  36 01                        rol 1,x
0027A8r 3               z_cells:
0027A8r 3  60           z_two_star:     rts
0027A9r 3               
0027A9r 3               
0027A9r 3               ; ## TWO_STORE ( n1 n2 addr -- ) "Store two numbers at given address"
0027A9r 3               ; ## "2!"  auto  ANS core
0027A9r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TwoStore
0027A9r 3                       ; Stores so n2 goes to addr and n1 to the next consecutive cell.
0027A9r 3                       ; Is equivalent to  `SWAP OVER ! CELL+ !`
0027A9r 3                       ; """
0027A9r 3               xt_two_store:
0027A9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
0027ACr 3               
0027ACr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0027AEr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
0027B0r 3  B4 01                        ldy 1,x
0027B2r 3  84 rr                        sty tmp1+1
0027B4r 3               
0027B4r 3  E8                           inx
0027B5r 3  E8                           inx
0027B6r 3               
0027B6r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; copy MSB
0027B8r 3  92 rr                        sta (tmp1)
0027BAr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; copy next
0027BCr 3  A0 01                        ldy #1
0027BEr 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
0027C0r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; copy next
0027C2r 3  C8                           iny
0027C3r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
0027C5r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; copy MSB
0027C7r 3  C8                           iny
0027C8r 3  91 rr                        sta (tmp1),y
0027CAr 3               
0027CAr 3  E8                           inx             ; 2DROP
0027CBr 3  E8                           inx
0027CCr 3  E8                           inx
0027CDr 3  E8                           inx
0027CEr 3               
0027CEr 3  60           z_two_store:    rts
0027CFr 3               
0027CFr 3               
0027CFr 3               ; ## TWO_SWAP ( n1 n2 n3 n4 -- n3 n4 n1 n1 ) "Exchange two double words"
0027CFr 3               ; ## "2swap"  auto  ANS core
0027CFr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TwoSWAP"""
0027CFr 3               xt_two_swap:
0027CFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_4
0027D2r 3

0027D2r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0027D4r 3  B4 04                        ldy 4,x
0027D6r 3  95 04                        sta 4,x
0027D8r 3  94 00                        sty 0,x
0027DAr 3               
0027DAr 3                               ; 1 <-> 5
0027DAr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0027DCr 3  B4 05                        ldy 5,x
0027DEr 3  95 05                        sta 5,x
0027E0r 3  94 01                        sty 1,x
0027E2r 3               
0027E2r 3                               ; 2 <-> 6
0027E2r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
0027E4r 3  B4 06                        ldy 6,x
0027E6r 3  95 06                        sta 6,x
0027E8r 3  94 02                        sty 2,x
0027EAr 3

0027EAr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
0027ECr 3  B4 07                        ldy 7,x
0027EEr 3  95 07                        sta 7,x
0027F0r 3  94 03                        sty 3,x
0027F2r 3               
0027F2r 3  60           z_two_swap:     rts
0027F3r 3               
0027F3r 3               
0027F3r 3               ; ## TWO_TO_R ( n1 n2 -- )(R: -- n1 n2 "Push top two entries to Return Stack"
0027F3r 3               ; ## "2>r"  auto  ANS core ext
0027F3r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TwotoR
0027F3r 3                       ; Push top two entries to Return Stack.
0027F3r 3                       ;
0027F3r 3                       ; The same as SWAP >R >R
0027F3r 3                       ; except that if we jumped here, the return address will be in the
0027F3r 3                       ; way. May not be natively compiled unless we're clever and use
0027F3r 3                       ; special routines.
0027F3r 3                       ; """
0027F3r 3               xt_two_to_r:
0027F3r 3                               ; save the return address
0027F3r 3  68                           pla             ; LSB
0027F4r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
0027F6r 3  68                           pla             ; MSB
0027F7r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
0027F9r 3               
0027F9r 3                               ; --- CUT HERE FOR NATIVE CODING ---
0027F9r 3               
0027F9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0027FCr 3               
0027FCr 3                               ; now we can move the data
0027FCr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x         ; MSB
0027FEr 3  48                           pha
0027FFr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x         ; LSB
002801r 3  48                           pha
002802r 3               
002802r 3                               ; now we can move the data
002802r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB
002804r 3  48                           pha
002805r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; LSB
002807r 3  48                           pha
002808r 3               
002808r 3  E8                           inx
002809r 3  E8                           inx
00280Ar 3  E8                           inx
00280Br 3  E8                           inx
00280Cr 3               
00280Cr 3                               ; --- CUT HERE FOR NATIVE CODING ---
00280Cr 3               
00280Cr 3                               ; restore return address
00280Cr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1      ; MSB
00280Er 3  48                           pha
00280Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1        ; LSB
002811r 3  48                           pha
002812r 3               
002812r 3  60           z_two_to_r:     rts
002813r 3               
002813r 3               
002813r 3               ; ## TWO_CONSTANT (C: d "name" -- ) ( -- d) "Create a constant for a double word"
002813r 3               ; ## "2constant"  auto  ANS double
002813r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/double/TwoCONSTANT
002813r 3                       ;
002813r 3                       ; Based on the Forth code
002813r 3                       ; : 2CONSTANT ( D -- )  CREATE SWAP , , DOES> DUP @ SWAP CELL+ @ ;
002813r 3                       ; """
002813r 3               xt_two_constant:
002813r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002816r 3

002819r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
00281Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
00281Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
002822r 3               
002822r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr does_runtime    ; does> turns into these two routines.
002825r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr dodoes
002828r 3               
002828r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
00282Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch
00282Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
002831r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cell_plus
002834r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch
002837r 3

002838r 3                       ; Based on the Forth code

002838r 3                       ; """
002838r 3               xt_two_literal:

002845r 3               ; ## TWO_VARIABLE ( "name" -- ) "Create a variable for a double word"
002845r 3               ; ## "2variable"  auto  ANS double
002845r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/double/TwoVARIABLE
002845r 3                       ; The variable is not initialized to zero.
002845r 3                       ;
002845r 3                       ; This can be realized in Forth as either
002845r 3                       ; CREATE 2 CELLS ALLOT  or just  CREATE 0 , 0 ,
002845r 3                       ; """
002845r 3               xt_two_variable:
002845r 3                               ; We just let CRATE and ALLOT do the heavy lifting
002845r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_create
002848r 3               
002848r 3  CA                           dex
002849r 3  CA                           dex
00284Ar 3  A9 04                        lda #4
00284Cr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00284Er 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002850r 3               
002850r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_allot
002853r 3
