002854r 3               
002854r 3               ; ## TYPE ( addr u -- ) "Print string"
002854r 3               ; ## "type"  auto  ANS core
002854r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/TYPE
002854r 3                       ; Works through EMIT to allow OUTPUT revectoring.
002854r 3                       ; """
002854r 3               
002854r 3               xt_type:
002854r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002857r 3               
002857r 3                               ; Save the starting address into tmp1
002857r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
002859r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
00285Br 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
00285Dr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
00285Fr 3               @loop:
00285Fr 3                               ; done if length is zero
00285Fr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002861r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002863r 3  F0 15                        beq @done
002865r 3               
002865r 3                               ; Send the current character
002865r 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
002867r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a      ; avoids stack foolery
00286Ar 3               
00286Ar 3                               ; Move the address along (in tmp1)
00286Ar 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1
00286Cr 3  D0 02                        bne @1
00286Er 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
002870r 3               @1:
002870r 3                               ; Reduce the count (on the data stack)
002870r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002872r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
002874r 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
002876r 3               @2:
002876r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
002878r 3               
002878r 3  80 E5                        bra @loop
00287Ar 3               @done:
00287Ar 3  E8                           inx
00287Br 3  E8                           inx
00287Cr 3  E8                           inx
00287Dr 3  E8                           inx
00287Er 3               
00287Er 3  60           z_type:         rts
00287Fr 3               
00287Fr 3               
00287Fr 3               
00287Fr 3               ; ## U_DOT ( u -- ) "Print TOS as unsigned number"
00287Fr 3               ; ## "u."  tested  ANS core
00287Fr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Ud
00287Fr 3                       ;
00287Fr 3                       ; This is : U. 0 <# #S #> TYPE SPACE ; in Forth
00287Fr 3                       ; We use the internal assembler function print_u followed
00287Fr 3                       ; by a single space
00287Fr 3                       ; """
00287Fr 3               xt_u_dot:
00287Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002882r 3               
002882r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr print_u
002885r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
002887r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
00288Ar 3               
00288Ar 3  60           z_u_dot:        rts
00288Br 3               
00288Br 3               
00288Br 3               ; ## U_DOT_R ( u u -- ) "Print NOS as unsigned number right-justified with TOS width"
00288Br 3               ; ## "u.r"  tested  ANS core ext
00288Br 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UDotR"""
00288Br 3               xt_u_dot_r:
00288Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
00288Er 3               
00288Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r
002891r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
002894r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_less_number_sign
002897r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_s
00289Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_greater
00289Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from
0028A0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_over
0028A3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
0028A6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_spaces
0028A9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
0028ACr 3               
0028ACr 3  60           z_u_dot_r:      rts
0028ADr 3               
0028ADr 3               
0028ADr 3               ; ## U_GREATER_THAN ( n m -- f ) "Return true if NOS > TOS (unsigned)"
0028ADr 3               ; ## "u>"  auto  ANS core ext
0028ADr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Umore"""
0028ADr 3               xt_u_greater_than:
0028ADr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0028B0r 3               
0028B0r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
0028B2r 3  D5 02                        cmp 2,x
0028B4r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
0028B6r 3  F5 03                        sbc 3,x
0028B8r 3  E8                           inx
0028B9r 3  E8                           inx
0028BAr 3               
0028BAr 3  A9 00                        lda #0
0028BCr 3  69 FF                        adc #$ff
0028BEr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x         ; store flag
0028C0r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0028C2r 3               
0028C2r 3  60           z_u_greater_than:    rts
0028C3r 3               
0028C3r 3               ; ## U_LESS_THAN ( n m -- f ) "Return true if NOS < TOS (unsigned)"
0028C3r 3               ; ## "u<"  auto  ANS core
0028C3r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Uless"""
0028C3r 3               xt_u_less_than:
0028C3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
0028C6r 3               
0028C6r 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
0028C8r 3  D5 00                        cmp 0,x
0028CAr 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
0028CCr 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x
0028CEr 3  E8                           inx
0028CFr 3  E8                           inx
0028D0r 3               
0028D0r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
0028D2r 3  69 FF                        adc #$ff
0028D4r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x         ; store flag
0028D6r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0028D8r 3               
0028D8r 3  60           z_u_less_than:    rts
0028D9r 3               
0028D9r 3               
0028D9r 3               ; ## UD_DOT ( d -- ) "Print double as unsigned"
0028D9r 3               ; ## "ud."  auto  Tali double
0028D9r 3                       ;
0028D9r 3                       ; """Based on the Forth code  : UD. <# #S #> TYPE SPACE ;
0028D9r 3                       ; """
0028D9r 3               xt_ud_dot:
0028D9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2 ; double number
0028DCr 3               
0028DCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_less_number_sign
0028DFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_s
0028E2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_greater
0028E5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
0028E8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
0028EBr 3

0028ECr 3               
0028ECr 3               
0028ECr 3               ; ## UD_DOT_R ( d u -- ) "Print unsigned double right-justified u wide"
0028ECr 3               ; ## "ud.r"  auto  Tali double
0028ECr 3                       ;
0028ECr 3                       ; """Based on the Forth code : UD.R  >R <# #S #> R> OVER - SPACES TYPE ;
0028ECr 3                       ; """
0028ECr 3               xt_ud_dot_r:
0028ECr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
0028EFr 3               
0028EFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r
0028F2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_less_number_sign
0028F5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_s
0028F8r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_number_sign_greater
0028FBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from
0028FEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_over
002901r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
002904r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_spaces
002907r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
00290Ar 3               
00290Ar 3  60           z_ud_dot_r:      rts
00290Br 3               
00290Br 3               
00290Br 3               ; ## UM_SLASH_MOD ( ud u -- ur u ) "32/16 -> 16 division"
00290Br 3               ; ## "um/mod"  auto  ANS core
00290Br 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UMDivMOD
00290Br 3                       ; Divide double cell number by single cell number, returning the
00290Br 3                       ; quotient as TOS and any remainder as NOS. All numbers are unsigned.
00290Br 3                       ; This is the basic division operation all others use. Based on FIG
00290Br 3                       ; Forth code, modified by Garth Wilson, see
00290Br 3                       ; http://6502.org/source/integers/ummodfix/ummodfix.htm
00290Br 3                       ;
00290Br 3                       ; This uses tmp1, tmp1+1, and tmptos
00290Br 3                       ; """
00290Br 3               
00290Br 3               xt_um_slash_mod:
00290Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
00290Er 3               
00290Er 3                               ; catch division by zero
00290Er 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002910r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002912r 3  D0 05                        bne @not_zero
002914r 3               
002914r 3  A9 04                        lda #err_divzero
002916r 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
002919r 3               
002919r 3               @not_zero:
002919r 3                               ; We loop 17 times
002919r 3  A9 11                        lda #17
00291Br 3  85 rr                        sta tmptos
00291Dr 3               
00291Dr 3               @loop:
00291Dr 3                               ; rotate low cell of dividend one bit left (LSB)
00291Dr 3  36 04                        rol 4,x
00291Fr 3  36 05                        rol 5,x
002921r 3               
002921r 3                               ; loop control
002921r 3  C6 rr                        dec tmptos
002923r 3  F0 22                        beq @done
002925r 3               
002925r 3                               ; rotate high cell of dividend one bit left (MSB)
002925r 3  36 02                        rol 2,x
002927r 3  36 03                        rol 3,x
002929r 3               
002929r 3  64 rr                        stz tmp1        ; store the bit we got from hi cell (MSB)
00292Br 3  26 rr                        rol tmp1
00292Dr 3               
00292Dr 3                               ; subtract dividend hi cell minus divisor
00292Dr 3  38                           sec
00292Er 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
002930r 3  F5 00                        sbc 0,x
002932r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
002934r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
002936r 3  F5 01                        sbc 1,x
002938r 3               
002938r 3  A8                           tay
002939r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
00293Br 3  E9 00                        sbc #0
00293Dr 3  90 DE                        bcc @loop
00293Fr 3               
00293Fr 3                               ; make result new dividend high cell
00293Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
002941r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002943r 3  94 03                        sty 3,x         ; used as temp storage
002945r 3               
002945r 3  80 D6                        bra @loop
002947r 3               @done:
002947r 3  E8                           inx
002948r 3  E8                           inx
002949r 3               
002949r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
00294Cr 3               
00294Cr 3  60           z_um_slash_mod: rts
00294Dr 3               
00294Dr 3               
00294Dr 3               
00294Dr 3               ; ## UM_STAR ( u u -- ud ) "Multiply 16 x 16 -> 32"
00294Dr 3               ; ## "um*"  auto  ANS core
00294Dr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UMTimes
00294Dr 3                       ; Multiply two unsigned 16 bit numbers, producing a 32 bit result.
00294Dr 3                       ; Old Forth versions such as FIG Forth call this U*
00294Dr 3                       ;
00294Dr 3                       ; This is based on modified FIG Forth code by Dr. Jefyll, see
00294Dr 3                       ; http://forum.6502.org/viewtopic.php?f=9&t=689 for a detailed
00294Dr 3                       ; discussion.
00294Dr 3                       ;
00294Dr 3                       ; We don't use the system scratch pad (SYSPAD) for temp
00294Dr 3                       ; storage because >NUMBER uses it as well, but instead tmp1 to
00294Dr 3                       ; tmp3 (tmp1 is N in the original code, tmp1+1 is N+1, etc).
00294Dr 3                       ;
00294Dr 3                       ; Consider switching to a table-supported version based on
00294Dr 3                       ; http://codebase64.org/doku.php?id=base:seriously_fast_multiplication
00294Dr 3                       ; http://codebase64.org/doku.php?id=magazines:chacking16#d_graphics_for_the_masseslib3d>
00294Dr 3                       ; http://forum.6502.org/viewtopic.php?p=205#p205
00294Dr 3                       ; http://forum.6502.org/viewtopic.php?f=9&t=689
00294Dr 3                       ; """
00294Dr 3               
00294Dr 3               xt_um_star:
00294Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002950r 3               
002950r 3                               ; to eliminate clc inside the loop, the value at
002950r 3                               ; tmp1 is reduced by 1 in advance
002950r 3  18                           clc
002951r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x         ; copy TOS to tmp2
002953r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0
002955r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2
002957r 3               
002957r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002959r 3  E9 00                        sbc #0
00295Br 3  90 31                        bcc @zero       ; is TOS zero?
00295Dr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp2+1
00295Fr 3               
00295Fr 3  A9 00                        lda #0
002961r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002963r 3  86 rr                        stx tmp3        ; tested for exit from outer loop
002965r 3  CA                           dex
002966r 3  CA                           dex
002967r 3               
002967r 3               @outer_loop:
002967r 3  A0 08                        ldy #8          ; counter inner loop
002969r 3  56 04                        lsr 4,x         ; think "2,x" then later "3,x"
00296Br 3               
00296Br 3               @inner_loop:
00296Br 3  90 0C                        bcc @no_add
00296Dr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1      ; save time, don't CLC
00296Fr 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
002971r 3  65 rr                        adc tmp2
002973r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002975r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1+1
002977r 3  65 rr                        adc tmp2+1
002979r 3               
002979r 3               @no_add:
002979r 3  6A                           ror
00297Ar 3  66 rr                        ror tmp1
00297Cr 3  76 04                        ror 4,x         ; think "2,x" then later "3,x"
00297Er 3               
00297Er 3  88                           dey
00297Fr 3  D0 EA                        bne @inner_loop ; go back for one more shift?
002981r 3               
002981r 3  E8                           inx
002982r 3  E4 rr                        cpx tmp3
002984r 3  D0 E1                        bne @outer_loop ; go back for eight more shifts?
002986r 3               
002986r 3                               ; all done, store high word of result
002986r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002988r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp1
00298Ar 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
00298Cr 3  80 04                        bra @done
00298Er 3               
00298Er 3               @zero:
00298Er 3  74 02                        stz 2,x
002990r 3  74 03                        stz 3,x
002992r 3               @done:
002992r 3  60           z_um_star:      rts
002993r 3               
002993r 3               
002993r 3               
002993r 3               ; ## UNLOOP ( -- )(R: n1 n2 n3 ---) "Drop loop control from Return stack"
002993r 3               ; ## "unloop"  auto  ANS core
002993r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UNLOOP
002993r 3                       ;
002993r 3                       ; Note that 6xPLA uses just as many bytes as a loop would
002993r 3                       ; """
002993r 3               xt_unloop:
002993r 3                               ; Drop fudge number (limit/start from DO/?DO off the
002993r 3                               ; return stack
002993r 3  68                           pla
002994r 3  68                           pla
002995r 3  68                           pla
002996r 3  68                           pla
002997r 3               
002997r 3                               ; Now drop the LEAVE address that was below them off
002997r 3                               ; the Return Stack as well
002997r 3  68                           pla
002998r 3  68                           pla
002999r 3               
002999r 3  60           z_unloop:       rts
00299Ar 3               
00299Ar 3               
00299Ar 3               ; ## UNTIL (C: dest -- ) ( -- ) "Loop flow control"
00299Ar 3               ; ## "until"  auto  ANS core
00299Ar 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UNTIL"""
00299Ar 3               xt_until:
00299Ar 3                               ; Compile a 0BRANCH
00299Ar 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>zero_branch_runtime
00299Cr 3  A9 rr                        lda #<zero_branch_runtime
00299Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
0029A1r 3               
0029A1r 3                               ; The address to loop back to is on the stack.
0029A1r 3                               ; Just compile it as the destination for the
0029A1r 3                               ; 0branch.
0029A1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
0029A4r 3               
0029A4r 3  60           z_until:        rts
0029A5r 3               
0029A5r 3               
0029A5r 3               ; ## UNUSED ( -- u ) "Return size of space available to Dictionary"
0029A5r 3               ; ## "unused"  auto  ANS core ext
0029A5r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/UNUSED
0029A5r 3                       ; UNUSED does not include the ACCEPT history buffers. Total RAM
0029A5r 3                       ; should be HERE + UNUSED + <history buffer size>, the last of which
0029A5r 3                       ; defaults to $400
0029A5r 3                       ; """
0029A5r 3               xt_unused:
0029A5r 3  CA                           dex
0029A6r 3  CA                           dex
0029A7r 3               
0029A7r 3  A9 FF                        lda #<cp_end
0029A9r 3  38                           sec
0029AAr 3  E5 rr                        sbc cp
0029ACr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0029AEr 3               
0029AEr 3  A9 7F                        lda #>cp_end
0029B0r 3  E5 rr                        sbc cp+1
0029B2r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0029B4r 3               
0029B4r 3  60           z_unused:       rts
0029B5r 3               
0029B5r 3               
0029B5r 3               ; ## UPDATE ( -- ) "Mark current block as dirty"
0029B5r 3               ; ## "update"  auto  ANS block
0029B5r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/block/UPDATE"""
0029B5r 3               xt_update:
0029B5r 3                               ; Turn on the dirty bit. We can't use TSB here because it only
0029B5r 3                               ; has Absolute and Direct Pages addressing modes
0029B5r 3  A0 2C                        ldy #buffstatus_offset
0029B7r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
0029B9r 3  09 02                        ora #2          ; Turn on dirty flag (bit 2)
0029BBr 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y
0029BDr 3               
0029BDr 3  60           z_update:       rts
0029BEr 3               
0029BEr 3               
0029BEr 3               ; ## USERADDR ( -- addr ) "Push address of base address of user variables"
0029BEr 3               ; ## "useraddr"  tested  Tali Forth
0029BEr 3               xt_useraddr:
0029BEr 3  CA                           dex
0029BFr 3  CA                           dex
0029C0r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<up
0029C2r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
0029C4r 3  A9 rr                        lda #>up
0029C6r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
0029C8r 3               
0029C8r 3  60           z_useraddr:     rts
0029C9r 3               
0029C9r 3               
0029C9r 3               ; ## VALUE ( n "name" -- ) "Define a value"
0029C9r 3               ; ## "value"  auto  ANS core
0029C9r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/VALUE
0029C9r 3                       ;
0029C9r 3                       ; This is a dummy header for the WORDLIST. The actual code is
0029C9r 3                       ; identical to that of CONSTANT
0029C9r 3                       ; """
0029C9r 3               
0029C9r 3               
0029C9r 3               ; ## VARIABLE ( "name" -- ) "Define a variable"
0029C9r 3               ; ## "variable"  auto  ANS core
0029C9r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/VARIABLE
0029C9r 3                       ; There are various Forth definitions for this word, such as
0029C9r 3                       ; `CREATE 1 CELLS ALLOT`  or  `CREATE 0 ,`  We use a variant of the
0029C9r 3                       ; second one so the variable is initialized to zero
0029C9r 3                       ; """
0029C9r 3               xt_variable:
0029C9r 3                               ; we let CREATE do the heavy lifting
0029C9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_create
0029CCr 3               
0029CCr 3                               ; there is no "STZ (CP)" so we have to do this the hard
0029CCr 3                               ; way
0029CCr 3  A9 00                        lda #0
0029CEr 3               
0029CEr 3  92 rr                        sta (cp)
0029D0r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp
0029D2r 3  D0 02                        bne @1
0029D4r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
0029D6r 3               @1:
0029D6r 3  92 rr                        sta (cp)
0029D8r 3  E6 rr                        inc cp
0029DAr 3  D0 02                        bne @2
0029DCr 3  E6 rr                        inc cp+1
0029DEr 3               @2:
0029DEr 3                               ; Now we need to adjust the length of the complete word by two
0029DEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr adjust_z
0029E1r 3               
0029E1r 3  60           z_variable:     rts
0029E2r 3               
0029E2r 3               
0029E2r 3               ; ## WHILE ( C: dest -- orig dest ) ( x -- ) "Loop flow control"
0029E2r 3               ; ## "while"  auto  ANS core
0029E2r 3                       ; """http://forth-standard.org/standard/core/WHILE"""
0029E2r 3               xt_while:
0029E2r 3                               ; Compile a 0branch
0029E2r 3  A0 rr                        ldy #>zero_branch_runtime
0029E4r 3  A9 rr                        lda #<zero_branch_runtime
0029E6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr cmpl_subroutine
0029E9r 3               
0029E9r 3                               ; Put the address (here) where the destination
0029E9r 3                               ; address needs to go so it can be put there later.
0029E9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_here
0029ECr 3               
0029ECr 3                               ; Fill in the destination address with 0 for now.
0029ECr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_zero
0029EFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_comma
0029F2r 3               
0029F2r 3                               ; Swap the two addresses on the stack.
0029F2r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_swap
0029F5r 3               
0029F5r 3  60           z_while:        rts
0029F6r 3               
0029F6r 3               
0029F6r 3               ; ## WITHIN ( n1 n2 n3 -- ) "See if within a range"
0029F6r 3               ; ## "within"  auto  ANS core ext
0029F6r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/WITHIN
0029F6r 3                       ;
0029F6r 3                       ; This an assembler version of the ANS Forth implementation
0029F6r 3                       ; at https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/WITHIN which is
0029F6r 3                       ; OVER - >R - R> U<  note there is an alternative high-level version
0029F6r 3                       ; ROT TUCK > -ROT > INVERT AND
0029F6r 3                       ; """"
0029F6r 3               xt_within:
0029F6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_3
0029F9r 3               
0029F9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_over
0029FCr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
0029FFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_to_r
002A02r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
002A05r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_r_from
002A08r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_u_less_than
002A0Br 3               
002A0Br 3  60           z_within:       rts
002A0Cr 3               
002A0Cr 3               
002A0Cr 3               ; ## WORD ( char "name " -- caddr ) "Parse input stream"
002A0Cr 3               ; ## "word"  auto  ANS core
002A0Cr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/WORD
002A0Cr 3                       ; Obsolete parsing word included for backwards compatibility only.
002A0Cr 3                       ; Do not use this, use `PARSE` or `PARSE-NAME`. Skips leading delimiters
002A0Cr 3                       ; and copies word to storage area for a maximum size of 255 bytes.
002A0Cr 3                       ; Returns the result as a counted string (requires COUNT to convert
002A0Cr 3                       ; to modern format), and inserts a space after the string. See "Forth
002A0Cr 3                       ; Programmer's Handbook" 3rd edition p. 159 and
002A0Cr 3                       ; http://www.forth200x.org/documents/html/rationale.html#rat:core:PARSE
002A0Cr 3                       ; for discussions of why you shouldn't be using WORD anymore.
002A0Cr 3                       ;
002A0Cr 3                       ; Forth
002A0Cr 3                       ; would be   PARSE DUP BUFFER1 C! OUTPUT 1+ SWAP MOVE BUFFER1
002A0Cr 3                       ; We only allow input of 255 chars. Seriously, use PARSE-NAME.
002A0Cr 3                       ; """
002A0Cr 3               
002A0Cr 3               xt_word:
002A0Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002A0Fr 3               
002A0Fr 3                               ; Skip over leading delimiters - this is like PARSE-NAME,
002A0Fr 3                               ; but unlike PARSE
002A0Fr 3  A4 rr                        ldy toin                ; >IN
002A11r 3               @loop:
002A11r 3  C4 rr                        cpy ciblen              ; quit if end of input
002A13r 3  F0 09                        beq @found_char
002A15r 3  B1 rr                        lda (cib),y
002A17r 3  D5 00                        cmp 0,x                 ; ASCII of delimiter
002A19r 3  D0 03                        bne @found_char
002A1Br 3               
002A1Br 3  C8                           iny
002A1Cr 3  80 F3                        bra @loop
002A1Er 3               @found_char:
002A1Er 3                               ; Save index of where word starts
002A1Er 3  84 rr                        sty toin
002A20r 3               
002A20r 3                               ; The real work is done by parse
002A20r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_parse            ; Returns ( addr u )
002A23r 3               
002A23r 3                               ; Convert the modern ( addr u ) string format to obsolete
002A23r 3                               ; ( caddr ) format. We just do this in the Dictionary
002A23r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002A25r 3  92 rr                        sta (cp)                ; Save length of string
002A27r 3  48                           pha                     ; Keep copy of length for later
002A28r 3               
002A28r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup              ; ( addr u u )
002A2Br 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
002A2Dr 3  18                           clc
002A2Er 3  69 01                        adc #1
002A30r 3  95 02                        sta 2,x                 ; LSB of CP
002A32r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
002A34r 3  69 00                        adc #0
002A36r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x                 ; ( addr cp+1 u )
002A38r 3               
002A38r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_move
002A3Br 3               
002A3Br 3                               ; Return caddr
002A3Br 3  CA                           dex
002A3Cr 3  CA                           dex
002A3Dr 3  A5 rr                        lda cp
002A3Fr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002A41r 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
002A43r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002A45r 3               
002A45r 3                               ; Adjust CP
002A45r 3  68                           pla                     ; length of string
002A46r 3  18                           clc
002A47r 3  65 rr                        adc cp
002A49r 3  85 rr                        sta cp
002A4Br 3  A5 rr                        lda cp+1
002A4Dr 3  69 00                        adc #0                  ; we only need the carry
002A4Fr 3  85 rr                        sta cp+1
002A51r 3  60           z_word:         rts
002A52r 3               
002A52r 3               
002A52r 3               ; ## WORDLIST ( -- wid ) "Create new wordlist (from pool of 8)"
002A52r 3               ; ## "wordlist" auto ANS search
002A52r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/search/WORDLIST
002A52r 3                       ; See the tutorial on Wordlists and the Search Order for
002A52r 3                       ; more information.
002A52r 3                       ; """
002A52r 3               
002A52r 3               xt_wordlist:
002A52r 3                               ; Get the current number of wordlists
002A52r 3  A0 05                        ldy #num_wordlists_offset
002A54r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y      ; This is a byte variable, so only
002A56r 3                                               ; the LSB needs to be checked.
002A56r 3               
002A56r 3                               ; See if we are already at the max.
002A56r 3  C9 0C                        cmp #max_wordlists
002A58r 3  D0 05                        bne @ok
002A5Ar 3               
002A5Ar 3                               ; Print an error message if all wordlists used.
002A5Ar 3  A9 0B                        lda #err_wordlist
002A5Cr 3  4C rr rr                     jmp error
002A5Fr 3               
002A5Fr 3               @ok:
002A5Fr 3  1A                           inc             ; Increment the wordlist#
002A60r 3  91 rr                        sta (up),y      ; Save it into byte variable #wordlists
002A62r 3  CA                           dex             ; and put it on the stack.
002A63r 3  CA                           dex
002A64r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002A66r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x         ; 12 is the max, so upper byte is always zero.
002A68r 3               
002A68r 3  60           z_wordlist:     rts
002A69r 3               
002A69r 3               
002A69r 3               
002A69r 3               ; ## WORDS ( -- ) "Print known words from Dictionary"
002A69r 3               ; ## "words"  tested  ANS tools
002A69r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/tools/WORDS
002A69r 3                       ; This is pretty much only used at the command line so we can
002A69r 3                       ; be slow and try to save space.
002A69r 3                       ; """
002A69r 3               
002A69r 3               xt_words:
002A69r 3                               ; we follow Gforth by starting on the next
002A69r 3                               ; line
002A69r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002A6Cr 3               
002A6Cr 3                               ; We pretty-format the output by inserting a line break
002A6Cr 3                               ; before the end of the line. We can get away with pushing
002A6Cr 3                               ; the counter to the stack because this is usually an
002A6Cr 3                               ; interactive word and speed is not that important
002A6Cr 3  A9 00                        lda #0
002A6Er 3  48                           pha
002A6Fr 3               
002A6Fr 3                               ; Set up for traversing the wordlist search order.
002A6Fr 3  CA                           dex                     ; Make room on the stack for
002A70r 3  CA                           dex                     ; a dictionary pointer.
002A71r 3  64 rr                        stz tmp3                ; Start at the beginning of
002A73r 3                                                       ; the search order.
002A73r 3               @wordlist_loop:
002A73r 3  A0 1E                        ldy #num_order_offset   ; Check against byte variable #ORDER.
002A75r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp3
002A77r 3  D1 rr                        cmp (up),y              ; See if we are done.
002A79r 3  D0 02                        bne @have_wordlist
002A7Br 3               
002A7Br 3                               ; We ran out of wordlists to search.
002A7Br 3  80 44                        bra @words_done
002A7Dr 3               
002A7Dr 3               @have_wordlist:
002A7Dr 3                               ; start with last word in Dictionary
002A7Dr 3                               ; Get the current wordlist id
002A7Dr 3  18                           clc                     ; Index into byte array SEARCH-ORDER.
002A7Er 3  69 1F                        adc #search_order_offset
002A80r 3  A8                           tay
002A81r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y              ; Get the index into array WORDLISTS
002A83r 3               
002A83r 3                               ; Get the DP for that wordlist.
002A83r 3  0A                           asl                     ; Turn offset into cells offset.
002A84r 3  18                           clc
002A85r 3  69 06                        adc #wordlists_offset
002A87r 3  A8                           tay
002A88r 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y              ; Save the DP for this wordlist
002A8Ar 3  95 00                        sta 0,x                 ; on the stack. ( nt )
002A8Cr 3  C8                           iny
002A8Dr 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
002A8Fr 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002A91r 3               
002A91r 3               @loop:
002A91r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup              ; ( nt nt )
002A94r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_name_to_string   ; ( nt addr u )
002A97r 3               
002A97r 3                               ; Insert line break if we're about to go past the end of the
002A97r 3                               ; line
002A97r 3  68                           pla
002A98r 3  18                           clc
002A99r 3  75 00                        adc 0,x
002A9Br 3  1A                           inc                     ; don't forget the space between words
002A9Cr 3  C9 4F                        cmp #MAX_LINE_LENGTH    ; usually 79
002A9Er 3  90 05                        bcc @1
002AA0r 3               
002AA0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002AA3r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
002AA5r 3               @1:
002AA5r 3  48                           pha
002AA6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type             ; ( nt )
002AA9r 3               
002AA9r 3  A9 20                        lda #AscSP
002AABr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
002AAEr 3               
002AAEr 3                               ; get next word, which begins two down
002AAEr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one_plus         ; 1+
002AB1r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_one_plus         ; 1+
002AB4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch            ; @ ( nt+1 )
002AB7r 3               
002AB7r 3                               ; if next address is zero, we're done
002AB7r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002AB9r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002ABBr 3  D0 D4                        bne @loop
002ABDr 3               
002ABDr 3                               ; Move on to the next wordlist in the search order.
002ABDr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp3
002ABFr 3  80 B2                        bra @wordlist_loop
002AC1r 3               
002AC1r 3               @words_done:
002AC1r 3  68                           pla                     ; dump counter
002AC2r 3               
002AC2r 3  E8                           inx
002AC3r 3  E8                           inx
002AC4r 3               
002AC4r 3  60           z_words:        rts
002AC5r 3               
002AC5r 3               
002AC5r 3               
002AC5r 3               ; ## WORDSIZE ( nt -- u ) "Get size of word in bytes"
002AC5r 3               ; ## "wordsize"  auto  Tali Forth
002AC5r 3                       ; """Given an word's name token (nt), return the size of the
002AC5r 3                       ; word's payload size in bytes (CFA plus PFA) in bytes. Does not
002AC5r 3                       ; count the final RTS.
002AC5r 3                       ; """
002AC5r 3               xt_wordsize:
002AC5r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002AC8r 3               
002AC8r 3                               ; We get the start address of the word from its header entry
002AC8r 3                               ; for the start of the actual code (execution token, xt)
002AC8r 3                               ; which is four bytes down, and the pointer to the end of the
002AC8r 3                               ; code (z_word, six bytes down)
002AC8r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002ACAr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002ACCr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002ACEr 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
002AD0r 3               
002AD0r 3  A0 06                        ldy #6
002AD2r 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y    ; LSB of z
002AD4r 3  88                           dey
002AD5r 3  88                           dey
002AD6r 3               
002AD6r 3  38                           sec
002AD7r 3  F1 rr                        sbc (tmp1),y    ; LSB of xt
002AD9r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002ADBr 3               
002ADBr 3  A0 07                        ldy #7
002ADDr 3  B1 rr                        lda (tmp1),y    ; MSB of z
002ADFr 3  88                           dey
002AE0r 3  88                           dey
002AE1r 3               
002AE1r 3  F1 rr                        sbc (tmp1),y    ; MSB of xt
002AE3r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002AE5r 3               
002AE5r 3  60           z_wordsize:     rts
002AE6r 3               
002AE6r 3               
002AE6r 3               ; ## XOR ( n n -- n ) "Logically XOR TOS and NOS"
002AE6r 3               ; ## "xor"  auto  ANS core
002AE6r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/XOR"""
002AE6r 3               xt_xor:
002AE6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002AE9r 3               
002AE9r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002AEBr 3  55 02                        eor 2,x
002AEDr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002AEFr 3               
002AEFr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002AF1r 3  55 03                        eor 3,x
002AF3r 3  95 03                        sta 3,x
002AF5r 3               
002AF5r 3  E8                           inx
002AF6r 3  E8                           inx
002AF7r 3               
002AF7r 3  60           z_xor:          rts

002AF8r 3               ; ## ZERO ( -- 0 ) "Push 0 to Data Stack"
002AF8r 3               ; ## "0"  auto  Tali Forth
002AF8r 3                       ; """The disassembler assumes that this routine does not use Y. Note
002AF8r 3                       ; that CASE and FORTH-WORDLIST use the same routine, as the WD for Forth
002AF8r 3                       ; is 0."""
002AF8r 3               xt_case:
002AF8r 3               xt_forth_wordlist:
002AF8r 3               xt_zero:
002AF8r 3  CA                           dex             ; push
002AF9r 3  CA                           dex
002AFAr 3  74 00                        stz 0,x
002AFCr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002AFEr 3               z_case:
002AFEr 3               z_forth_wordlist:
002AFEr 3               z_zero:
002AFEr 3  60                           rts
002AFFr 3               
002AFFr 3               
002AFFr 3               ; ## ZERO_EQUAL ( n -- f ) "Check if TOS is zero"
002AFFr 3               ; ## "0="  auto  ANS core
002AFFr 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/ZeroEqual"""
002AFFr 3               
002AFFr 3               xt_zero_equal:
002AFFr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002B02r 3               
002B02r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002B04r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002B06r 3  F0 04                        beq @zero
002B08r 3               
002B08r 3                               ; not a zero, so we need a FALSE flag (0)
002B08r 3  A9 00                        lda #0
002B0Ar 3  80 02                        bra @store
002B0Cr 3               @zero:
002B0Cr 3                               ; We have a zero, so we need a TRUE flag (-1)
002B0Cr 3  A9 FF                        lda #$ff
002B0Er 3               @store:
002B0Er 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B10r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B12r 3               
002B12r 3  60           z_zero_equal:   rts
002B13r 3               
002B13r 3               
002B13r 3               
002B13r 3               ; ## ZERO_GREATER ( n -- f ) "Return a TRUE flag if TOS is positive"
002B13r 3               ; ## "0>"  auto  ANS core ext
002B13r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Zeromore"""
002B13r 3               
002B13r 3               xt_zero_greater:
002B13r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002B16r 3               
002B16r 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; Default is FALSE (TOS is negative)
002B18r 3               
002B18r 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB
002B1Ar 3  30 05                        bmi @done       ; TOS is negative, keep FLASE
002B1Cr 3  15 00                        ora 0,x
002B1Er 3  F0 01                        beq @done       ; TOS is zero, keep FALSE
002B20r 3               
002B20r 3  88                           dey             ; TOS is postive, make true
002B21r 3               @done:
002B21r 3  98                           tya
002B22r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B24r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B26r 3               
002B26r 3  60           z_zero_greater: rts
002B27r 3               
002B27r 3               
002B27r 3               
002B27r 3               ; ## ZERO_LESS ( n -- f ) "Return a TRUE flag if TOS negative"
002B27r 3               ; ## "0<"  auto  ANS core
002B27r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Zeroless"""
002B27r 3               
002B27r 3               xt_zero_less:
002B27r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002B2Ar 3               
002B2Ar 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; Default is FALSE (TOS positive)
002B2Cr 3               
002B2Cr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x         ; MSB
002B2Er 3  10 01                        bpl @done       ; TOS is positive, so keep FALSE
002B30r 3               
002B30r 3  88                           dey             ; TOS is negative, make TRUE
002B31r 3               @done:
002B31r 3  98                           tya
002B32r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B34r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B36r 3               
002B36r 3  60           z_zero_less:    rts
002B37r 3               
002B37r 3               
002B37r 3               
002B37r 3               ; ## ZERO_UNEQUAL ( m -- f ) "Return TRUE flag if not zero"
002B37r 3               ; ## "0<>"  auto  ANS core ext
002B37r 3                       ; """https://forth-standard.org/standard/core/Zerone"""
002B37r 3               
002B37r 3               xt_zero_unequal:
002B37r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002B3Ar 3               
002B3Ar 3  A0 00                        ldy #0          ; default false
002B3Cr 3               
002B3Cr 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002B3Er 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002B40r 3  F0 01                        beq @got_zero
002B42r 3               
002B42r 3  88                           dey
002B43r 3               @got_zero:
002B43r 3  98                           tya
002B44r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B46r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B48r 3

002B49r 3               ; ==========================================================
002B49r 3               ; EDITOR words
002B49r 3               
002B49r 3               ; This routine is used by both enter-screen and erase-screen
002B49r 3               ; to get a buffer for the given screen number and set SCR to
002B49r 3               ; the given screen number.  This word is not in the dictionary.
002B49r 3               xt_editor_screen_helper:
002B49r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
002B4Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_scr
002B4Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_store
002B52r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_buffer
002B55r 3               z_editor_screen_helper:
002B55r 3  60                           rts
002B56r 3               
002B56r 3               
002B56r 3               ; ## EDITOR_ENTER_SCREEN ( scr# -- ) "Enter all lines for given screen"
002B56r 3               ; ## "enter-screen"  auto  Tali Editor
002B56r 3               
002B56r 3               xt_editor_enter_screen:
002B56r 3                               ; Set the variable SCR and get a buffer for the
002B56r 3                               ; given screen number.
002B56r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_screen_helper
002B59r 3               
002B59r 3                               ; Drop the buffer address.
002B59r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_drop
002B5Cr 3               
002B5Cr 3                               ; Overwrite the lines one at a time.
002B5Cr 3  64 rr                        stz editor1
002B5Er 3               @prompt_loop:
002B5Er 3                               ; Put the current line number on the stack.
002B5Er 3  CA                           dex
002B5Fr 3  CA                           dex
002B60r 3  A5 rr                        lda editor1
002B62r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B64r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002B66r 3               
002B66r 3                               ; Use the O word to prompt for overwrite.
002B66r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_o
002B69r 3               
002B69r 3                               ; Move on to the next line.
002B69r 3  E6 rr                        inc editor1
002B6Br 3  A9 10                        lda #16
002B6Dr 3  C5 rr                        cmp editor1
002B6Fr 3  D0 ED                        bne @prompt_loop
002B71r 3               
002B71r 3               z_editor_enter_screen:
002B71r 3  60                           rts
002B72r 3               
002B72r 3               
002B72r 3               
002B72r 3               ; ## EDITOR_ERASE_SCREEN ( scr# -- ) "Erase all lines for given screen"
002B72r 3               ; ## "erase-screen"  tested  Tali Editor
002B72r 3               xt_editor_erase_screen:
002B72r 3                               ; Set the variable SCR and get a buffer for the
002B72r 3                               ; given screen number.
002B72r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_screen_helper

002B75r 3  CA                           dex
002B76r 3  CA                           dex

002B7Br 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002B7Dr 3

002B7Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_blank
002B80r 3               
002B80r 3                               ; Mark buffer as updated.
002B80r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_update
002B83r 3

002B84r 3               xt_editor_el:

002B84r 3                               ; This also loads the block into the buffer if it's
002B84r 3                               ; not there for some reason.
002B84r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_line
002B87r 3

002B87r 3  CA                           dex

002B8Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_blank
002B92r 3               
002B92r 3                               ; Mark buffer as updated.
002B92r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_update
002B95r 3               
002B95r 3  60           z_editor_el:    rts
002B96r 3               
002B96r 3               
002B96r 3               ; ## EDITOR_L ( -- ) "List the current screen"
002B96r 3               ; ## "l"  tested  Tali Editor
002B96r 3               
002B96r 3               xt_editor_l:
002B96r 3                               ; Load the current screen
002B96r 3  CA                           dex             ; Put SCR on the stack.
002B97r 3  CA                           dex
002B98r 3  A0 02                        ldy #scr_offset
002B9Ar 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
002B9Cr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002B9Er 3  C8                           iny
002B9Fr 3  B1 rr                        lda (up),y
002BA1r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002BA3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_block    ; Get the current screen.
002BA6r 3               
002BA6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002BA9r 3               
002BA9r 3                               ; Print the screen number.
002BA9r 3                               ; We're using sliteral, so we need to set up the
002BA9r 3                               ; appropriate data structure (see sliteral)
002BA9r 3  80 08                        bra @after_screen_msg
002BABr 3               
002BABr 3               @screen_msg:
002BABr 3  53 63 72 65                  .byte "Screen #"
002BAFr 3  65 6E 20 23  
002BB3r 3               
002BB3r 3               @after_screen_msg:
002BB3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr sliteral_runtime
002BB6r 3  rr rr 08 00                  .word @screen_msg, @after_screen_msg-@screen_msg
002BBAr 3               
002BBAr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
002BBDr 3               
002BBDr 3                               ; Put the screen number and printed size for u.r on the stack.
002BBDr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_scr
002BC0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch
002BC3r 3  CA                           dex
002BC4r 3  CA                           dex
002BC5r 3  A9 04                        lda #4          ; four spaces
002BC7r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002BC9r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002BCBr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_u_dot_r
002BCEr 3               
002BCEr 3                               ; The address of the buffer is currently on the stack.
002BCEr 3                               ; Print 64 chars at a time. TYPE uses tmp1, so we'll
002BCEr 3                               ; keep track of the line number in tmp3.
002BCEr 3  64 rr                        stz tmp3
002BD0r 3               
002BD0r 3               @line_loop:
002BD0r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002BD3r 3               
002BD3r 3                               ; Print the line number (2-space fixed width)
002BD3r 3  CA                           dex
002BD4r 3  CA                           dex
002BD5r 3  CA                           dex
002BD6r 3  CA                           dex
002BD7r 3  74 03                        stz 3,x
002BD9r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp3
002BDBr 3  95 02                        sta 2,x
002BDDr 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002BDFr 3  A9 02                        lda #2
002BE1r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002BE3r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_u_dot_r
002BE6r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
002BE9r 3               
002BE9r 3                               ; Print one line using the address on the stack.
002BE9r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
002BECr 3  CA                           dex
002BEDr 3  CA                           dex
002BEEr 3  A9 40                        lda #64
002BF0r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002BF2r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002BF4r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_type
002BF7r 3               
002BF7r 3                               ; Add 64 to the address on the stack to move to the next line.
002BF7r 3  18                           clc
002BF8r 3  A9 40                        lda #64
002BFAr 3  75 00                        adc 0,x
002BFCr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002BFEr 3  B5 01                        lda 1,x
002C00r 3  69 00                        adc #0      ; Add carry
002C02r 3  95 01                        sta 1,x
002C04r 3               
002C04r 3                               ; Increment the line number (held in tmp3)
002C04r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp3
002C06r 3               
002C06r 3                               ; See if we are done.
002C06r 3  A5 rr                        lda tmp3
002C08r 3  C9 10                        cmp #16
002C0Ar 3  D0 C4                        bne @line_loop
002C0Cr 3               
002C0Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002C0Fr 3                               ; Drop the address on the stack.
002C0Fr 3  E8                           inx
002C10r 3  E8                           inx
002C11r 3               
002C11r 3  60           z_editor_l:            rts
002C12r 3               
002C12r 3               
002C12r 3               
002C12r 3               ; ## EDITOR_LINE ( line# -- c-addr ) "Turn a line number into address in current screen"
002C12r 3               ; ## "line"  tested  Tali Editor
002C12r 3               
002C12r 3               xt_editor_line:
002C12r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002C15r 3               
002C15r 3                               ; Multiply the TOS by 64 (chars/line) to compute offset.
002C15r 3  A0 06                        ldy #6          ; *64 is same as left shift 6 times.
002C17r 3               @shift_tos_left:
002C17r 3  16 00                        asl 0,x         ; Shift TOS to the left
002C19r 3  36 01                        rol 1,x         ; ROL brings MSb from lower byte.
002C1Br 3  88                           dey
002C1Cr 3  D0 F9                        bne @shift_tos_left
002C1Er 3                               ; Load the current screen into a buffer
002C1Er 3                               ; and get the buffer address
002C1Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_scr
002C21r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_fetch
002C24r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_block
002C27r 3               
002C27r 3                               ; Add the offset to the buffer base address.
002C27r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_plus
002C2Ar 3               
002C2Ar 3  60           z_editor_line:  rts
002C2Br 3               
002C2Br 3               
002C2Br 3               
002C2Br 3               ; ## EDITOR_O ( line# -- ) "Overwrite the given line"
002C2Br 3               ; ## "o"  tested  Tali Editor
002C2Br 3               xt_editor_o:
002C2Br 3                               ; Print prompt
002C2Br 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_cr
002C2Er 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
002C31r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_two
002C34r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_u_dot_r
002C37r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
002C3Ar 3  A9 2A                        lda #42         ; ASCII for *
002C3Cr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr emit_a
002C3Fr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_space
002C42r 3               
002C42r 3                               ; Accept new input (directly into the buffer)
002C42r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_editor_line
002C45r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup      ; Save a copy of the line address for later.
002C48r 3  CA                           dex
002C49r 3  CA                           dex
002C4Ar 3  A9 40                        lda #64         ; chars/line
002C4Cr 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002C4Er 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002C50r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_accept
002C53r 3               
002C53r 3                               ; Fill the rest with spaces.
002C53r 3                               ; Stack is currently ( line_address numchars_from_accept )
002C53r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_dup
002C56r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_not_rote ; -rot
002C59r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_plus
002C5Cr 3  CA                           dex
002C5Dr 3  CA                           dex
002C5Er 3  A9 40                        lda #64         ; chars/line
002C60r 3  95 00                        sta 0,x
002C62r 3  74 01                        stz 1,x
002C64r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_rot
002C67r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_minus
002C6Ar 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_blank
002C6Dr 3               
002C6Dr 3                               ; Mark buffer as updated.
002C6Dr 3  20 rr rr                     jsr xt_update
002C70r 3               
002C70r 3  60           z_editor_o:     rts
002C71r 3               
002C71r 3               ; ## LCDPUT ( s -- ) "Print single character to LCD"
002C71r 3               ; ## "lcdput" coded Custom
002C71r 3               xt_lcdput:
002C71r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_1
002C74r 3               
002C74r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002C76r 3                       .ifdef lcd_print
002C76r 3                               jsr lcd_print
002C76r 3                       .endif
002C76r 3  E8                           inx
002C77r 3  E8                           inx
002C78r 3  60           z_lcdput: rts
002C79r 3               
002C79r 3               
002C79r 3               ; ## LCDPRINT ( addr u -- ) "Print string to LCD"
002C79r 3               ; ## "lcdprint"  coded Custom
002C79r 3               
002C79r 3               xt_lcdprint:
002C79r 3  20 rr rr                     jsr underflow_2
002C7Cr 3               
002C7Cr 3                               ; Save the starting address into tmp1
002C7Cr 3  B5 02                        lda 2,x
002C7Er 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1
002C80r 3  B5 03                        lda 3,x
002C82r 3  85 rr                        sta tmp1+1
002C84r 3               @loop:
002C84r 3                               ; done if length is zero
002C84r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002C86r 3  15 01                        ora 1,x
002C88r 3  F0 12                        beq @done
002C8Ar 3               
002C8Ar 3                               ; Send the current character
002C8Ar 3  B2 rr                        lda (tmp1)
002C8Cr 3                       .ifdef lcd_print
002C8Cr 3                               jsr lcd_print      ; avoids stack foolery
002C8Cr 3                       .endif
002C8Cr 3                               ; Move the address along (in tmp1)
002C8Cr 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1
002C8Er 3  D0 02                        bne @1
002C90r 3  E6 rr                        inc tmp1+1
002C92r 3               @1:
002C92r 3                               ; Reduce the count (on the data stack)
002C92r 3  B5 00                        lda 0,x
002C94r 3  D0 02                        bne @2
002C96r 3  D6 01                        dec 1,x
002C98r 3               @2:
002C98r 3  D6 00                        dec 0,x
002C9Ar 3               
002C9Ar 3  80 E8                        bra @loop
002C9Cr 3               @done:
002C9Cr 3  E8                           inx
002C9Dr 3  E8                           inx
002C9Er 3  E8                           inx
002C9Fr 3  E8                           inx
002CA0r 3               
002CA0r 3  60           z_lcdprint:         rts

002CC0r 3

002CC3r 3                       .ifdef sd_readsector

002CC3r 3                               lda 3, X

002CC3r 3                       .endif

002CC5r 3  74 01                        stz 1,X         ;reset value there

002CE1r 3                               lda #<textfile

002CE1r 3                               lda #>textfile

002CE1r 3                               bne @error

002CE1r 3                               bne @error
002CE1r 3                               dex
002CE1r 3                               dex
002CE1r 3                               lda sd_buffer_address
002CE1r 3                               sta 0,x
002CE1r 3                               lda sd_buffer_address+1
002CE1r 3                               sta 1, x

002CE1r 3                               beq @end
002CE1r 3                           .endif
002CE1r 3               .endif

002CF5r 3               
002CF5r 3               ; ## cf_fat_init ( addr -- ) "Initialize FAT16 on CF card at specified address"
002CF5r 3               ; ## "cf_fat_init" coded Custom
002CF5r 3               xt_cf_fat_init:
002CF5r 3               check_fat_sector_signature:
002CF5r 3               
002CF5r 3               .ifdef cf_init
002CF5r 3                       ; jsr underflow_1
002CF5r 3                       ; save CF card address
002CF5r 3                       ; lda 0, x
002CF5r 3                       ; sta CF_ADDRESS
002CF5r 3                       ; lda 1, x
002CF5r 3                       ; sta CF_ADDRESS + 1
002CF5r 3               
002CF5r 3                       ; initialize CF card
002CF5r 3  20 rr rr             jsr cf_init
002CF8r 3                       ; prepare to read first sector
002CF8r 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_LBA
002CFBr 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_LBA + 1
002CFEr 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_LBA + 2
002D01r 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_LBA + 3
002D04r 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_CURRENT_CLUSTER                  ; reset variables
002D07r 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_CURRENT_CLUSTER + 1
002D0Ar 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_CURRENT_DIR_SEC
002D0Dr 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_CURRENT_DIR_SEC + 1
002D10r 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_CURRENT_DIR_SEC + 2
002D13r 3  9C rr rr             stz CF_CURRENT_DIR_SEC + 3
002D16r 3               
002D16r 3                       ; LBA is set, now read sector
002D16r 3  20 rr rr             jsr cf_read_sector
002D19r 3                       ; we now have the first sector in FAT_BUFFER
002D19r 3               .ifdef check_fat_sector_signature
002D19r 3                       ; check signature
002D19r 3  AD rr rr             lda FAT_BUFFER + $1FE
002D1Cr 3  C9 55                cmp #$55
002D1Er 3  D0 07                bne @sigerr
002D20r 3  AD rr rr             lda FAT_BUFFER + $1FF
002D23r 3  C9 AA                cmp #$AA
002D25r 3  F0 03                beq @sigok
002D27r 3               @sigerr:
002D27r 3  4C rr rr             jmp cf_fat_init_error
002D2Ar 3               @sigok:
002D2Ar 3               .endif
002D2Ar 3                       ; check if this is MBR or FAT start sector
002D2Ar 3  AD rr rr             lda FAT_BUFFER + 54
002D2Dr 3  C9 46                cmp #'F'
002D2Fr 3  D0 10                bne @read_fat_sector
002D31r 3  AD rr rr             lda FAT_BUFFER + 55
002D34r 3  C9 41                cmp #'A'
002D36r 3  D0 09                bne @read_fat_sector
002D38r 3  AD rr rr             lda FAT_BUFFER + 56
002D3Br 3  C9 54                cmp #'T'
002D3Dr 3  D0 02                bne @read_fat_sector
002D3Fr 3               
002D3Fr 3  80 38                bra @is_fat_sector
002D41r 3               
002D41r 3               @read_fat_sector:
002D41r 3               
002D41r 3                       ; read FAT start sector
002D41r 3                       ; and save to sector address to read
002D41r 3  AD rr rr             lda FAT_BUFFER + 454
002D44r 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_LBA
002D47r 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_PART_START
002D4Ar 3  AD rr rr             lda FAT_BUFFER + 455
002D4Dr 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_LBA + 1
002D50r 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_PART_START + 1

002D5Fr 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_LBA + 3
002D62r 3  8D rr rr             sta CF_PART_START + 3

002D65r 3                       ; LBA is set, now read sector
002D65r 3  20 rr rr             jsr cf_read_sector
002D68r 3                       ; We now have the FAT start sector in the buffer
002D68r 3               .ifdef check_fat_sector_signature

002D6Br 3  C9 55                cmp #$55

002DACr 3

002DACr 3                       ; RootDirSectors = ((BPB_RootEntCnt * 32) + (BPB_BytsPerSec  1)) / BPB_BytsPerSec;
002DACr 3  AD rr rr 8D          cp16 CF_ROOT_ENT_CNT, CF_ROOT_DIR_SECS

003130r 3               
003130r 2                   .include "headers.s"          ; Headers of native words
003130r 3               ; Dictionary Headers for Tali Forth 2
003130r 3               ; Scot W. Stevenson <scot.stevenson@gmail.com>
003130r 3               ; First version: 05. Dec 2016 (Liara Forth)
003130r 3               ; This version: 29. Dec 2018
003130r 3               
003130r 3               ; Dictionary headers are kept separately from the code, which allows various
003130r 3               ; tricks in the code. We roughly follow the Gforth terminology: The Execution
003130r 3               ; Token (xt) is the address of the first byte of a word's code that can be, uh,
003130r 3               ; executed; the Name Token (nt) is a pointer to the beginning of the word's
003130r 3               ; header in the Dictionary. There the link to the next word in the Dictionary
003130r 3               ; is always one cell down from the current word's own nt. In the code itself,
003130r 3               ; we use "nt_<WORD>" for the nt and "xt_<WORD>" for the xt.
003130r 3               
003130r 3               ; This gives us the following header structure:
003130r 3               
003130r 3               ;              8 bit     8 bit
003130r 3               ;               LSB       MSB
003130r 3               ; nt_word ->  +--------+--------+
003130r 3               ;          +0 | Length | Status |
003130r 3               ;             +--------+--------+
003130r 3               ;          +2 | Next Header     | -> nt_next_word
003130r 3               ;             +-----------------+
003130r 3               ;          +4 | Start of Code   | -> xt_word
003130r 3               ;             +-----------------+
003130r 3               ;          +6 | End of Code     | -> z_word
003130r 3               ;             +--------+--------+
003130r 3               ;          +8 | Name   |        |
003130r 3               ;             +--------+--------+
003130r 3               ;             |        |        |
003130r 3               ;             +--------+--------+
003130r 3               ;             |        |  ...   | (name string does not end with a zero)
003130r 3               ;          +n +--------+--------+
003130r 3               
003130r 3               ; The Status Byte is created by adding the flags defined in definitions.asm,
003130r 3               ; which are:
003130r 3               
003130r 3               ;       CO - Compile Only
003130r 3               ;       IM - Immediate Word
003130r 3               ;       NN - Never Native Compile (must always be called by JSR)
003130r 3               ;       AN - Always Native Compile (may not be called by JSR)
003130r 3               ;       UF - Contains underflow check
003130r 3               ;       HC - Has CFA (words created by CREATE and DOES> only)
003130r 3               
003130r 3               ; Note there are currently two bits unused.
003130r 3               
003130r 3               ; By default, all existing words can be natively compiled (compiled inline) or
003130r 3               ; as a subroutine jump target; the system decides which variant to use based on
003130r 3               ; a threshold the user can set. By default, all user-created words are flagged
003130r 3               ; never-native. The user can override this by using the always-native word
003130r 3               ; just after defining their new word.  The NN flag forbids native compiling,
003130r 3               ; the AN flag forces it.
003130r 3               
003130r 3               ; The last word (top word in code) is always BYE. It is marked as the last word
003130r 3               ; by its value of 0000 in its Next Header field. The words are sorted with the
003130r 3               ; more common ones first (further down in code) so they are found earlier.
003130r 3               ; Anything to do with output comes later (further up) because things will
003130r 3               ; always be slow if there is a human involved.
003130r 3               
003130r 3               ; The initial skeleton of this list was automatically generated by a script
003130r 3               ; in the tools folder and then sorted by hand.
003130r 3               
003130r 3               nt_bye:
003130r 3  03                   .byte 3         ; length of word strings
003131r 3  00                   .byte 0         ; status byte
003132r 3  00 00                .word 0000      ; next word in Dictionary, 0000 signals end
003134r 3  rr rr                .word xt_bye    ; start of code block (xt of this word)
003136r 3  rr rr                .word z_bye     ; end of code (RTS)
003138r 3  62 79 65             .byte "bye"     ; word name, always lower case, not zero-terminated
00313Br 3               
00313Br 3               
00313Br 3               nt_cold:
00313Br 3  04 00                .byte 4, 0
00313Dr 3  rr rr rr rr          .word nt_bye, xt_cold, z_cold
003141r 3  rr rr        
003143r 3  63 6F 6C 64          .byte "cold"
003147r 3

00403Cr 3               
00403Cr 3               ; ; ASSEMBLER-WORDLIST
00403Cr 3               
00403Cr 3               ; ; Labels for the opcodes have the format "nt_asm_<OPC>" where a futher
00403Cr 3               ; ; underscore replaces any dot present in the SAN mnemonic. The hash sign for
00403Cr 3               ; ; immediate addressing is replaced by an "h" (for example, the label code for
00403Cr 3               ; ; "lda.#" is "xt_adm_lda_h"). All opcodes are immediate.
00403Cr 3               assembler_dictionary_start:
00403Cr 3               ; nt_asm_adc_h:
00403Cr 3               ; 		.byte 5, IM
00403Cr 3               ;                 .word nt_asm_adc_x
