0049F3r 2               
0049F3r 2               
0049F3r 2               ; =====================================================================
0049F3r 2               ; COMPILE WORDS, JUMPS and SUBROUTINE JUMPS INTO CODE
0049F3r 2               
0049F3r 2               ; These three routines compile instructions such as "jsr xt_words" into a word
0049F3r 2               ; at compile time so they are available at run time. Words that use this
0049F3r 2               ; routine may not be natively compiled. We use "cmpl" as not to confuse these
0049F3r 2               ; routines with the COMPILE, word. Always call this with a subroutine jump.
0049F3r 2               ; This means combining JSR/RTS to JMP in those cases is not going to work. To
0049F3r 2               ; use, load the LSB of the address in A and the MSB in Y. You can remember
0049F3r 2               ; which comes first by thinking of the song "Young Americans" ("YA") by David
0049F3r 2               ; Bowie.
0049F3r 2               
0049F3r 2               ;               ldy #>addr      ; MSB   ; "Young"
0049F3r 2               ;               lda #<addr      ; LSB   ; "Americans"
0049F3r 2               ;               jsr cmpl_subroutine
0049F3r 2               
0049F3r 2               ; Also, we keep a routine here to compile a single byte passed through A.
0049F3r 2               
0049F3r 2               cmpl_subroutine:
0049F3r 2                   ; This is the entry point to compile JSR <ADDR>
0049F3r 2  48               pha             ; save LSB of address
0049F4r 2  A9 20            lda #$20        ; load opcode for JSR
0049F6r 2  80 03            bra cmpl_common
0049F8r 2               cmpl_jump:
0049F8r 2                   ; This is the entry point to compile JMP <ADDR>
0049F8r 2  48               pha             ; save LSB of address
0049F9r 2  A9 4C            lda #$4c        ; load opcode for JMP, fall thru to cmpl_common
0049FBr 2               cmpl_common:
0049FBr 2                   ; At this point, A contains the opcode to be compiled,
0049FBr 2                   ; the LSB of the address is on the 65c02 stack, and the MSB of
0049FBr 2                   ; the address is in Y
0049FBr 2  20 rr rr         jsr cmpl_a      ; compile opcode
0049FEr 2  68               pla             ; retrieve address LSB; fall thru to cmpl_word
0049FFr 2               cmpl_word:
0049FFr 2                   ; This is the entry point to compile a word (little-endian)
0049FFr 2  20 rr rr         jsr cmpl_a      ; compile LSB of address
004A02r 2  98               tya             ; fall thru for MSB
004A03r 2               cmpl_a:
004A03r 2                   ; This is the entry point to compile a single byte which
004A03r 2                   ; is passed in A. The built-in assembler assumes that this
004A03r 2                   ; routine does not modify Y.
004A03r 2  92 rr            sta (cp)
004A05r 2  E6 rr            inc cp
004A07r 2  D0 02            bne _done
004A09r 2  E6 rr            inc cp+1
004A0Br 2               _done:
004A0Br 2  60               rts
004A0Cr 2               
004A0Cr 2               
004A0Cr 2               
004A0Cr 2               ; =====================================================================
004A0Cr 2               ; CODE FIELD ROUTINES
004A0Cr 2               
004A0Cr 2               doconst:
004A0Cr 2               ; """Execute a CONSTANT: Push the data in the first two bytes of
004A0Cr 2               ; the Data Field onto the Data Stack
004A0Cr 2               ; """
004A0Cr 2  CA               dex             ; make room for constant
004A0Dr 2  CA               dex
004A0Er 2               
004A0Er 2                   ; The value we need is stored in the two bytes after the
004A0Er 2                   ; JSR return address, which in turn is what is on top of
004A0Er 2                   ; the Return Stack
004A0Er 2  68               pla             ; LSB of return address
004A0Fr 2  85 rr            sta tmp1
004A11r 2  68               pla             ; MSB of return address
004A12r 2  85 rr            sta tmp1+1
004A14r 2               
004A14r 2                   ; Start LDY with 1 instead of 0 because of how JSR stores
004A14r 2                   ; the return address on the 65c02
004A14r 2  A0 01            ldy #1
004A16r 2  B1 rr            lda (tmp1),y
004A18r 2  95 00            sta 0,x
004A1Ar 2  C8               iny
004A1Br 2  B1 rr            lda (tmp1),y
004A1Dr 2  95 01            sta 1,x
004A1Fr 2               
004A1Fr 2                   ; This takes us back to the original caller, not the
004A1Fr 2                   ; DOCONST caller
004A1Fr 2  60               rts
004A20r 2               
004A20r 2               
004A20r 2               dodefer:
004A20r 2               ; """Execute a DEFER statement at runtime: Execute the address we
004A20r 2               ; find after the caller in the Data Field
004A20r 2               ; """
004A20r 2                   ; The xt we need is stored in the two bytes after the JSR
004A20r 2                   ; return address, which is what is on top of the Return
004A20r 2                   ; Stack. So all we have to do is replace our return jump
004A20r 2                   ; with what we find there
004A20r 2  68               pla             ; LSB
004A21r 2  85 rr            sta tmp1
004A23r 2  68               pla             ; MSB
004A24r 2  85 rr            sta tmp1+1
004A26r 2               
004A26r 2  A0 01            ldy #1
004A28r 2  B1 rr            lda (tmp1),y
004A2Ar 2  85 rr            sta tmp2
004A2Cr 2  C8               iny
004A2Dr 2  B1 rr            lda (tmp1),y
004A2Fr 2  85 rr            sta tmp2+1
004A31r 2               
004A31r 2  6C rr rr         jmp (tmp2)      ; This is actually a jump to the new target
004A34r 2               
004A34r 2               defer_error:
004A34r 2                   ; """Error routine for undefined DEFER: Complain and abort"""
004A34r 2  A9 03            lda #err_defer
004A36r 2  4C rr rr         jmp error
004A39r 2               
004A39r 2               dodoes:
004A39r 2               ; """Execute the runtime portion of DOES>. See DOES> and
004A39r 2               ; docs/create-does.txt for details and
004A39r 2               ; http://www.bradrodriguez.com/papers/moving3.htm
004A39r 2               ; """
004A39r 2                   ; Assumes the address of the CFA of the original defining word
004A39r 2                   ; (say, CONSTANT) is on the top of the Return Stack. Save it
004A39r 2                   ; for a later jump, adding one byte because of the way the
004A39r 2                   ; 6502 works
004A39r 2  7A               ply             ; LSB
004A3Ar 2  68               pla             ; MSB
004A3Br 2  C8               iny
004A3Cr 2  D0 01            bne @1
004A3Er 2  1A               inc
004A3Fr 2               @1:
004A3Fr 2  84 rr            sty tmp2
004A41r 2  85 rr            sta tmp2+1
004A43r 2               
004A43r 2                   ; Next on the Return Stack should be the address of the PFA of
004A43r 2                   ; the calling defined word (say, the name of whatever constant we
004A43r 2                   ; just defined). Move this to the Data Stack, again adding one.
004A43r 2  CA               dex
004A44r 2  CA               dex
004A45r 2               
004A45r 2  7A               ply
004A46r 2  68               pla
004A47r 2  C8               iny
004A48r 2  D0 01            bne @2
004A4Ar 2  1A               inc
004A4Br 2               @2:
004A4Br 2  94 00            sty 0,x         ; LSB
004A4Dr 2  95 01            sta 1,x         ; MSB
004A4Fr 2               
004A4Fr 2                   ; This leaves the return address from the original main routine
004A4Fr 2                   ; on top of the Return Stack. We leave that untouched and jump
004A4Fr 2                   ; to the special code of the defining word. It's RTS instruction
004A4Fr 2                   ; will take us back to the main routine
004A4Fr 2  6C rr rr         jmp (tmp2)
004A52r 2               
004A52r 2               
004A52r 2               dovar:
004A52r 2               ; """Execute a variable: Push the address of the first bytes of
004A52r 2               ; the Data Field onto the stack. This is called with JSR so we
004A52r 2               ; can pick up the address of the calling variable off the 65c02's
004A52r 2               ; stack. The final RTS takes us to the original caller of the
004A52r 2               ; routine that itself called DOVAR. This is the default
004A52r 2               ; routine installed with CREATE.
004A52r 2               ; """
004A52r 2                   ; Pull the return address off the machine's stack, adding
004A52r 2                   ; one because of the way the 65c02 handles subroutines
004A52r 2  7A               ply             ; LSB
004A53r 2  68               pla             ; MSB
004A54r 2  C8               iny
004A55r 2  D0 01            bne @1
004A57r 2  1A               inc
004A58r 2               @1:
004A58r 2  CA               dex
004A59r 2  CA               dex
004A5Ar 2               
004A5Ar 2  95 01            sta 1,x
004A5Cr 2  98               tya
004A5Dr 2  95 00            sta 0,x
004A5Fr 2               
004A5Fr 2  60               rts
004A60r 2               
004A60r 2               ; =====================================================================
004A60r 2               ; LOW LEVEL HELPER FUNCTIONS
004A60r 2               
004A60r 2               byte_to_ascii:
004A60r 2               ; """Convert byte in A to two ASCII hex digits and EMIT them"""
004A60r 2               .scope
004A60r 2  48               pha
004A61r 2  4A               lsr             ; convert high nibble first
004A62r 2  4A               lsr
004A63r 2  4A               lsr
004A64r 2  4A               lsr
004A65r 2  20 rr rr         jsr _nibble_to_ascii
004A68r 2  68               pla
004A69r 2               
004A69r 2                   ; fall through to _nibble_to_ascii
004A69r 2               
004A69r 2               _nibble_to_ascii:
004A69r 2               ; """Private helper function for byte_to_ascii: Print lower nibble
004A69r 2               ; of A and and EMIT it. This does the actual work.
004A69r 2               ; """
004A69r 2  29 0F            and #$0F
004A6Br 2  09 30            ora #'0'
004A6Dr 2  C9 3A            cmp #$3A        ; '9+1
004A6Fr 2  90 02            bcc @1
004A71r 2  69 06            adc #$06
004A73r 2               
004A73r 2  4C rr rr     @1:               jmp emit_a
004A76r 2               
004A76r 2  60               rts
004A77r 2               .endscope
004A77r 2               
004A77r 2               compare_16bit:
004A77r 2               ; """Compare TOS/NOS and return results in form of the 65c02 flags
004A77r 2               ; Adapted from Leventhal "6502 Assembly Language Subroutines", see
004A77r 2               ; also http://www.6502.org/tutorials/compare_beyond.html
004A77r 2               ; For signed numbers, Z signals equality and N which number is larger:
004A77r 2               ;       if TOS = NOS: Z=1 and N=0
004A77r 2               ;       if TOS > NOS: Z=0 and N=0
004A77r 2               ;       if TOS < NOS: Z=0 and N=1
004A77r 2               ; For unsigned numbers, Z signals equality and C which number is larger:
004A77r 2               ;       if TOS = NOS: Z=1 and N=0
004A77r 2               ;       if TOS > NOS: Z=0 and C=1
004A77r 2               ;       if TOS < NOS: Z=0 and C=0
004A77r 2               ; Compared to the book routine, WORD1 (MINUED) is TOS
004A77r 2               ;                               WORD2 (SUBTRAHEND) is NOS
004A77r 2               ; """
004A77r 2               .scope
004A77r 2                   ; Compare LSB first to set the carry flag
004A77r 2  B5 00            lda 0,x                 ; LSB of TOS
004A79r 2  D5 02            cmp 2,x                 ; LSB of NOS
004A7Br 2  F0 0A            beq _equal
004A7Dr 2               
004A7Dr 2                   ; LSBs are not equal, compare MSB
004A7Dr 2  B5 01            lda 1,x                 ; MSB of TOS
004A7Fr 2  F5 03            sbc 3,x                 ; MSB of NOS
004A81r 2  09 01            ora #1                  ; Make zero flag 0 because not equal
004A83r 2  70 08            bvs _overflow
004A85r 2  80 08            bra _not_equal
004A87r 2               _equal:
004A87r 2                   ; Low bytes are equal, so we compare high bytes
004A87r 2  B5 01            lda 1,x                 ; MSB of TOS
004A89r 2  F5 03            sbc 3,x                 ; MSB of NOS
004A8Br 2  50 04            bvc _done
004A8Dr 2               _overflow:
004A8Dr 2                   ; Handle overflow because we use signed numbers
004A8Dr 2  49 80            eor #$80                ; complement negative flag
004A8Fr 2               _not_equal:
004A8Fr 2  09 01            ora #1                  ; if overflow, we can't be eqal
004A91r 2               _done:
004A91r 2  60               rts
004A92r 2               .endscope
004A92r 2               
004A92r 2               current_to_dp:
004A92r 2               ; """Look up the current (compilation) dictionary pointer
004A92r 2               ; in the wordlist set and put it into the dp zero-page
004A92r 2               ; variable. Uses A and Y.
004A92r 2               ; """
004A92r 2                   ; Determine which wordlist is current
004A92r 2  A0 04            ldy #current_offset
004A94r 2  B1 rr            lda (up),y      ; current is a byte variable
004A96r 2  0A               asl             ; turn it into an offset (in cells)
004A97r 2               
004A97r 2                   ; Get the dictionary pointer for that wordlist.
004A97r 2  18               clc
004A98r 2  69 06            adc #wordlists_offset   ; add offset to wordlists base.
004A9Ar 2  A8               tay
004A9Br 2  B1 rr            lda (up),y              ; get the dp for that wordlist.
004A9Dr 2  85 rr            sta dp
004A9Fr 2  C8               iny
004AA0r 2  B1 rr            lda (up),y
004AA2r 2  85 rr            sta dp+1
004AA4r 2               
004AA4r 2  60               rts
004AA5r 2               
004AA5r 2               
004AA5r 2               dp_to_current:
004AA5r 2               ; """Look up which wordlist is current and update its pointer
004AA5r 2               ; with the value in dp. Uses A and Y.
004AA5r 2               ; """
004AA5r 2                   ; Determine which wordlist is current
004AA5r 2  A0 04            ldy #current_offset
004AA7r 2  B1 rr            lda (up),y      ; current is a byte variable
004AA9r 2  0A               asl             ; turn it into an offset (in cells)
004AAAr 2               
004AAAr 2                   ; Get the dictionary pointer for that wordlist.
004AAAr 2  18               clc
004AABr 2  69 06            adc #wordlists_offset   ; add offset to wordlists base.
004AADr 2  A8               tay
004AAEr 2  A5 rr            lda dp
004AB0r 2  91 rr            sta (up),y              ; get the dp for that wordlist.
004AB2r 2  C8               iny
004AB3r 2  A5 rr            lda dp+1
004AB5r 2  91 rr            sta (up),y
004AB7r 2               
004AB7r 2  60               rts
004AB8r 2               
004AB8r 2               interpret:
004AB8r 2               .scope
004AB8r 2               ; """Core routine for the interpreter called by EVALUATE and QUIT.
004AB8r 2               ; Process one line only. Assumes that the address of name is in
004AB8r 2               ; cib and the length of the whole input line string is in ciblen
004AB8r 2               ; """
004AB8r 2                   ; Normally we would use PARSE here with the SPACE character as
004AB8r 2                   ; a parameter (PARSE replaces WORD in modern Forths). However,
004AB8r 2                   ; Gforth's PARSE-NAME makes more sense as it uses spaces as
004AB8r 2                   ; delimiters per default and skips any leading spaces, which
004AB8r 2                   ; PARSE doesn't
004AB8r 2               _loop:
004AB8r 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_parse_name       ; ( "string" -- addr u )
004ABBr 2               
004ABBr 2                   ; If PARSE-NAME returns 0 (empty line), no characters were left
004ABBr 2                   ; in the line and we need to go get a new line
004ABBr 2  B5 00            lda 0,x
004ABDr 2  15 01            ora 1,x
004ABFr 2  F0 70            beq _line_done
004AC1r 2               
004AC1r 2                   ; Go to FIND-NAME to see if this is a word we know. We have to
004AC1r 2                   ; make a copy of the address in case it isn't a word we know and
004AC1r 2                   ; we have to go see if it is a number
004AC1r 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_two_dup          ; ( addr u -- addr u addr u )
004AC4r 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_find_name        ; ( addr u addr u -- addr u nt|0 )
004AC7r 2               
004AC7r 2                   ; A zero signals that we didn't find a word in the Dictionary
004AC7r 2  B5 00            lda 0,x
004AC9r 2  15 01            ora 1,x
004ACBr 2  D0 28            bne _got_name_token
004ACDr 2               
004ACDr 2                   ; We didn't get any nt we know of, so let's see if this is
004ACDr 2                   ; a number.
004ACDr 2  E8               inx                     ; ( addr u 0 -- addr u )
004ACEr 2  E8               inx
004ACFr 2               
004ACFr 2                   ; If the number conversion doesn't work, NUMBER will do the
004ACFr 2                   ; complaining for us
004ACFr 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_number           ; ( addr u -- u|d )
004AD2r 2               
004AD2r 2                   ; Otherweise, if we're interpreting, we're done
004AD2r 2  A5 rr            lda state
004AD4r 2  F0 E2            beq _loop
004AD6r 2               
004AD6r 2                   ; We're compiling, so there is a bit more work.  Check
004AD6r 2                   ; status bit 5 to see if it's a single or double-cell
004AD6r 2                   ; number.
004AD6r 2  A9 20            lda #$20
004AD8r 2  24 rr            bit status
004ADAr 2  F0 0D            beq _single_number
004ADCr 2               
004ADCr 2                   ; It's a double cell number.  If we swap the
004ADCr 2                   ; upper and lower half, we can use the literal_runtime twice
004ADCr 2                   ; to compile it into the dictionary.
004ADCr 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_swap
004ADFr 2  A0 rr            ldy #>literal_runtime
004AE1r 2  A9 rr            lda #<literal_runtime
004AE3r 2  20 rr rr         jsr cmpl_subroutine
004AE6r 2               
004AE6r 2                   ; compile our number
004AE6r 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_comma
004AE9r 2               
004AE9r 2                   ; Fall into _single_number to process the other half.
004AE9r 2               _single_number:
004AE9r 2  A0 rr            ldy #>literal_runtime
004AEBr 2  A9 rr            lda #<literal_runtime
004AEDr 2  20 rr rr         jsr cmpl_subroutine
004AF0r 2               
004AF0r 2                   ; compile our number
004AF0r 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_comma
004AF3r 2               
004AF3r 2                   ; That was so much fun, let's do it again!
004AF3r 2  80 C3            bra _loop
004AF5r 2               
004AF5r 2               _got_name_token:
004AF5r 2                   ; We have a known word's nt TOS. We're going to need its xt
004AF5r 2                   ; though, which is four bytes father down.
004AF5r 2               
004AF5r 2                   ; We arrive here with ( addr u nt ), so we NIP twice
004AF5r 2  B5 00            lda 0,x
004AF7r 2  95 04            sta 4,x
004AF9r 2  B5 01            lda 1,x
004AFBr 2  95 05            sta 5,x
004AFDr 2               
004AFDr 2  E8               inx
004AFEr 2  E8               inx
004AFFr 2  E8               inx
004B00r 2  E8               inx                     ; ( nt )
004B01r 2               
004B01r 2                   ; Save a version of nt for error handling and compilation stuff
004B01r 2  B5 00            lda 0,x
004B03r 2  85 rr            sta tmpbranch
004B05r 2  B5 01            lda 1,x
004B07r 2  85 rr            sta tmpbranch+1
004B09r 2               
004B09r 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_name_to_int      ; ( nt - xt )
004B0Cr 2               
004B0Cr 2                   ; See if we are in interpret or compile mode, 0 is interpret
004B0Cr 2  A5 rr            lda state
004B0Er 2  D0 13            bne _compile
004B10r 2               
004B10r 2                   ; We are interpreting, so EXECUTE the xt that is TOS. First,
004B10r 2                   ; though, see if this isn't a compile-only word, which would be
004B10r 2                   ; illegal. The status byte is the second one of the header.
004B10r 2  A0 01            ldy #1
004B12r 2  B1 rr            lda (tmpbranch),y
004B14r 2  29 01            and #CO                 ; mask everything but Compile Only bit
004B16r 2  F0 05            beq _interpret
004B18r 2               
004B18r 2  A9 02            lda #err_compileonly
004B1Ar 2  4C rr rr         jmp error
004B1Dr 2               
004B1Dr 2               _interpret:
004B1Dr 2                   ; We JSR to EXECUTE instead of calling the xt directly because
004B1Dr 2                   ; the RTS of the word we're executing will bring us back here,
004B1Dr 2                   ; skipping EXECUTE completely during RTS. If we were to execute
004B1Dr 2                   ; xt directly, we have to fool around with the Return Stack
004B1Dr 2                   ; instead, which is actually slightly slower
004B1Dr 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_execute
004B20r 2               
004B20r 2                   ; That's quite enough for this word, let's get the next one
004B20r 2  4C rr rr         jmp _loop
004B23r 2               
004B23r 2               _compile:
004B23r 2                   ; We're compiling! However, we need to see if this is an
004B23r 2                   ; IMMEDIATE word, which would mean we execute it right now even
004B23r 2                   ; during compilation mode. Fortunately, we saved the nt so life
004B23r 2                   ; is easier. The flags are in the second byte of the header
004B23r 2  A0 01            ldy #1
004B25r 2  B1 rr            lda (tmpbranch),y
004B27r 2  29 04            and #IM                 ; Mask all but IM bit
004B29r 2  D0 F2            bne _interpret          ; IMMEDIATE word, execute right now
004B2Br 2               
004B2Br 2                   ; Compile the xt into the Dictionary with COMPILE,
004B2Br 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_compile_comma
004B2Er 2  4C rr rr         jmp _loop
004B31r 2               
004B31r 2               _line_done:
004B31r 2                   ; drop stuff from PARSE_NAME
004B31r 2  E8               inx
004B32r 2  E8               inx
004B33r 2  E8               inx
004B34r 2  E8               inx
004B35r 2               
004B35r 2  60               rts
004B36r 2               .endscope
004B36r 2               
004B36r 2               
004B36r 2               is_printable:
004B36r 2               .scope
004B36r 2               ; """Given a character in A, check if it is a printable ASCII
004B36r 2               ; character in the range from $20 to $7E inclusive. Returns the
004B36r 2               ; result in the Carry Flag: 0 (clear) is not printable, 1 (set)
004B36r 2               ; is printable. Keeps A. See
004B36r 2               ; http://www.obelisk.me.uk/6502/algorithms.html for a
004B36r 2               ; discussion of various ways to do this
004B36r 2  C9 20            cmp #AscSP              ; $20
004B38r 2  90 08            bcc _done
004B3Ar 2  C9 7F            cmp #'~' + 1             ; $7E
004B3Cr 2  B0 03            bcs _failed
004B3Er 2               
004B3Er 2  38               sec
004B3Fr 2  80 01            bra _done
004B41r 2               _failed:
004B41r 2  18               clc
004B42r 2               _done:
004B42r 2  60               rts
004B43r 2               .endscope
004B43r 2               
004B43r 2               
004B43r 2               is_whitespace:
004B43r 2               .scope
004B43r 2               ; """Given a character in A, check if it is a whitespace
004B43r 2               ; character, that is, an ASCII value from 0 to 32 (where
004B43r 2               ; 32 is SPACE). Returns the result in the Carry Flag:
004B43r 2               ; 0 (clear) is no, it isn't whitespace, while 1 (set) means
004B43r 2               ; that it is whitespace. See PARSE and PARSE-NAME for
004B43r 2               ; a discussion of the uses. Does not change A or Y.
004B43r 2  C9 00            cmp #00         ; explicit comparison to leave Y untouched
004B45r 2  90 08            bcc _done
004B47r 2               
004B47r 2  C9 21            cmp #AscSP+1
004B49r 2  B0 03            bcs _failed
004B4Br 2               
004B4Br 2  38               sec
004B4Cr 2  80 01            bra _done
004B4Er 2               _failed:
004B4Er 2  18               clc
004B4Fr 2               _done:
004B4Fr 2  60               rts
004B50r 2               .endscope
004B50r 2               
004B50r 2               
004B50r 2               ; Underflow tests. We jump to the label with the number of cells (not: bytes)
004B50r 2               ; required for the word. This routine flows into the generic error handling
004B50r 2               ; code
004B50r 2               underflow_1:
004B50r 2               ; """Make sure we have at least one cell on the Data Stack"""
004B50r 2  E0 rr            cpx #dsp0-1
004B52r 2  10 10            bpl underflow_error
004B54r 2  60               rts
004B55r 2               underflow_2:
004B55r 2               ; """Make sure we have at least two cells on the Data Stack"""
004B55r 2  E0 rr            cpx #dsp0-3
004B57r 2  10 0B            bpl underflow_error
004B59r 2  60               rts
004B5Ar 2               underflow_3:
004B5Ar 2               ; """Make sure we have at least three cells on the Data Stack"""
004B5Ar 2  E0 rr            cpx #dsp0-5
004B5Cr 2  10 06            bpl underflow_error
004B5Er 2  60               rts
004B5Fr 2               underflow_4:
004B5Fr 2               ; """Make sure we have at least four cells on the Data Stack"""
004B5Fr 2  E0 rr            cpx #dsp0-7
004B61r 2  10 01            bpl underflow_error
004B63r 2  60               rts
004B64r 2               
004B64r 2               underflow_error:
004B64r 2                   ; Entry for COLD/ABORT/QUIT
004B64r 2  A9 09            lda #err_underflow      ; fall through to error
004B66r 2               
004B66r 2               error:
004B66r 2               ; """Given the error number in a, print the associated error string and
004B66r 2               ; call abort. Uses tmp3.
004B66r 2               ; """
004B66r 2  0A               asl
004B67r 2  A8               tay
004B68r 2  B9 rr rr         lda error_table,y
004B6Br 2  85 rr            sta tmp3                ; LSB
004B6Dr 2  C8               iny
004B6Er 2  B9 rr rr         lda error_table,y
004B71r 2  85 rr            sta tmp3+1              ; MSB
004B73r 2               
004B73r 2  20 rr rr         jsr print_common
004B76r 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_cr
004B79r 2  4C rr rr         jmp xt_abort            ; no jsr, as we clobber return stack
004B7Cr 2               
004B7Cr 2               
004B7Cr 2               ; =====================================================================
004B7Cr 2               ; PRINTING ROUTINES
004B7Cr 2               
004B7Cr 2               ; We distinguish two types of print calls, both of which take the string number
004B7Cr 2               ; (see strings.asm) in A:
004B7Cr 2               
004B7Cr 2               ;       print_string       - with a line feed
004B7Cr 2               ;       print_string_no_lf - without a line feed
004B7Cr 2               
004B7Cr 2               ; In addition, print_common provides a lower-level alternative for error
004B7Cr 2               ; handling and anything else that provides the address of the
004B7Cr 2               ; zero-terminated string directly in tmp3. All of those routines assume that
004B7Cr 2               ; printing should be more concerned with size than speed, because anything to
004B7Cr 2               ; do with humans reading text is going to be slow.
004B7Cr 2               
004B7Cr 2               print_string_no_lf:
004B7Cr 2               ; """Given the number of a zero-terminated string in A, print it to the
004B7Cr 2               ; current output without adding a LF. Uses Y and tmp3 by falling
004B7Cr 2               ; through to print_common
004B7Cr 2               ; """
004B7Cr 2                   ; Get the entry from the string table
004B7Cr 2  0A               asl
004B7Dr 2  A8               tay
004B7Er 2  B9 rr rr         lda string_table,y
004B81r 2  85 rr            sta tmp3                ; LSB
004B83r 2  C8               iny
004B84r 2  B9 rr rr         lda string_table,y
004B87r 2  85 rr            sta tmp3+1              ; MSB
004B89r 2               
004B89r 2                   ; fall through to print_common
004B89r 2               print_common:
004B89r 2               ; """Common print routine used by both the print functions and
004B89r 2               ; the error printing routine. Assumes string address is in tmp3. Uses
004B89r 2               ; Y.
004B89r 2               ; """
004B89r 2               .scope
004B89r 2  A0 00            ldy #0
004B8Br 2               _loop:
004B8Br 2  B1 rr            lda (tmp3),y
004B8Dr 2  F0 06            beq _done               ; strings are zero-terminated
004B8Fr 2               
004B8Fr 2  20 rr rr         jsr emit_a              ; allows vectoring via output
004B92r 2  C8               iny
004B93r 2  80 F6            bra _loop
004B95r 2               _done:
004B95r 2  60               rts
004B96r 2               .endscope
004B96r 2               
004B96r 2               print_string:
004B96r 2               ; """Print a zero-terminated string to the console/screen, adding a LF.
004B96r 2               ; We do not check to see if the index is out of range. Uses tmp3.
004B96r 2               ; """
004B96r 2  20 rr rr         jsr print_string_no_lf
004B99r 2  4C rr rr         jmp xt_cr               ; JSR/RTS because never compiled
004B9Cr 2               
004B9Cr 2               
004B9Cr 2               print_u:
004B9Cr 2               ; """basic printing routine used by higher-level constructs,
004B9Cr 2               ; the equivalent of the forth word  0 <# #s #> type  which is
004B9Cr 2               ; basically u. without the space at the end. used for various
004B9Cr 2               ; outputs
004B9Cr 2               ; """
004B9Cr 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_zero                     ; 0
004B9Fr 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_less_number_sign         ; <#
004BA2r 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_number_sign_s            ; #S
004BA5r 2  20 rr rr         jsr xt_number_sign_greater      ; #>
004BA8r 2  4C rr rr         jmp xt_type                     ; JSR/RTS because never compiled
004BABr 2               
004BABr 2               ; END
004BABr 2               
004BABr 1               ; .include "../../ed.s"
004BABr 1               
004BABr 1               
004BABr 1               .segment "DATA"
004BABr 1               
004BABr 1               platform_bye:
004BABr 1               kernel_init:
004BABr 1               v_nmi:
004BABr 1  A9 FF            lda #$FF
004BADr 1  8D 82 FF         sta DDRB
004BB0r 1  8D 83 FF         sta DDRA
004BB3r 1  9C 81 FF         stz PORTA
004BB6r 1  9C 80 FF         stz PORTB
004BB9r 1               .ifdef video_init
004BB9r 1                   jsr video_init
004BB9r 1               .endif
004BB9r 1               .ifdef ps2_init
004BB9r 1  20 rr rr         jsr ps2_init
004BBCr 1               .endif
004BBCr 1               
004BBCr 1               .ifdef timer_init
004BBCr 1  20 rr rr         jsr timer_init
004BBFr 1               .endif
004BBFr 1  20 rr rr         jsr acia_init
004BC2r 1               .ifdef lcd_init
004BC2r 1                   jsr lcd_init
004BC2r 1               .endif
004BC2r 1               .ifdef spi_init
004BC2r 1                   jsr spi_init
004BC2r 1               .endif
004BC2r 1               .ifdef kb_init
004BC2r 1                   jsr kb_init
004BC2r 1               .endif
004BC2r 1               
004BC2r 1               
004BC2r 1  DA A2 00 BD      printascii welcome_message
004BC6r 1  rr rr F0 06  
004BCAr 1  20 rr rr E8  
004BD1r 1               
004BD1r 1               
004BD1r 1  4C rr rr         jmp forth
004BD4r 1               
004BD4r 1               
004BD4r 1               kernel_putc:
004BD4r 1                   ; """Print a single character to the console. """
004BD4r 1                   ;; Send_Char - send character in A out serial port.
004BD4r 1                   ;; Uses: A (original value restored)
004BD4r 1               send_char:
004BD4r 1  48               pha
004BD5r 1                   .ifdef char_out
004BD5r 1                   jsr char_out
004BD5r 1                   .endif
004BD5r 1                   .ifdef acia_out
004BD5r 1  20 rr rr         jsr acia_out
004BD8r 1                   .endif
004BD8r 1               send_char_exit:
004BD8r 1               .ifdef lcd_print
004BD8r 1                   jsr lcd_print
004BD8r 1               .endif
004BD8r 1  68               pla
004BD9r 1  60               rts
004BDAr 1               
004BDAr 1               
004BDAr 1                       ;; Get_Char - get a character from the serial port into A.
004BDAr 1                       ;; Set the carry flag if char is valid.
004BDAr 1                       ;; Return immediately with carry flag clear if no char available.
004BDAr 1                       ;; Uses: A (return value)
004BDAr 1               
004BDAr 1               Get_Char:
004BDAr 1  20 rr rr         jsr acia_getc
004BDDr 1  90 05            bcc get_ps2_char                ; check keyboard buffer if nothing from ACIA
004BDFr 1  20 rr rr         jsr check_ctrl_c
004BE2r 1  38               sec                             ; Set Carry to show we got a character
004BE3r 1  60               rts                             ; Return
004BE4r 1               
004BE4r 1               get_ps2_char:                       ; no ACIA char available, try to get from KB buffer
004BE4r 1               .ifdef ps2_get_char
004BE4r 1  20 rr rr         jsr ps2_get_char
004BE7r 1               .endif
004BE7r 1  90 02            bcc get_kb_char
004BE9r 1  38               sec
004BEAr 1               
004BEAr 1  60               rts
004BEBr 1               get_kb_char:
004BEBr 1                   .ifdef kb_get_char
004BEBr 1               
004BEBr 1                   ; ldy #5
004BEBr 1                   ; jsr delay_short
004BEBr 1                   ; ply
004BEBr 1                       jsr kb_get_char
004BEBr 1               
004BEBr 1                   .endif
004BEBr 1               exit:                         ; Indicate no char available.
004BEBr 1  60               rts                             ; return
004BECr 1               
004BECr 1               kernel_getc:
004BECr 1                   ; """Get a single character from the keyboard (waits for key).
004BECr 1                   ; """
004BECr 1                   ;; Get_Char_Wait - same as Get_Char only blocking.
004BECr 1                   ;; Uses: A (return value)
004BECr 1               Get_Char_Wait:
004BECr 1  20 rr rr         jsr Get_Char
004BEFr 1  90 FB            bcc Get_Char_Wait
004BF1r 1  60               rts
004BF2r 1               
004BF2r 1               check_ctrl_c:
004BF2r 1                   ;; Check if we have ctrl-C character, if so jump to nmi
004BF2r 1  C9 03            cmp #$03
004BF4r 1  D0 12            bne exit_ctrl_c
004BF6r 1  DA A2 00 BD      printascii abort_message
004BFAr 1  rr rr F0 06  
004BFEr 1  20 rr rr E8  
004C05r 1  4C rr rr         jmp xt_abort
004C08r 1               
004C08r 1               exit_ctrl_c:
004C08r 1  60               rts
004C09r 1               
004C09r 1               
004C09r 1               v_irq:                          ; IRQ handler
004C09r 1  48                   pha
004C0Ar 1  5A                   phy
004C0Br 1                       ; lda #'.'
004C0Br 1                       ; jsr kernel_putc
004C0Br 1                       ; check if bit 7 of IFR is set
004C0Br 1  AD 8D FF             lda IFR
004C0Er 1  10 0B                bpl v_kb_irq  ; Interrupt not from VIA, exit
004C10r 1               
004C10r 1  29 08                and #$08        ; ps2 has priority
004C12r 1  D0 12                bne v_irq_ps2
004C14r 1  AD 8D FF             lda IFR
004C17r 1  29 40                and #$40
004C19r 1  D0 20                bne v_irq_timer
004C1Br 1               v_kb_irq:
004C1Br 1  AD 9D FF             lda KB_IFR
004C1Er 1  10 26                bpl v_irq_exit
004C20r 1  29 40                and #$40
004C22r 1  D0 22                bne v_kb_irq_timer
004C24r 1  80 20                bra v_irq_exit
004C26r 1               
004C26r 1               
004C26r 1               v_irq_ps2:
004C26r 1                   .ifdef ps2_irq
004C26r 1  A5 rr                lda time
004C28r 1  85 rr                sta last_ps2_time
004C2Ar 1  A5 rr                lda time+1
004C2Cr 1  85 rr                sta last_ps2_time+1
004C2Er 1  A5 rr                lda time+2
004C30r 1  85 rr                sta last_ps2_time+2
004C32r 1  A5 rr                lda time+3
004C34r 1  85 rr                sta last_ps2_time+3
004C36r 1                       ; this delay is here to ensure we prevent desynchronization
004C36r 1                       ;ldy #$04         ; correct delay seems to be #$20 at 10Mhz
004C36r 1                       ; jsr delay_short
004C36r 1               
004C36r 1               
004C36r 1  20 rr rr             jsr ps2_irq
004C39r 1               
004C39r 1                       ; ldy #$04         ; correct delay seems to be #$20 at 10Mhz
004C39r 1                       ; jsr delay_short
004C39r 1                   .endif
004C39r 1  80 0B                bra v_irq_exit
004C3Br 1               
004C3Br 1               v_irq_timer:
004C3Br 1  AD 84 FF             lda T1CL
004C3Er 1                       ; clear timer interrupt
004C3Er 1                   .ifdef timer_irq
004C3Er 1  20 rr rr             jsr timer_irq
004C41r 1                   .endif
004C41r 1  20 rr rr             jsr Get_Char ; Check if a char is waiting to be able to break on CTRL-C
004C44r 1                       ; check if there is a char waiting to be printed to the lcd
004C44r 1                       ; lda lcd_char
004C44r 1                       ; beq v_exit
004C44r 1                       ; jsr lcd_print
004C44r 1                       ; stz lcd_char
004C44r 1               
004C44r 1               
004C44r 1  80 00                bra v_irq_exit
004C46r 1               v_kb_irq_timer:
004C46r 1               .ifdef kb_time
004C46r 1                   lda KB_T1CL ; clear timer interrupt
004C46r 1                   inc kb_time
004C46r 1                   bne v_irq_exit
004C46r 1               .endif
004C46r 1                   ;jsr kb_scan
004C46r 1               v_irq_exit:
004C46r 1  7A               ply
004C47r 1  68               pla
004C48r 1  40               rti
004C49r 1               
004C49r 1               
004C49r 1               
004C49r 1               .segment "RODATA"
0000FFr 1               
0000FFr 1  57 65 6C 63  welcome_message: .byte "Welcome to Planck 6502", $0D, "Type 'words' for available words", 0
000103r 1  6F 6D 65 20  
000107r 1  74 6F 20 50  
000137r 1  0D 0A 00     abort_message: .byte AscCR, AscLF, 0
00013Ar 1

000004r 1  rr rr        .word v_irq
